ĀTV_1.1–1.4–10.7–10.14	svāmyam yasya nijam jagatsu janiteṣu ādau tatas pālanaṃ vyutpatteḥ karaṇam hita āhita vidhi vyāsedha sambhāvanam bhūta uktiḥ sahajā kṛpā nirupadhiḥ yatnaḥ tad artha ātmakaḥ tasmai pūrva guru uttamāya jagatām īśāya pitre namaḥ iha khalu nisarga pratikūla svabhāvam sarva jana saṃvedana siddham duḥkham jihāsavaḥ sarve eva tad dhāna upāyam avidvāṃsaḥ anusarantaḥ ca sarva adhyātma vid eka vākya tayā tattva jñānam eva tad upāyam ākarṇayanti na tatas anyam pratiyogi anuyogi tayā ca ātmā eva tattvataḥ jñeyaḥ tathā hi yadi nairātmyam yadi vā ātmā asti vastu bhūtaḥ ubhayathā api naisargikam ātma jñānam atattva jñānam eva iti atra api eka vākyatā eva vādinām atas ātma tattvam vivicyate 
ĀTV_20.7–22.18–34.1–34.6	 tatra bādhakam bhavat kṣaṇa bhaṅgaḥ vā bāhya artha bhaṅgaḥ vā guṇa guṇi bheda bhaṅgaḥ vā anupalambhaḥ vā iti tatra na prathamaḥ pramāṇa abhāvāt yat sat tat kṣaṇikam yathā ghaṭaḥ san ca vivāda adhyāsitaḥ śabda ādiḥ iti ced na pratibandha asiddheḥ sāmarthya asāmarthya lakṣaṇa viruddha dharma saṃsargeṇa bheda siddhau tad siddhiḥ iti ced na viruddha dharma saṃsarga asiddheḥ prasaṅga viparyayābhyām tad siddhiḥ iti ced na sāmarthyam hi karaṇa tvam vā yogya tā vā na ādyaḥ sādhya aviśiṣṭa tva prasaṅgāt vyāvṛtti bhedāt ayam adoṣaḥ iti ced na tad anupapatteḥ vyāvartya bhedena virodhaḥ hi tad mūlam 
ĀTV_39.1–39.3–43.10–43.11	 sa ca na tāvat mithas vyāvartya pratikṣepāt go tva aśva tva vat tathā sati virodhāt anyatara apāye bādhā siddhyoḥ anyatara prasaṅgāt na api tad ākṣepa pratikṣepābhyām vṛkṣa tva śiṃśapātva vat para apara bhāva anabhyupagamāt abhyupagame vā samarthyasya api akaraṇam asamarthyasya api vā karaṇam prasajyeta na api upādhi bhedāt kāryatva anitya tva vat tad abhāvāt ca śabda mātram upādhiḥ paryāya śabda uccheda prasaṅgāt 
ĀTV_45.3–45.6–49.9–49.10	 na api vikalpa bhedaḥ svarūpa kṛtasya tasya vyāvṛtti bhedaka tve asamartha vyāvṛtteḥ api bheda prasaṅgāt viṣaya kṛtasya tu tasya bhedaka tve anyonya āśraya prasaṅgāt na ca nirnimittaḥ eva ayam vyāvṛtti bheda vyavahāraḥ ati prasaṅgāt na api dvitīyaḥ sā hi sahakāri sākalyam vā prātisvikī vā na tāvat ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ siddha sādhanāt para anabhyupagamena hetu asiddheḥ ca yat sahakāri samavadhāna vat tat dhi karoti eva iti kaḥ nāma na abhyupaiti yam uddiśya sādhyate na ca akaraṇa kāle sahakāri samavadhāna vat tvam asmābhiḥ abhyupeyate yatas prasaṅgaḥ pravarteta prātisvikī tu yogyatā anvaya vyatireka viṣayībhūtam bīja tvam vā syāt tat avāntara jāti bhedaḥ vā sahakāri vaikalya prayukta kārya abhāvavat tvam vā na tāvat ādyaḥ akurvataḥ api bīja jātīyasya pratyakṣa siddha tvāt tava api tatra avipratipatteḥ 
ĀTV_50.4–50.18	 na dvitīyaḥ tasya kurvataḥ api mayā anabhyupagamena dṛṣṭāntasya sādhana vikala tvāt kaḥ hi nāma sustha ātmā pramāṇa śūnyam abhyupagacchet sa hi na tāvat pratyakṣeṇa anubhūyate tathā anavasāyāt na api anumānena liṅga abhāvāt yadi na kaḥ cit viśeṣaḥ katham tarhi karaṇa akaraṇe iti ced kaḥ evam āha na iti param kim jāti bheda rūpaḥ sahakāri lābha alābha rūpaḥ vā iti niyāmakam pramāṇam anusarantaḥ na paśyāmaḥ tathā api yaḥ ayam sahakāri madhyam adhyāsīnaḥ akṣepa karaṇa svabhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ sa yadi prāk api āsīt tadā prasahya kāryam kurvāṇaḥ gīrvāṇa śāpa śatena api apahastayitum na śakyate iti ced yuktam etat yadi akṣepa karaṇa svabhāva tvam bhāvasya pramāṇa gocaraḥ syāt tat eva kutas siddham iti na adhigacchāmaḥ prasaṅga tad viparyayābhyām iti ced na paraspara āśraya prasaṅgāt evaṃsvabhāva tva siddhau hi tayoḥ pravṛttiḥ tad pravṛttau ca evaṃsvabhāva tva siddhiḥ iti 
ĀTV_54.16–55.3	 syāt etat kārya janma eva asmin arthe pramāṇam vilamba kāri svabhāva anuvṛttau kārya anupattiḥ sarvadā iti ced na vilamba kāri svabhāvasya sarva daiva akaraṇe tattva vyāghātāt tatas ca vilamba kārī iti asya yāvat saha kārya sannidhānam tāvat na karoti iti arthaḥ evam ca kārya janma sāmagryām pramāṇayitum śakyate na tu jāti bhede te tu kim yathā anubhavam vilamba kāri svabhāvāḥ parasparam pratyāsannāḥ kāryam kṛtavantaḥ kim vā yathā tu at parikalpanam kṣiprakāri svabhāvāḥ iti atra kārya jananam ajāgarūkam eva iti 
ĀTV_57.3–57.7–58.17–59.5	 na api tṛtīyaḥ virodhāt saha kārya bhāva prayukta kārya abhāvavān ca sahakāri virahe kāryavān ca iti vyāhatam tasmāt yat yad abhāve eva yat na karoti tat tad sadbhāve tat karoti eva iti tu syāt etat ca sthairya siddheḥ eva param bījam sarva svam iti etena samartha vyavahāra gocara tvam hetuḥ iti nirastam tādṛś vyavahāra gocarasya api bījasya aṅkura akaraṇa darśanāt na asau mukhaḥ tad vyavahāraḥ tasya janana nimittaka tvāt anyathā tu aniyama prasaṅgāt iti ced kīdṛśam punar jananam mukha samartha vyavahāra nimittam na tāvat akṣepa karaṇam tasya asiddheḥ niyamasya ca sahakāri sākalye sati eva karaṇam karaṇam eva iti evaṃsvabhāva tvena api upapatteḥ tatas ca janana nimittaḥ eva ayam vyavahāraḥ na vyāpti siddhiḥ iti 
ĀTV_62.17–63.2–64.11–64.18	 syāt etat etāvatā api bhāvasya kaḥ svabhāvaḥ samarthitaḥ bhavati na hi kṣepa ākṣepābhyām anyaḥ prakāraḥ asti iti ced na dūṣaṇa abhidhāna samaye niścaya abhāvena eva sandigdhā siddhi nirvāhe kathā pūrvarūpa paryavasānāt uttara pakṣa avasare tu saḥ api na durvacaḥ tathā hi karaṇam pratyavilambaḥ iti kaḥ arthaḥ kim utpatteḥ anantaram eva karaṇam sahakāri samavadhāna anantaram eva vā vilambaḥ iti api kaḥ arthaḥ kim yāvat na sahakāri samavadhānam tāvat akaraṇam sarvathā eva akaraṇam iti vā tatra prathama caturthayoḥ pramāṇa abhāvāt aniścaye api dvitīya tṛtīyayoḥ pratyakṣam eva pramāṇam bīja jātīyasya hi sahakāri samavadhāna anantaram eva karaṇam karaṇam eva iti pratyakṣa siddham eva tathā sahakāri samavadhāna rahitasya akaraṇam iti api 
ĀTV_66.3–66.11–68.3–68.5	 atra ca bhāvana api na vipratipadyate eva pramāṇa siddha tvāt viparyaye bādhakāt ca tathā hi yadi sahakāri virahe akurvāṇaḥ tad samavadhāne api na kuryāt tad jātīyam akaraṇam eva syāt samavadhāna asam avadhānayoḥ ubhayoḥ api akaraṇāt evam tad samavadhāna virahe api yadi kuryāt sahakāriṇaḥ na kāraṇam syuḥ tān antareṇa api karaṇāt tathā ca ananyathā siddha anvaya vyatirekavatām api akāraṇa tve kāryasya akasmika tva prasaṅgaḥ tathā ca kādācid ka tva vihatiḥ iti evam ca dvitīya pakṣa vivakṣāyām akṣepa kāri tvam eva bhāvasya svabhāvaḥ tṛtīya pakṣa vivakṣāyām tu kṣepa kāri tvam eva bhāvasya svarūpam iti na ubhaya prakāra nivṛttiḥ iti 
ĀTV_68.13–69.5	 tathā api kim asamarthasya eva sahakāri virahaḥ sva rūpa lābha anantaram kartuḥ eva vā sahakāri samavadhānam anyathā vā iti kim niyāmakam iti ced idam ucyate kuśūla stha bījasya aṅkura anukūlaḥ śilā śakalāt kaścid asti viśeṣaḥ vā na ced nityam ena ekatra pravṛttiḥ anyasmāt nivṛttiḥ ca tad arthinaḥ na syāt paramparayā aṅkura prasava samartha bīja kṣaṇa jananāt asti eva iti ced kadā punar paramparayā api tathābhūtam kariṣyati iti tatra sandehaḥ iti ced sa punar kim ākāraḥ kim sahakāriṣu samavahiteṣu api kariṣyati na vā iti uta asamavahiteṣu api teṣu kariṣyati na vā iti 
ĀTV_71.20–72.7	 atha yadā sahakāri samavadhānam tadā eva kariṣyati eva param kadā teṣām samavadhānam iti sandehaḥ na syāt pūrvaḥ sāmānyatas kāraṇatva avadhāraṇe tasya anavakāśāt avakāśe vā kāraṇa tva anavadhāraṇāt na api dvitīyaḥ sahakāriṇām tattva avadhāraṇe tasya anavakāśāt avakāśe vā teṣām tattva anavadhāraṇāt tṛtīye tu sarve eva tad santāna antaḥpātinaḥ bīja kṣaṇāḥ samāna śīlāḥ prāpnuvanti yatra tatra sahakāri samavadhāne sati karaṇa niyamāt sarvatra ca sahakāri samavadhāna sambhavāt 
ĀTV_73.10–73.15–74.7–74.11	 samarthaḥ eva kṣaṇe kṣiti ādi samavadhānam iti ced tat kim asamarthe sahakāri samavadhānam eva na asti samavadhāne sati api vā tasmāt na kārya janma na ādyaḥ śilā śakala ādau api kṣiti salila tejaḥ pavana yoga darśanāt na dvitīyaḥ śilā śakalāt iva kadācid sahakāri sākalyavataḥ api bījāt aṅkura anutpatti prasaṅgāt evam api syāt kaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced na tāvat idam upalabdam āśaṅkyate iti ced na tad samavadhāne sati api akaraṇa vat tad virahe karaṇam api āśaṅkyeta āśaṅkyatām iti ced tarhi bīja virahe api āśaṅkyeta tathā ca sati sādhyaḥ pratyakṣa anupalambha pariśuddhiḥ 
ĀTV_75.11–75.16–77.8–77.13	 syāt etat na bīja ādīnām paraspara samavadhānavatām eva kārya karaṇam aṅgīkṛtya āśaṅkyate yena samavadhāna niyamāt sarveṣām eva tad jātīyānām eka rasa tā niścayaḥ syāt na api yatra tatra samartha utpattim aṅgīkṛtya yena vikalebhyaḥ api kadācid kārya janma sambhāvanāyām pratyakṣa anupalambha virodhaḥ syāt kid nāma bīja ādiṣu samavahiteṣu avāntara jāti viśeṣam āśritya api kārya janma sambhāvyate iti na dṛṣṭa samavadhāna mātreṇa eva upapattau tad kalyanāyām pramāṇa abhāvāt kalpanā gaurava prasaṅga pratihata tvāt atīndriya indriya ādi vilopa prasaṅgāt vikalpa anupapatteḥ viśeṣasya viśeṣam prati prayojaka tvāt ca iti 
ĀTV_81.4–81.10	 tathā hi utpatteḥ ārabhya mudgara prahāra paryantam ghaṭaḥ tāvat jāti antarān ākrānta eva anubhūyamānaḥ krama vat sahakāri vaicitryāt kārya koṭaiḥ sarūpāḥ virūpāḥ karoti tatra etāvatā eva sarvasmin samañjase anupalabhyamāna jāti koṭi kalpanā kena pramāṇena kena vā upayogena yena kalpanā gaurava prasaṅga doṣaḥ na syāt yaḥ yad arthaḥ kalpyate tasya anyathā siddhiḥ eva tasya abhāvaḥ iti bhavān eva āha iti 
ĀTV_82.14–82.17–84.1–84.6	 dṛṣṭam ca jāti bhedam tiraskṛtya svabhāva bheda kalpanayā eva kārya utpattau sahakāriṇaḥ api dṛṣṭa tvāt kathañcid svīkriyante atīndriya indriya ādi kalpanā tu vilīyeta māna abhāvāt vikalpa anupapatteḥ ca sa khalu jāti viśeṣaḥ śāli tva saṃgrāhakaḥ vā syāt tad pratikṣepakaḥ vā ādye kuśūla sthasya api śāleḥ katham na tad rūpa tvam dvitīye tu abhimatasya api śāleḥ katham tat rūpa tvam evam śāli tvam api tasya saṃgrāhakam pratikṣepakam vā ādye aśāleḥ atattva prasaṅgaḥ dvitīye tu śāleḥ eva atattva prasaṅgaḥ 
ĀTV_85.14–85.18–89.6–89.12	 na ca na ubhayam api iti vācyam virodha avirodhayoḥ prakāra antara abhāvāt vyakti bhedena saṅgraha pratikṣepau api na viruddhau iti ced vilīnam idānīm tad atad jātīya tā virodhena paridṛśyamāna katipaya vyakti pratikṣepe api mithas kvacid turaga vihagayoḥ api sambheda sambhavāt yaḥ ca yasya jāti viśeṣaḥ sa ced tam vyabhicaret vyabhicaret api śiṃśapā pādapam aviśeṣāt tathā ca gatam svabhāva hetunā viparyaye bādhakam viśeṣaḥ iti ced na tasya iha api sattvāt tad abhāve svabhāva tva anupapatteḥ upapattau vā kim bādhaka anusaraṇa vyasanena iti viśeṣasya viśeṣam prati prayojaka tvāt ca tathā hi kārya gatam aṅkura tvam prati bīja tu asya aprayojaka tve abījāt api tad utpatti prasaṅgaḥ 
ĀTV_91.19–92.5	 bījasya viśeṣaḥ katham abīje bhaviṣyati iti ced tarhi śāleḥ viśeṣaḥ katham aśālau syāt iti śāleḥ aṅkura anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ aśāli vat abīje api asau bhavatu viśeṣaḥ tathā api bījatvā eka artha samavetaḥ eva asau aṅkuram prati prayojakaḥ iti ced na śāli tva vyabhicāre śāli tvā eka artha samavāya vat bīja tu a vyabhicāre bījatvā eka artha samavāyena api niyantum aśakya tvāt aviśeṣāt 
ĀTV_94.1–94.4–94.14–94.19	 tasmāt yaḥ yathābhūtaḥ yathābhūtam ātmanaḥ anvaya vyatirekau anukārayati tasya tathābhūtasya eva tathābhūte sāmarthyam tad viśeṣāḥ tu kārya viśeṣam prayojayanti śāli ādi vat iti yuktam utpaśyāmaḥ kasya punar pramāṇasya ayam vyāpāra kalāpaḥ iti ced tad utpatti niścaya hetoḥ pratyakṣa anupalambha ātmakasya iti brūmaḥ atha nyāyena vinā na te paritoṣaḥ śṛṇu tam api tadā yat aṅkuram pratyaprayojakam na tat bīja jātīyam yathā śilā śakalam aṅkuram pratyaprayojakam ca kuśūla nihitam bījam abhyupetam paraiḥ iti vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ prasaṅga hetuḥ 
ĀTV_96.14–96.18–98.16–98.18	 viparyaye api kim bādhakam iti ced aṅkurasya jāti pratiniyama āka smika tva prasaṅgaḥ iti uktam bīja tvam tasya pratyakṣa siddham aśakya apahnavam iti ced astu tarhi viparyayaḥ yat bījam tat aṅkuram prati prayojakam yathā antyasāmagrī madhyam adhyāsīnam bījam bījam ca idam vivāda āspadam iti svabhāva hetuḥ aṅkurasya hi jāti pratiniyamaḥ na tāvat nirnimittaḥ sārvatrika tva prasaṅgāt na api anya nimittaḥ tathābhūtasya tasya abhāvāt sā iyam nimitta vat tā vipakṣāt vyāvartamānā sva vyāpyam ādāya bīja prayojaka tāyām eva viśrāmyati iti pratibandha siddhiḥ 
ĀTV_99.15–100.7	 athavā kṛtam aṅkura graheṇa bīja svabhāva tvam kvacid kārye prayojakam na vā na ced na tad svabhāvam bījam tena rūpeṇa kvacid api anupayogāt evam ca pratyakṣa siddham bīja svabhāva tvam na asti sarva pramāṇa agocaraḥ tu viśeṣaḥ asti iti viśudvā buddhiḥ kvacid upayoge api ekasya tena rūpeṇa sarveṣām aviśeṣaḥ tādrūpyāt tathā ca katham kiñcid eva bījam sva kāryam kuryāt na aparāṇi na ca vastu mātram tat kāryam abījāt tad anupatti prasaṅgāt na api bīja mātram aṅkura kāriṇaḥ api tad utpatti prasaṅgāt na api aṅkura ādi anyatama mātram prāk api tad utpatti prasaṅgāt 
ĀTV_103.13–104.2	 yadā yat utpannam sat yat kārya anukūla sahakāri madhyam adhiśete tadā tat eva kāryam prati tasya prayojaka tvam iti ced tat kim avāntara jāti bhedam upādāya bīja svabhāvena eva vā ādye saḥ eva jāti bhedaḥ tatra prayojakaḥ kim āyātam bīja tvasya dvitīye tu samāna śīlānām api saha kāri vaikalyāt akaraṇam iti āyātam tad tad sahakāri sāhitye sati tat tat kāryam prati prayojakasya bīja svabhāvasya sarva sādhāraṇa tvāt iti 
ĀTV_105.5–105.10–106.10–106.14	 atra api prayogaḥ yat yena rūpeṇa artha kriyāsu na upayujyate na tat tad rūpam yathā bījam kuñjara tvena kiñcid api akurvan na kuñjara svarūpam tathā ca śāli ādayaḥ sāmagrī praviṣṭāḥ bīja tvena artha kriyāsu na upayujyante iti vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ prasaṅga hetuḥ tad rūpa tāyāḥ artha kriyām prati yogyatayā vyāpta tvāt anyathā ati prasaṅgāt tad rūpa tvam etasya pratyakṣa siddha tvāt aśakya apahnavam iti ced astu tarhi viparyayaḥ yat yat rūpam tat tena rūpeṇa artha kriyāsu upayujyate yathā svabhāvena sāmagrī niveśinaḥ bhāvāḥ bīja jātīyāśrā ete kuśūla sthādaya iti svabhāva hetuḥ tad rūpa tva mātra anubandhi tvāt yogyatāyāḥ 
ĀTV_107.12–107.18	 tatas ca asti kiñcid kāryam yatra bīja tvena bījam upayujyate iti bīja anubhavaḥ eva asādhāraṇam kāryam yatra bīja tvam prayojakam tat ca sarvasmāt eva bījāt bhavati iti kim anupapannam iti ced na yaugika tad anubhavasya tad antareṇa api upapatteḥ laukikaḥ iti ced na satyam etat na tu idam avaśyam sarvasmāt bījāt bhavati indriya ādi pratyāsatteḥ asadātana tvāt asārvatrika tvāt ca 
ĀTV_108.13–109.3	 tatas ca yogyam api saha kārya sannidhānāt na karoti iti artha siddham kārya antaram eva atīndriyam sarva bīja avi abhicāri bhaviṣyati iti ced tat na tāvat upādeyam amūrtasya mūrtān upādeya tvāt paridṛśyamāna mūrta ghaṭita tayā mūrta antarasya tad deśasya anupapatteḥ na api saha kāryam mithas sahakāriṇām avyabhicāra anupapatteḥ 
ĀTV_110.13–110.16–111.17–112.3	 api ca evam sati prayojaka svabhāvaḥ na anvaya vyatireka gocaraḥ tad gocaraḥ tu na prayojakaḥ dṛśyam ca kārya jātam adṛśyena eva svabhāvena kriyate dṛśyena tu adṛśyam eva iti saḥ ayam yaḥ dhruvāṇi iti asya viṣayaḥ athavā vyatirekeṇa prayogaḥ vivāda adhyāsitam bījam sahakāri vaikalya prayukta aṅkura ādi kārya vaikalyam tad utpatti niścaya viṣayībhūta bīja jātīya tvāt yat punar sahakāri vaikalya prayukta aṅkura ādi kārya vaikalyam na bhavati na tat evam bhūtabīja jātīyam yathā śilā śakalam iti 
ĀTV_114.1–114.4–115.1–115.7	 na ca kim ukta sādhya vyāvṛtteḥ ukta sādana vyāvṛttiḥ udāhṛtāt kim vā paramparayā api tathāvidha prasava sāmarthya virahāt iti vyatireka sandehaḥ iti vācyam prāk eva śaṅkābījasya nirākṛta tvāt iti syāt etat mā bhūt sāmarthya asāmarthya lakṣaṇa viruddha dharma saṃsargaḥ astu bīja tvam eva prayojakam bhavatu ca sahakāri samavadhāne sati kartṛ svabhāva tvam bhāvasya tathā ca tad asannidhāne akaraṇam api upapadyatām tathā api tad jātīya mātraḥ eva iyam vyavasthā na tu ekasyām vyaktau karaṇa akaraṇa lakṣaṇa viruddha dharma saṃsargasya pratyakṣa siddha tayā tatra durvāra tvāt iti ced na virodha svarūpa anavadhāraṇāt 
ĀTV_117.9–117.11–118.14–118.18	 sa khalu dharmayoḥ paramparā bhāva rūpa tvam vā syāt nitya tva anitya tva vat dharmiṇi tad āpādaka tvam vā śīta uṣṇa tva vat tadvat tā ca daṇḍi tva kuṇḍali tva vat na prathamaḥ nirviśeṣaṇasya asiddha tvāt yāvat sattvam kiñcid karaṇāt sa viśeṣaṇasya tu virodha siddhau api adhyāsa anupapatteḥ yadā yat akaraṇam hi tadā tad karaṇasya abhāvaḥ na tu anyadā tad karaṇasya na ca etayoḥ eka dharmi samāveśam ātiṣṭhāmahe 
ĀTV_120.13–121.2	 na dvitīyaḥ bhāva abhāva vyatiriktayoḥ karaṇa akaraṇayoḥ asiddheḥ vyāpāra apara vyapadeśa sahakāri bhāva abhāvau hi karaṇa akaraṇe kārya bhāva abhāvau vā iti atireka siddhau api sva kālaḥ eva svabhāva pratikṣepa vat akaraṇa abhāvam ākṣipet karaṇam na tu anyadā na hi yaḥ yadā na asti sa tadā svabhāvam pratikṣeptum arhati iti virodhi abhāvam vā ākṣeptum tathā sati na kadāpi tat na syāt na vā kadāpi tad virodhau bhavet iti na asataḥ vidyate bhāvaḥ na abhāvaḥ vidyate sataḥ iti āyātam na vā virodhaḥ 
ĀTV_123.12–124.5	 nanu evam sati parimāṇa bhedaḥ api kāla bhedena na viruddhyate tatra api evam vaktum sukara tvāt na bādhaka balena tatra kāla bhedasya vivakṣita tvāt tathā hi na ārabdha dravyaiḥ eva dravya avayavaiḥ dravya antaram ārabhyate mūrta tva samāna deśa tvayoḥ ekadā virodhāt tathā ca ārambha pakṣe pūrva dravya nivṛttiḥ anivṛttau anārambhaḥ iti tatra nivṛttau āśraya bhedāt eva parimāṇa bhedaḥ anivṛttau saṃyogi dravya antara an upacaye kva parimāṇa bheda upalambhaḥ yaḥ virodham āvahet tad upacaye tu kva parimāṇa antara utpattiḥ āśraya anutpatteḥ atas eva sthailya atiśaya pratyayaḥ api tatra bhrāntaḥ tasmāt kāla bhedena api na parimāṇa bhedaḥ ekasmin dharmiṇī upasaṃhartum śakyate ityādi pada arhta cintā caturaiḥ saha vivecanīyam 
ĀTV_128.4–128.12	 astu tarhi iha api bādhakam balam prasaṅga tad viparyayoḥ ukta tvāt iti ced na tayoḥ sāmarthya asāmarthya viṣaya tvāt tatra ca ukta tvāt stām vā na tathā api tābhyām śakti aśaktyoḥ avivakṣita tvāt kāla bhedaḥ eva virodhaḥ sādhyate tathā upasaṃhartum aśakya tvāt yadā tadā iti upekṣya yat samartham tat karoti eva iti upasaṃhartum śakyam iti ced na kāla niyama avivakṣāyām yat samartham tat karoti eva iti kadācid syāt tathā ca sambhavavidheḥ atyanta ayogaḥ viruddhaḥ na tu ayogaḥ nīlam sarojam bhavati eva iti vat 
ĀTV_132.8–133.3	 nanu yat asamartham prathamam āsīt tasya sāmarthyam paścāt api kutas āgatam prathamam samarthasya vā paścāt kutra gatam na etat evam tat tad sahakārimataḥ tad tad kāraka tvam hi sāmarthyam atadvataḥ tad anyavataḥ vā tad akartṛ tvam asāmarthyam idam ca utpattikam asya rūpam te ca sahakāriṇaḥ sva upasarpaṇa kāraṇa vaśāt bhinna kālāḥ iti arthāt kāryāṇām api bhinna kālatā iti tathā api eka kāla sthaḥ eva bhāvaḥ jāta naṣṭaḥ tadā tadā tat kāryam karotu utpanna mātrasya tad svabhāva tvāt eka deśa stha vat iti ced 
ĀTV_135.11–135.19	 sā iyam eka kāla stha tā svarūpa apekṣayā sahakāri sānnidhya apekṣayā vā ādye na kiñcid anupapannam nityānām api evaṃrūpa tvāt vartamāna eka svabhāva tvāt sarva bhāvānām tat eva tu kvacid sa avadhi kvacid niravadhaī iti viśeṣaḥ sa avadhi tve api vyāpāra phala pravāha prakarṣa apakarṣābhyām viśeṣaḥ dvitīyaḥ tu syāt api yadi teṣām yaugapadyam bhavet kramiṇaḥ tu sahakāriṇaḥ iti uktam sahakāri sahitaḥ svabhāvena karoti iti vaktari tu jāta naṣṭaḥ eva karotu iti uttara prasaṅgaḥ nirargala śaiśavasya iti alam anena 
ĀTV_138.4–138.12	 tasmāt kāryasya saḥ eva kālaḥ kāraṇasya tu sa ca anyaḥ ca iti sambandhi kāla apekṣayā pūrva kāla tā vyavahāraḥ api ca yadā tadā iti sthāne yatra tatra iti prakṣipya tayoḥ eva prasaṅga tad viparyayoḥ kaḥ doṣaḥ na kaścid iti ced tarhi deśa advaitam vā kāraṇa bhedaḥ vā āpadyeta āpadyatām tat ādāya yoga ācāra naya nagaram pravekṣyāmaḥ iti ced na hetu phala bhāva vāda vairiṇam anapodya tatra praveṣṭum aśakya tvāt tad apavāde vā sattva ākhya sādhana śastra saṃnyāsinaḥ tava vahiḥ vāda saṅgrāma bhūmau api kutas bhayam 
ĀTV_143.15–143.18–144.17–144.20	 nanu yāvat yaḥ artha kriyāḥ bhinna deśāḥ tāvat bhedam kāraṇam astu kaḥ virodhaḥ iti ced na teṣām api pratyekam tad prasaṅgrasya tad avastha tvāt evam ekasya jagati vastu tattvasyāḥ alābhe sādhvī kṣaṇa bhaṅga sādhana pariśuddhiḥ astu tarhi kaścid doṣaḥ eva anayoḥ iti ced sa punar kasmin sādhye kim sāmarthya asāmarthyoḥ kim vā tad viruddham ārdhyāsena bhede āhosvit śakti aśaktyoḥ virodhe 
ĀTV_146.17–147.3–147.13–147.15	 na ādyaḥ sarvatra sāmarthye hi prasahya karaṇāt sarvatra aśaktau kvacid api akaraṇāt sarva deśa samāna svabhāva tve api asya sva upādāna deśaḥ eva tat kāryam karoti iti ayam asya svabhāvaḥ sva kāraṇāt āyātaḥ na niyoga paryanuyogau= arhati iti ced tarhi sarva kāla samāna svabhāva tve api tad tad sahakāri kālaḥ eva karoti iti ayam asya svabhāvaḥ sva kāraṇāt āyātaḥ iti kid na rocayeḥ na dvitīyaḥ viruddha dharma adhyāsena api abhede bheda vyavahārasya nirnimittaka tva prasaṅgāt anaikāntikaḥ ca hetuḥ kālataḥ api na bhedam sādhayet 
ĀTV_148.13–149.7	 na tṛtīyaḥ virodha lakṣaṇa yoge bādhaka sahasreṇa api virodhasya apanetum aśakya tvāt ayoge vā tat eva cintyam yat vidhāne yasya niṣedhaḥ yat niṣedhe vā yasya vidhānam tayoḥ ekatra dharmiṇi paraspara parīhāra sthita tayā virodhaḥ sa ca iha na asti tad deśa kārya kāri tvam hi tad deśa kārya akāri tvena viruddham tad vidhau tasya niyamena niṣedhāt na punar deśa antare tad kārya akāri tvena tasya aniṣedhāt na hi anyatra tad akaraṇam atatkaraṇam vā tatra tad karaṇasya abhāvaḥ api tu tatra tat akaraṇam iti ced hantaivambhūta virodha lakṣaṇa vyāvṛttiḥ bhinna kāla śakti aśaktyoḥ api iti ukta prāyam tad pratisanda dhīthāḥ 
ĀTV_151.7–151.13	 tasmāt prasaṅga tad viparyaya sthitau api asiddhaḥ viruddha dharma adhyāsaḥ nanu yat ekadā yat karoti tat yāvat sattvam tat karoti eva yathā kaścid śabdaḥ śabda antaram iti prasaṅgaḥ astu viparyayaḥ tu yat ekadā yat na karoti tat sarvadā eva tat na karoti yathā śilā śakalam aṅkuram na karoti ca ekadā kuśūla stham bījam aṅkuram iti ced tat etat jāti abhiprāyeṇa vā syāt vyakti abhiprāyeṇa vā syāt 
ĀTV_154.13–154.16–156.1–156.4	 prathame dvayam api anaikāntikam aniyama darśanāt dvitīye dvayam api anyathā siddham ekānta asāmarthya prayukta tvāt atyanta akaraṇasya sāmarthye sati sahakāri sannidhi prayukta tvāt karaṇa niyamasya etena yat yat karoti tad tad utpanna mātram yathā karma vibhāgam yat utpanna mātram yat na karoti tat na kadācid api yathā śilā śakalam aṅkuram iti nirastam atra api pūrva vadana ekāntān yathā siddhī doṣau iti 
ĀTV_156.15–156.16–157.8–157.12	 na api tṛtīyaḥ kṛtaka tva anitya tva ādeḥ api paraspara abhāvavat tā mātreṇa eva virodha prasaṅgāt iti astu tarhi tasya eva tena eva sahakāriṇā sambandhaḥ asambandhaḥ ca iti virodaḥ na vikalpa anupapatteḥ tathā hi sambandhinaḥ sambandhi antare svābhāva svāhbāvyam vā viruddhi eta abhāva pratiyogi tvam vā tadā eva iti sahitam vā tatra eva iti sahitam vā ubhaya sahitam vā tathā eva iti sahitam vā iti 
ĀTV_160.4–160.15	 na prathamaḥ anabhyupagamāt na dvitīyaḥ satkārya pratiṣedhāt na tṛtīyaḥ prāc pradhvaṃsa abhāvayoḥ bhāva samāna kāla tva anabhyupagamāt na caturthaḥ sa hi na tāvat sthiti yaugapadya niyamena sambandhinoḥ tad asiddheḥ itas eva tad siddhau= itaretara āśraya tvam niyama siddhau hi virodha siddhiḥ tad siddhau ca bhede sati niyama siddhiḥ iti na ca anyatas tad siddhiḥ tad abhāvāt aniyata upasarpaṇa apasarpaṇa kāraṇa prayukta tvāt ca sambandha asambandhayoḥ na api vināśasya ahetuka tvāt ayam virodhaḥ arthāt siddhyati tasya api asiddheḥ dhruva bhāvi tve tu pakṣyāmaḥ na api pañcamaḥ na hi tat eva tarā eva saḥ eva sahakārī asti na asti ca iti abhyupagacchāmaḥ 
ĀTV_164.4–164.18	 nanu samavadhānam nāma sahakāriṇām dharmaḥ saṃyogaḥ bhavadbhiḥ iṣyate sa ca tebhyaḥ vyatiriktaḥ avyāpya vṛttiḥ ca iti api tathā ca saḥ eva tadā eva tatra eva asti na asti ca iti anatireke sthira vādinaḥ vyastāni api bījavāri dharaṇi dhāmāni tāni eva iti tebhyaḥ api kārya utpatti prasaṅgaḥ vyāpya vṛtti tve ca sarvatra rakta ādi vibhramaḥ śabda ādi kārya utpatti prasaṅgaḥ ca tasmāt asaṃyuktebhyaḥ anyaḥ eva saṃyukta svabhāvāḥ paramāṇavaḥ jātāḥ iti eva jyāyaḥ na etat evam kṣaṇika paramāṇau api asya virodhasya durvāra tvāt tathā hi pūrva diś ava sthitaḥ paramāṇuḥ yathā para diś avasthitena paramāṇunā a para diś avacchedena āvṛta rūpaḥ utpannaḥ tathā eva kim pūrva diś avacchedena api na vā ubhayathā vai ādye ubhayatas api anupalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ dvitīye tu ubhayatas api upalambha āpattiḥ tṛtīye punar saḥ eva durātmā virodhaḥ saḥ eva tena eva tadā eva āvṛtaḥ anāvṛtaḥ ca iti 
ĀTV_167.1–167.6	 prakāra bhedam upādāya avirodhaḥ iti ced kaḥ punar asau digantara avacchedaḥ yadi hi yat diś ava= chedena eva saṃyuktaḥ tad diś ava= chedena eva asaṃyuktaḥ api tatas virodhaḥ syāt iha tu na evam iti ced hanta saṃyoga saṃyoginoḥ bheda pakṣe api yadi evam siddhānta vṛttāntaḥ syāt kīdṛśaḥ doṣaḥ iti etena vyatireka pakṣe api nirastaḥ 
ĀTV_168.4–168.10	 adhikaḥ ca tatra āśraya hetu dṛṣṭānta siddhau pramāṇa abhāvaḥ avastuni pramāṇa apravṛtteḥ pramāṇa pravṛttau alīka tva anupapatteḥ evam tarhi avyavahāre sva vacana virodhaḥ syāt iti ced tat kim sva vacana virodhena teṣu pramāṇam upadarśitam bhavati vyavahāra niṣedha vyavahāraḥ vā khaṇḍitaḥ syāt aprāmāṇikaḥ ayam vyavahāraḥ avaśya abhyupagantavyaḥ iti vā bhavet 
ĀTV_170.12–170.18	 na tāvat prathamaḥ na hi virodha sahastreṇa api sthire tasya krama ādi virahe vā śaśa śṛṅge vā pratyakṣam anumānam vā darśayitum śakyam tathā tve vā kṛtam bhauta kalahena dvitīyaḥ tu iṣyate eva prāmāṇikaiḥ avacanam eva tarhi prāptam kim kurmaḥ yatra vacanam sarvathā eva anupapannam tatra avacanam eva śreyaḥ tvam api paribhāvaya tāvat niṣprāmāṇike arthe mūkavāvadvakayoḥ kataraḥ śreyān 
ĀTV_172.5–172.12	 evam viduṣā api bhavatā na mūkībhūya sthitam api tu vyavahāraḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ eva asatī iti ced satyam yathā aprāmāṇikaḥ sva vacana viruddhaḥ arthaḥ mā prasāṅkṣīt iti manyamānena tvayā aprāmāṇikaḥ eva asati vyavahāraḥ svīkṛtaḥ tathā asmābhiḥ api pramāṇa cintāyām aprāmāṇikaḥ vyavahāraḥ mā prasāṅkṣīt iti manyamānaiḥ aprāmāṇikaḥ eva sva vaca virodhaḥ svīkriyate yadi tu ubhayatra api bhavān samāna dṛṣṭiḥ syāt asmābhiḥ api tadā na kiñcid ucyate iti 
ĀTV_174.11–174.16	 tṛtīye tu aprāmāṇikaḥ ca api avaśya abhyupagantavyaḥ ca iti kasya iyam ājñā iti bhavān eva praṣṭavyaḥ vyavahārasya suddaḍha nirūḍha tvāt iti ced aprāmāṇikaḥ ca suddaḍha nirūḍhaḥ ca iti vyāghātaḥ kathan cit api vyavasthita tvāt iti ced aprāmāṇikaḥ ced na kathañcid api vyavatiṣṭhate prāmāṇikaḥ ca iti tat eva ucyatām iti vāde vyavasthā 
ĀTV_176.4–176.8–177.7–177.10	 jalpa vitaṇḍayoḥ tu pakṣa ādiṣu pramāṇa praśna mātra pravṛttasya na sva vacana virodhaḥ tatra pramāṇena uttaram aniṣṭam aśkyam ca apramāṇena eva tu uttare sva vacanena eva bhaṅgaḥ mad ukteṣu pakṣa ādiṣu pramāṇam na asti iti svayam eva svīkārāt anuttare tu apratibhā eva iti yadi ca vyavahāra svīkāre virodha parihāraḥ syāt asau svīkriyeta api na tu evam na khalu sakala vyavahāra abhājanam ca tad niṣedha vyavahāra bhājanam ca iti vacanam parasparam avirodhi 
ĀTV_178.4–178.8–179.12–179.16	 vidhi vyavahāra mātra abhiprāyeṇa abhājana tva vāde kutas virodhaḥ iti ced hanta sakala vidhi niṣedha vyavahāra abhājana tvena kiñcid vyavahriyate na vai ubhayathā api sva vacana virodhaḥ ubhayathā api avastunā eva tena bhavitavyam vastunaḥ sarva vyavahāra viraha anupapatteḥ na iti pakṣe sakala vidhi niṣedha vyavahāra virahī iti anena eva vyavahāreṇa virodhāt avyavahṛtasya niṣeddhum aśakya tvāt vyavahriyate iti pakṣe api viṣaya svarūpa paryālocanayā eva virodhāt na hi sarva vyavahāra aviṣayaḥ ca vyavahriyate ca iti 
ĀTV_180.18–181.8	 yadi ca avastunaḥ niṣedha vyavahāra gocara tvam vidhi vyavahāra gocaratā api kim na syāt pramāṇa abhāvasya ubhayatra api tulya tvāt iti bandhyā sutasya avaktṛ tve acetana tva ādikam eva pramāṇam vaktṛ tve na kiñcid iti ced na tatra api suta tvasya vidyamāna tvāt na hi bandhyāyaḥ sutaḥ na sutaḥ tathā sati sva vacana virodhāt vacana mātram eva etat na tu parama arthaḥ sutaḥ eva asau iti ced na acaitanyasya api evaṃrūpa tvāt cetanāt anyat svabhāva antaram eva hi acetanam iti ucyate caitanya nivṛtti mātram eva iha vivakṣitam tat ca sambhavati eva iti ced na tatra api asuta tva nivṛtti mātrasya eva vivakṣita tvāt 
ĀTV_183.1–183.8	 asuta tva nivṛtti mātrasya sva rūpeṇa kṛti jñaptyoḥ asāmarthye samartham artha antaram adhyavaseyam anantarbhāvya kutas hetu tvam iti ced na acaitanye api asya nyāyasya samāna tvāt vyāvṛtti rūpam api tat eva gamakam yat atasmāt eva yathā śiṃśapā tvam bandhyā sutaḥ tu asutāt iva ghaṭa ādeḥ sutāt api devadatta ādeḥ vyāvartate atas na hetuḥ iti ced nanu idam acaitanyam api asya evaṃrūpam eva na hi bandhyā sutaḥ cetanāt iva devadatta ādeḥ acetana ādi kāṣṭha ādeḥ na vyāvartate 
ĀTV_185.17–186.3	 vaktṛ tvam vastu eka niyataḥ dharmaḥ sa katham avastuni sādhyaḥ virodhāt iti ced sa punar ayam virodhaḥ kutas pramāṇāt siddhaḥ kim kaktṛ tva viviktasya avastunaḥ niyamena upalambhāt āhosvit vastu viviktasya vaktṛ tvasya anupalambhāt iti na tāvat avastu kena api pramāṇa upalambha gocaraḥ tathā tve vā na avastu na api uttaraḥ samāna tvāt na hi vaktṛ tvam iva avaktṛ tvam api vastu viviktam kasya cit pramāṇasya viṣayaḥ 
ĀTV_187.11–187.20	 tad vivikta vikalpa mātram tāvat asti iti ced tad saṃsṛṣṭa vikalpane api kaḥ vārayitā nanu vaktṛ tvam vacanam prati kartṛ tvam tat katham avastuni tasya sarva sāmarthya viraha lakṣaṇa tvāt iti ced avaktṛ tvam api katham tatra tasya vacana itara kartṛ tva lakṣaṇa tvāt iti sarva sāmarthya virahe vacana sāmārthya virahaḥ na viruddhaḥ iti ced atha sarva sāmarthya virahaḥ bandhyāḥ tasya kutas pramāṇāt siddhaḥ avastu tvāt eva iti ced nanu etat api kutas siddham sarva sāmarthya virahāt iti ced saḥ ayam itas tatas kevalaiḥ vacanaiḥ nirdhana adharmaṇikaḥ iva sādhūn bhrāmayan paraspara āśraya doṣam api na paśyati 
ĀTV_189.17–190.3–191.7–191.11	 krama yaugapadya virahāt iti ced na tad viraha siddhau api pramāṇa anuyogasya anivṛtteḥ suta tve ca parāmṛṣyamāṇe tad avinābhūta sakala vaktṛ tva ādi dharma prasaktau kutas krama yaugapadya viraha sādhanasya avakāśaḥ kutas tarām ca avastu tva sādhanasya kutas tamām ca avaktṛ tva ādi sādhanānām tasmāt pramāṇam eva sīmā vyavahāra niyamasya tad atikrame tu aniyamaḥ eva iti na hi apratīte devadatta ādau sa kim gauraḥ kṛṣṇaḥ vā iti vaiyātyam vinā praśnaḥ tatra api yadi ekaḥ apratīta parāmarṣa viṣayaḥ eva uttaram dadāti na gauraḥ iti aparaḥ api kim na dadyāt na kṛṣṇaḥ iti na ca evam sati kācid artha siddhiḥ pramāṇa abhāva virodhayoḥ ubhayatra api tulya tvāt iti 
ĀTV_192.7–193.2	 nanu apratīte vyavahāra abhāvaḥ iti yuktam kūrma roma ādayaḥ tu pratīyanta eva na hi ete vikalpāḥ kañcid artha bhedam anullikhante eva utpadyante na ca pramāṇa āspadam eva vyavahāra āspadam iti tattvam uktam tathā hi śaśa viṣāṇam iti jñānam anyathā khyātiḥ vā syāt asat khyātiḥ vā na tāvat ādyaḥ te rocate tathā sati hi kiñcid āropyam kiñcid āropaviṣayaḥ iti syāt tathā cāra upaviṣayaḥ tatra eva asti āropaṇīyaḥ tu anyatra eva iti jitam naiyāyikaiḥ na api dvitīyaḥ kāraṇa anupapatteḥ indriyasya jñāna janane viṣaya adhipati ena eva vyāpārāt liṅga śabda ābhāsayoḥ anyathā khyāti mātra janaka tvāt apahastitasva arthayoḥ ca asat khyāti janaka tve śaśa viṣāṇa ādi śabdāt kūrma roma ādi vikalpānām api utpatti prasaṅgāt niyāmaka abhāvāt 
ĀTV_195.19–196.6	 sa hi saṅketaḥ vā syāt śabda svābhāvyam vā ādyaḥ tāvat saṅketa viṣayā pratīteḥ eva parāhataḥ tatas eva tad pratītau itaretara āśraya tvam pada saṅketa balena eva pratītau sva artha aparityāgāt tathā ca ananvitāḥ padārthāḥ eva anvitatayā parisphuranti iti viparīta khyātiḥ eva anuvartate sva artha parityāge tu punar api aniyamaḥ asāmayika artha pratyāyanāt śabda sva abhāvyāt tu niyame vyutpanna vat avyutpannasya api tathāvidha vikalpa udaya prasaṅgāt iti 
ĀTV_197.17–198.6	 vāsanā viśeṣāt iti ced atha āsat ullekhinaḥ pratyayasya vāsanā eva kāraṇam uta vāsanā api na tāvat ādyaḥ śaśa viṣāṇa ādi pratyayānām sadātana tva prasaṅgāt kadācid prabodhāt kadācid iti ced na prabodhaḥ api sahakāri antaram vā atiśaya paramparā paripākaḥ vā ādye vāsanā eva iti pakṣa anupapattiḥ dvitīye api yadi artha antara pratyāsatteḥ tadā pūrvavat sva santati mātra adhīna tve tu vāhya vāda vyāghātaḥ nīla ādi buddhīnām api vāsanā paripākāt eva utpādāt vāsanā api iti pakṣe tu tad anyaḥ api hetuḥ kaścid vaktavyaḥ sa ca vicāryamāṇaḥ pūrva nyāyam na ativartate iti 
ĀTV_200.9–200.15	 na ca śaśa viṣāṇa ādi śabdānām asat arthaiḥ saha sambandha avagamaḥ api tathā hi para buddhīnām anullekhāt tad viṣayasya api anullekhaḥ eva na ca artha kriyā viśeṣaḥ api asti yatas viṣaya viśeṣam unnīya tatra saṅketaḥ gṛhyatām na ca saṅketayituḥ eva vacanāt tad avagatiḥ tad viṣayāṇām sarveṣām vacanānām apratīta viṣaya tvena agṛhīta samaya tayā apratipādaka tvāt 
ĀTV_202.10–202.16	 na ca śaśa viṣāṇam uccārayataḥ kaḥ cit abhiprāyaḥ vṛttaḥ iti tad viṣayaḥ asya vācyaḥ iti sugrahaḥ samayaḥ iti vācyam na hi evam ākāraḥ samaya grahaḥ gām badhāna iti ukte apratīta śabda arthasya api abhiprāya mātra pratītau samaya graha prasaṅgāt na ca viśeṣa antara vinākṛtaḥ kalpanā mātra viṣayaḥ asya vācyaḥ iti sāmpratam ghaṭa kūrma roma ādīnām api tad artha tva prasaṅgāt 
ĀTV_204.5–204.13	 na ca sarve pratipattāraḥ sva sva vāsanayā asat artha śabda sambandha pratipatti bhājaḥ iti sāmpratam paraspara vārtā anabhijña tayā apara artha tva prasaṅgāt na hi svayam kṛtam samayam agrāhayitvā paraḥ vyavahārayitum śakyate na ca vyavahāra upadeśau antareṇa grāhayitum api na ca gām vadhāna iti vat śaśa viṣāṇa padārthe vyavahāraḥ na ca ayam asau aśvaḥ iti vat upadeśaḥ na ca yathā gauḥ tathā gavaya iti vat upalakṣaṇa atideśaḥ na ca iha prabhinna kamala udare madhūni madhukaraḥ pibati iti vat prasiddha pada sāmānādhikaraṇyam 
ĀTV_206.21–207.3–208.21–209.3	 tat amūḥ śaśa viṣāṇa ādi kalpāḥ na asat khyāti rūpāḥ tathā tve kāraṇa abhāvāt mūka svapna vat āsāṃvyāvahārika tva prasaṅgāt ca tasmāt anyathā ākhyāti rūpā eva iti na etat anurodhena api avastunaḥ niṣedhevyavahāra gocara tvam iti bhavatu vā asat khyātiḥ tathā api na tatas vyatirekaḥ prāmāṇikaḥ tathā hi kaḥ ayam vyatirekaḥ nāma yat yatas vyatiricyate tasya tatra abhāvaḥ vā tad abhāva svabhāva tvam vā tatra na tāvat krama yaugapadyayoḥ śaśa viṣāṇe abhāvaḥ pramāṇa gocaraḥ vṛkṣa rahita bhūbhṛt kaṭaka vat krama yaugapadya rahitasya śaśa viṣāṇasya pramāṇa agocara tvāt 
ĀTV_210.5–210.9–211.16–212.2	 na api krama yaugapadya abhāva rūpa tvam śaśa viṣāṇasya prāmāṇikam ghaṭa abhāvavat śaśa viṣāṇasya pramāṇena anupalambhāt ghaṭa abhāvaḥ api na pramāṇa gocaraḥ iti ced na tasya tad vivikteḥ asvabhāvasya api pramāṇataḥ eva siddheḥ asiddhau vā tatra api avyavahāraḥ eva ghaṭaḥ tāvat svābhāva viraha svabhāvaḥ pramāṇa siddhaḥ tādrūpyeṇa kadācid api anupalambhāt etāvatā eva tad abhāvaḥ api ghaṭa viraha svabhāvaḥ siddhaḥ iti ced na ghaṭa bhāvasya tad abhāva viraha svabhāva tva anabhyupagamāt na ca anyasya svabhāve pramāṇa gocare tad anyaḥ api siddhaḥ syāt atiprasaṅgāt 
ĀTV_213.15–214.2–215.5–215.13	 evambhūtau eva ghaṭa tada bhāvau yat ekasya paricchitiḥ aparasya vyavacchittiḥ iti ced na ghaṭa vat ghaṭa abhāvasya api prāmāṇika tva anabhyupagame svabhāva vāda an avakāśāt pramāṇa siddhe hi vastuni svabhāva vāda avalambanam na tu svabhāva vāda avalambanena eva vastu siddhiḥ iti bhavatām eva tatra tatra jayadundubhiḥ tat kim idānīm svābhāva viraha svabhāvaḥ ghaṭaḥ pramāṇān na eva siddhaḥ tava dṛṣṭyā evam etat ghaṭaḥ hi yādṛś tādṛś svabhāvaḥ tāvat pramāṇa patham avatīrṇaḥ tasya tu yadi paramārthataḥ abhāvaḥ api kaścid syāt syāt paramārthataḥ syāt na ca etat abhyupagamyate bhavatā tasmāt ghaṭa vat tad abhāvasya api prāmāṇika tvena eva anayoḥ paraspara viraha lakṣaṇa vyatireka siddhiḥ aprāmāṇika tve tu anyoḥ api na tathā abhāvaḥ iti śaśa viṣāṇa ādiṣu api iyam eva gatiḥ 
ĀTV_217.13–218.4	 nanu kālpanika rūpa sampattiḥ eva astu anumāna aṅgam tat na tasyāḥ sarvatra sulabha tvāt nanu pakṣa sa pakṣa vipakṣāḥ tāvat vastu avastu bhedena dvi rūpāḥ tatra ye kalpanā upanītāḥ tatra kālpanikāḥ eva pakṣa dharma anvaya vyatirekāḥ pramāṇa upanīteṣu tu prāmāṇikāḥ eva iti vibhāgaḥ tat iha kālpanikān niragneḥ yadi api prameya tva ādeḥ vyāvṛttiḥ kālpanikī siddhā tathā api prāmāṇikāt jala hrada ādeḥ prāmāṇikī eva eṣitavyā sā ca na siddhā iti kutas tasya hetu tvam evam prāmāṇike śabde pakṣīkṛte prāmāṇikaḥ eva hetu sadbhāvaḥ vaktavyaḥ na ca asau cākṣuṣa tvasya asti iti saḥ api katham hetuḥ evam kṛtaka tvasya api vastu eka niyatasya dharmasya vāstavaḥ eva anvayaḥ vaktavyaḥ vastunaḥ vipakṣāt ca vāstavaḥ eva vyatirekaḥ 
ĀTV_219.14–220.8	 na ca tasya tau staḥ tat katham asau api hetuḥ iti pralapitam etat na hi niyāmakam antareṇa sampadam kalpanā tu rate vipadam prati tu vilambate iti śakyam vaktum tathā ca niragnikam api kūrma roma sa dhūmam iti kalpanā mātreṇa vipakṣa vṛtti tvāt dhūmaḥ api na agnim gamyet vāstavyām rūpa sampattau kim anena kālpanikena doṣeṇa iti ced tarhi vāstavyām asampattau kim kā alpa nikyā tayā iti samānam virodha avirodhau viśeṣaḥ iti ced kutas eṣaḥ ubhayoḥ ekatra vastu avastu tvāt anyatra avastu tvāt iti ced tat kim kālpanikaḥ api dhūmaḥ vastu bhūtaḥ yena kūrma romṇaḥ tena saha virodhaḥ syāt kvacid vastu bhūtaḥ eva iti nirdhūma tvam api kvacid vastu bhūtam iti tena api virodhaḥ eva tasmāt yathā kālpanikī vipattiḥ na doṣāya tathā kālpanikī sampattiḥ api na guṇāya iti vyatireka bhaṅgaḥ 
ĀTV_223.11–223.15–226.10–226.13	 astu tarhi dhru babhāvi tvena vināśasya ahetuka tve siddhe kṣaṇa bhaṅgaḥ na vikalpa anupapatteḥ tat dhi tādātmyam vā nirupākhyā tvam vā tad kārya tvam vā tad vyāpaka tvam vā abhāva tvam eva vā iti na pūrvaḥ niṣedhya niṣedhayoḥ ekatva anupapatteḥ upapattau vā viśvasya vaiśvarūpya anupapatteḥ nanu kāla antare artha kriyām pratyaśaktiḥ eva asya na astitā sā ca kāla antare samartha itara svabhāva tvam eva iti ced nanu ayam eva kṣaṇabhaṅgaḥ tathā ca asiddham asiddhena sādhayataḥ kaḥ te pratinandaḥ 
ĀTV_228.1–228.7	 api ca deśa antara kāla antara anuṣaṅgiṇyasya na astitāḥ yadi ayam eva nūnam anakṣaram idam uktam yat ayam eva deśa antara kāla antara anuṣaṅgī iti yadi vā sva deśa kāla vat kāla antara deśa antarayoḥ api na astitān anuṣaṅge astitva prasaṅgaḥ aśakteḥ katham astu śakteḥ sattā lakṣaṇa tvāt iti ced atha kāla antara kāryam prati sva kāle aśaktiḥ asattvam kim vā sva akāryam api prati kāla antare aśaktiḥ asattvam 
ĀTV_229.7–229.11–230.5–230.9	 ādye sva kāle api asattva prasaṅgaḥ tadānīm api tasya tādrūpyāt kāla antara kāryam prati evem etat iti ced kim ayam mantra pāṭhaḥ na hi yaḥ yatra aśaktaḥ sa tad apekṣayā na asti iti vyavahiyate na hi rāsabha apekṣayā dhūmaḥ jagati na asti tat kasya hetoḥ na hi aśaktasya svarūpam nivartate iti dvitīye tu yadi kāla antara ādhārā aśaktiḥ katham tad ātmikāḥ tad ādhārā ced tadā eva asattva prasaṅgaḥ kāla antare tu viparyayaḥ tasmāt vidhiḥ ātmā asya bhāvasya niṣedhaḥ tu tatas paraḥ saḥ api ca ātmā iti kaḥ prekṣaḥ śṛṇvan api na lajjate 
ĀTV_231.14–232.4–234.5–234.8	 astu tarhi bhāva svarūpa atiriktā nivṛttiḥ na asti iti vākyasya sa upākhyā iti śeṣaḥ nanu ayam api kṣaṇa bhaṅgasya udgāraḥ sa ca kaphoṇi guḍāyitaḥ varttate bhavatu vā nivṛttiḥ asamarthā tathā api ahetuka tve tasyāḥ kim āyātam tucchasya kīdṛśam janma iti ced yādṛśaḥ kāla deśa niyamaḥ saḥ api tasya kīdṛśaḥ iti ced evam tarhi na ghaṭa nivṛttiḥ kvāpi kadāpi sarvatra eva sadā eva vā iti syāt bhavatu prathamaḥ eva iti ced saḥ ayam bhāvanā astitā svarūpa pratiṣedhaḥ vā bhāva pratiṣedhena nivṛtti svarūpa niruktiḥ vā iti ādye bhāvasya eva sadātana tva prasaṅgaḥ dvitīye tu nivṛtteḥ eva iti 
ĀTV_235.17–236.3–237.13–237.16	 astu tarhi tad kārya tvam eva dhruva bhāvi tvam na tasya api kāryaḥ iti pakṣe virodhāt tasya eva kāryaḥ iti asiddheḥ yat kiñcid panna mātrasya kāryam saḥ eva tasya nāśaḥ iti ced tarhi yasyāḥ sāmagryā yat kāryam tat tad arikta anapekṣam iti sādhana arthaḥ tam imam kaḥ nāma na anumanyate kāryam eva vināśaḥ iti tu kena anurodhena vyavahartavyam kim tad virahavat tvāt kāryasya kim vā tad viraha rūpa tvāt na tāvat pūrvaḥ sahakāriṣu api tathā aprasaṅgāt viraha svarūpa anirukteḥ ca na dvitīyaḥ sa hi kārya kāle kāraṇasya yogyā anupalambha niyamāt vā bhavet vyavahāra anurodhāt vā atirikta vināśe bādhaka anurodhāt vā iti 
ĀTV_240.1–240.8	 na prathamaḥ upalambhyante hi paṭa kāle vema ādayaḥ na te te iti ced kim atra pramāṇam abhedaḥ api vim pramāṇam iti ced mā bhūt tāvat sandeha sthitau api anupalabdhi bala ālambana vilayāt na dvitīyaḥ na hi paṭaḥ jātaḥ iti ukte tantavaḥ naṣṭāḥ iti kaścid vyavaharati paṭasya anatiḥ ekāt tantu mātra janmani bheda agrahāt avyavahāraḥ iti ced na tarhi vyavahāra balam api visabhāga santatau tāvat vyavahāra balam asti iti ced na etat evam 
ĀTV_242.6–242.12	 yadi hi tantumālā eva paṭa nivṛttiḥ katham tad āśrayaḥ tad ātmakaḥ vā paṭaḥ prāk anyā eva asau iti ced na tāvat jāti kṛtam anya tvam upalabhyate vyakti kṛtam tu na adya api siddhyati atas eva tad siddhau itaretara āśraya tvam tathā api yadi evam syāt kīdṛśaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced na kaścid kevalam pramāṇa abhāvaḥ vyavahārān anurodhaḥ ca tat asiddhau api siddhi atas tasya nimitta antara apekṣaṇāt 
ĀTV_245.3–245.12	 api ca tantu vināśaḥ sāmānyatas tantu viraha svabhāvaḥ vā syāt tad viparītaḥ vā ādye katham tantu antaram na hi sāmānyatas nīlam anīla viruddha svabhāvam anīla antaram dvitīye katham tad virodhī na hi nīlam sāmānyatas api nīla antara virodhi viśeṣa mātraḥ eva ayam virodhaḥ iti ced tat kim sāmānyatas anubhaya svabhāvaḥ eva vināśaḥ om iti bruvataḥ anyataram upādāya vināśa vyavahāra anupapattiḥ sāmānyasya alīka tvāt tatra virodhaḥ api kim kariṣyati iti ced vilīnam idānīm viruddha dharma adhyāsena bheda pratyāśayā tasya tad āśraya tvāt 
ĀTV_249.1–249.10	 nanu atirikta abhāva pakṣe yathā paṭaḥ paṭa antara abhāvavān ca tad jātīyaḥ ca abhāvaḥ vā paṭa virodhī paṭa antara saha vṛttiḥ ca iti na kaścid virodhaḥ tathā kārya abhāva pakṣe api bhaviṣyati iti na etat evam pratiyoginā hi tādātmya saṃsarga eka jātīya tvāni na iṣyante apratiyogi tva prasaṅgāt bhinna kāla tvāt sāmānyatas viruddha dharma saṃsargāt ca ati pariyoginā tu saṃsarge kaḥ doṣaḥ na hi bheda vijātīyata eka kālatāḥ saṃsarga virodhinyaḥ tādātmyam hi saṃsargi tve viruddham virodhi tvam ca te ca na iṣyate eva na api bādhaka anurpdhaḥ tad abhāvāt 
ĀTV_252.13–252.20	 nanu ghaṭa abhāve ghaṭaḥ asti na vai ādye ghaṭavati tad abhāvaḥ kapāle ghaṭaḥ asti iti tāni api tadvanti prasajyeran na asti iti pakṣe anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ abhāva antaram antareṇa tatra nāstita avyavahāre bhāva antare api tathā prasaṅgaḥ na bhāva antarasya sasvajātīya tvena aviruddha sajātīya tvāt viruddha jātīyasya vā samāna jātīyatva anupapatteḥ anya tva mātreṇa tathā vyavahāre tadvatī api prasaṅgāt abhāvasya tu viruddha svabhāva tayā eva abhāva antara anubhava tarkayoḥ abhāvāt iti 
ĀTV_255.16–256.4	 bhinna abhāva janmani ghaṭatāt vyakyam doṣaḥ iti ced na ghaṭatāt vyaktyam hi yadi ghaṭa tvam eva abhimatam eva tat na hi abhāva janmani ghaṭaḥ aghaṭa tām upaiti iti abhyupagaccchāmaḥ tad kāla sattvam ced na tarhi abhāvaḥ jātaḥ kāla antare ghaṭa anavasthāna svabhāvaḥ eva hi tad abhāvaḥ astu tarhi nirupādāna tvam bādhakam janmanaḥ upādānavyāpta tvāt iti ced na dharma grāhaka pramāṇa bādhāt bhāva avacchedāt ca vyāpteḥ etena nirupādeya tvam vyākhyātam guṇa ādi siddhau ca anaikāntika tvāt iti 
ĀTV_257.10–257.17	 astu tarhi vyāpaka tvam dhruva bhāvi tvam iti ced na atādātmyāt atatkaraṇa tvāt ca asmat diśā api vyāpti grahaḥ na māhitya niyamena virodhitayā viṣama samaya tvāt na api janma ānantari a niyamena tad asiddheḥ siddhau vā tatas eva kṣaṇa bhaṅga siddheḥ kim anena bhaviṣyat tā mātreṇa vyāpaka tvam asti iti ced astu na tu etāvatā hetu antarā anapekṣa tva siddhiḥ adyatana ghaṭasya śvastana kapāla mālayā eva anaikāntika tvāt iti 
ĀTV_260.13–261.2	 etena sa apekṣa tvam vyabhicāraḥ api syāt vināśa hetṛnā praibandha vaikalya sambhavāt iti parāḥ tam kapāla santati tulya yogakṣema tvāt vināśasya iti astu tarhi caramaḥ pakṣaḥ tathā hi vināśaḥ na jāyate abhāva tvāt prāk abhāva vat jātaḥ api vā nivartate jāta tvāt ghaṭa vat iti na etat evam prāgabhāvaḥ jāyate abhāva tvāt vināśi tvāt vā dhvaṃsa vat ghaṭa vat vā ajātaḥ vā na nivartate ajāta tvāt ākāśa vat śaśa viṣāṇa vat vā iti vat asādhana tvāt 
ĀTV_263.1–263.11	 kim eteṣām dūṣaṇam iti ced bhāva avicchinna vyāptika tvāt aprayojaka tvam prāc pradhvaṃsa abhāva grāhaka pratyakṣa bādhaḥ prāk paścāt ca kārya unmajjana prasaṅga lakṣaṇa pratikūla tarkaḥ ca atha unmajjane kaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced kāla viccheda pratyayasya anubhaya ātmaka tva prasaṅgaḥ ayathārtha tve tasya dvi candra darśana kāle candra deśa viccheda vat tadvataḥ kāla avicchede bhāvasya prāc pradhvaṃsa saha vṛtti tvena avirodha prasaṅgāt yathārtha tve tu bheda sthitau tad unmajjana anupapatteḥ etena prāc abhāva pradhvaṃsa unmajjanam tad kāle ca prāc abhāva unmajjanam apāstam bhāva vat abhāvayoḥ api ubhaya virodhi svabhāva tvāt iti 
ĀTV_267.13–268.2	 kutas punar sthira siddhiḥ pratyabhijñānāt kṣaṇikatva anupapatteḥ ca lakṣaṇa abhedena vyabhicāri jātīya tvāt pratyabhijñā na pramāṇam iti ced na avāntara lakṣaṇa bhedena avyabhicāra niyamāt kim tat iti ced viruddha dharma asaṃsṛṣṭa viṣaya tvam siddham ca tat atra evambhūtam api kadācid vyabhicaret iti ced na viruddha dharma saṃsargān āskanditasya ekatva pratyayasya vyabhicāre sarvatra ekatva uccheda prasaṅgāt tathā ca aneka tvam api na syāt iti bhava niṣkiñcanaḥ tasmāt bheda pravṛttau avaśyam viruddha dharma saṃsargaḥ tad asaṃsarge vā avaśyam bheda vyāvṛttiḥ iti bheda abheda vyavahāram aryādā 
ĀTV_270.1–270.9	 niṣkampa pradīpa kuṅmaleṣu nipuṇam nibhālayantaḥ api na viruddha dharma saṃsargam īkṣāmahe atha ca pratyabhijñānam avadhūya tatra bhedaḥ eva padam vidhattaḥ iti ced kasya pramāṇasya balena āśraya nāśasya hutāśana nāśa hetu tvena vijñāta tvāt tasya ca atra pratikṣaṇam upalabdheḥ varti tailayoḥ uttarottaram apacīyamāna tvāt pūrvasya nāśaḥ uttara utpādaḥ ca nyāya siddhaḥ iti ced nanu ayam pratyanīka dharma saṃsargaḥ eva naṣṭha tvānaṣṭa tvayoḥ āśraya nāśānāśayoḥ vai ekatra tejasi anupapatteḥ 
ĀTV_271.14–271.19	 saḥ ayam śatam śiraḥ cchede api na dadāti viṃśati pañcakam tu prayacchati iti kim atra brūmaḥ bhaviṣyati tarhi iha api viruddha saṃsargaḥ durūhaḥ iti ced atha saḥ eva ayam sphuṭikaḥ iti atra pramāṇa pratīta saṃsargāṇām virodha āśaṅkyate tad pratīti virodhānām saṃsargaḥ atha apratīti svarūpa virodha saṃsargāḥ eva kecid viruddha tayā saṃsṛṣṭa tayā vā iti 
ĀTV_272.12–273.5	 na prathamaḥ prāk eva nirākṛta tvāt na dvitīyaḥ ayogyānām anupalambha bādhita tvāt ayogyānām api kāraṇa ādi vyāpya vyāpaka vigama vilokana vyāvartita tvāt na tṛtīyaḥ tasya atiprasañjaka tayā sarvatra ekattva uccheda prasaṅgāt iti etena pratyabhijñānāt eva lakṣaṇa bhāgam ākṛṣya anumānena sthairya siddhiḥ tathā hi vivāda adhyāsitaḥ bhāvaḥ kāla bhede api na bhidyate tad bhede api viruddha dharma asaṃsṛṣṭa tvāt yaḥ yat bhede api na viruddha dharma saṃsṛṣṭaḥ na asau tad bhede api bhidyate yathā pratisambandhi paramāṇu bhede api ekaḥ paramāṇuḥ tathā ca ayam vivāda adhyāsitaḥ bhāvaḥ tasmāt kāla bhede api na bhidyate iti 
ĀTV_275.15–276.2–278.1–278.8	 atra vyāptau na kaścid vipratipadyate pakṣa dharma tā tu prasādhitā eva kṣaṇikatva anupapattiḥ ca anugata vyavahārān anyathā siddheḥ śabda liṅga vikalpāḥ hi sādhāraṇam rūpam anupathāpayantaḥ na tṛṇa kubjīkaraṇe api samarthāḥ iti avivādam bāhya artha sthitau sthirā sthira vicārāt tat ca alīkam vā ākāraḥ vā bāhyam vastu vā iti trayaḥ pakṣāḥ tatra na prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ tat dhi na tāvat anubhavāt eva tathā vyavasthāpyam tasya alīka tva anullekhāt tathā tve vā pravṛtti virodhāt na hi alīkam eva tat iti anubhūya api artha kriyā arthī pravarttate anya nivṛtti sphuraṇāt na eṣa doṣaḥ iti ced etat eva asat vidhi rūpasya eva sphuraṇāt na hi śabda liṅgābhyām iha mahīdhara uddeśe anagniḥ na bhavati iti sphuraṇam api tu agniḥ asti iti 
ĀTV_279.17–280.6	 yadi api nivṛttim aham pratyemi iti na vikalpaḥ tathā api nivṛtti padārtha ullekhaḥ eva nivṛtti ullekhaḥ na hi anantarbhāvita viśeṣaṇā viśiṣṭapratītiḥ nāma tatas yathā sāmānyam aham pratyemi iti anuvyavasāya abhāve api sādhāraṇa ākāra sphuraṇāt vikalpa dhīḥ sāmānya buddhiḥ pareṣām tathā nivṛtta pratyaya ākṣiptā nivṛtti buddhiḥ asmākam iti ced hanta sādhāraṇa ākāra parisphuraṇe vidhi rūpa tayā yadi sāmānya bodha vyavasthā kim āyātam asphurat abhāva ākāre cetasi nivṛtti pratīti vyavasthāyāḥ 
ĀTV_282.1–282.7	 na hi agopa ūḍhoyam iti vikalpaḥ kim tu gauḥ iti tatas anya nivṛttim aham pratyemi iti evam ākāra abhāve api nivṛtti ākāra sphuraṇam yadi syāt kaḥ nivṛtti pratītim apahnuvīta anyathā tu atad pratibhānam tathā iti vyavahṛtiḥ iti gavā ākāre cetasi turaga bodhaḥ iti astu na ca nivṛtti mātra pratibhāse api pravṛtti sambhavaḥ na hi aghaṭaḥ na asti iti eva ghaṭa arthī pravartate api tu ghaṭaḥ asti iti 
ĀTV_283.8–283.17	 aghaṭasya eva nivṛttiḥ iti pratītau na ayam doṣaḥ iti ced na ghaṭa nivṛtti apratikṣepe niyamasya evā asiddheḥ tad pratikṣepe tu kaḥ tatas anyaḥ vidhiḥ niṣedha pratikṣepasya eva vidhi tvāt nivṛtteḥ apari sphuraṇe gām badhāna iti deśitaḥ aśvam api badhnīyāt iti ced na bhavet api evam yadi aśvaḥ api gauḥ syāt kintu gauḥ gauḥ aśvaḥ aśvaḥ iti anyathā nivṛttau api kutas te samāśvāsaḥ iti nivṛtti antarāt ced anavasthā nivartya nivṛtti tadadhikaraṇānām svarūpa sāṅkarye pravṛtti saṅkaraḥ syāt svarūpa bhedena eva niyame vidhi mātra pratibhāse api tathā kim na syāt 
ĀTV_286.8–286.13	 svarūpa bhedaḥ eva anya apohaḥ anya apoḍha svarūpa tvāt vidheḥ iti ced na alīka pakṣe tad abhāvāt tasya sva rūpa vidhau analīka tva prasaṅgāt sva lakṣaṇasya ca vikalpān ārohāt api ca gām badhāna iti deśitaḥ gavi pravṛttaḥ na aśve tat apratīteḥ yadā tu aśvam upalapsyate tadā tatra pravṛtti unmukhaḥ api gorabhāvam pratītyā eva nivartsyati iti kim anupapannam 
ĀTV_289.1–289.11	 syāt etat na hi anubhavam avadhūya bhavitum kṣamam iti kaḥ vidhi sphuraṇam apanhutām tad upasarjanī bhūtaḥ tad niṣedhaḥ api sphurati eva anyathā vidheḥ avacchedaka tva anupapatteḥ na hi anyatas viśeṣyam avyāvartayataḥ viśeṣaṇa tvam nāma na cā anyatas vyāvartanam vyavacchitti pratyāyanāt anyat tatas yathā indīvara puṇḍarīka ādi śabdebhyaḥ guṇībhūta nīla dhavala ādi vidhi śekharā pratītiḥ tad anya vyavacchedaḥ tu tad garbha ābha kāyamāṇaḥ tathā sarvatra iti ced astu tāvat evam vidhiḥ tu sphurati iti atra samprati naḥ nirbandhaḥ anyathā avacchedya avacchedakayoḥ apratīteḥ avacchittiḥ api na syāt yathā utpala ādau eva nīla tva ādi apratītau 
ĀTV_292.6–292.12	 na ca niṣedhyam aspṛśatī pratītiḥ niṣedham spraṣṭum arhati tasya tad nirūpaṇa adhīna nirūpaṇa tvāt na ca niṣedha antaram eva niṣedhyam itaretara āśraya prasaṅgāt para anapekṣa nirūpaṇe tu vidhau na ayam doṣaḥ iti tatas pratītau itaretara āśraya tvam uktam saṅkete sañcārya yat parihṛtam jñāna śriyā tat etat grāmya jana dhandhīkaraṇam golaka ādi vat sthāna antara sañcārāt 
ĀTV_296.10–296.13–298.3–298.5	 sphuratu vidhi alīkam iti ced na vyāghātāt kiñcid iti vidhi arthaḥ na kiñcid iti cā alīka arthaḥ atad rūpa parāvṛtti mātreṇa alīka tve sva lakṣaṇasyāḥ api alīka tva prasaṅgāt rūpa mātra parāvṛttau tu katham vidhiḥ nāma vidhi aṃśasya āropita tvāt ayam eva doṣaḥ iti ced na sva lakṣaṇa vidheḥ vikalpa asaṃsparśāt sāmānya vidheḥ anupagamāt pariśeṣāt alīka vidhau virodhasya eva sthiteḥ 
ĀTV_299.7–299.13–302.4–302.7	 bheda agrahāt vidhi vyavahāra mātram iti ced sambhavet api etat yadi sva lakṣaṇam api vidhi tvam apahāya sphuret yadi ca alīkam api niṣedha rūpa tām parihṛtya prakāśeta na ca evam ubhayoḥ api niraṃśa tayā prakāra antaram upādāya aprathanāt aprathamāna rūpā sambhavāt ca kālpanikasyām śāṃśi bhāvasya atas eva mūlaḥ eva nihitaḥ kuṭhāraḥ sādhāraṇam ca rūpam vikalpa gocaraḥ na ca alīkam tathā bhavitum arhati tasya hi deśa kāla anugamaḥ na svābhāvikaḥ tuccha tvāt na kālpanikaḥ tasyāḥ kṣaṇika tvāt na āropitaḥ anyatra api asiddheḥ 
ĀTV_303.19–304.10	 bheda agrahāt eka tva mātram anusandhīyate iti ced na bhāvikasya bhedasya abhāvāt bhāve vā kālpanika tvasya vyāghātāt parama artha asataḥ parama artha abheda paryavasāyi tvāt āropitasya agraha anupapatteḥ abheda āropa anavakāśāt ca āropitā asattvasya parama artha sattva prasaṅgāt catur koṭi nirmuktasya ca ati prasañjaka tvāt tad agrahasya trailokye api sulabha tvāt anyatra pāramārthika bheda pratītau katham abhedaḥ āropyatām iti ced evam tarhi yasya pratibhāse yat na āropyate niyamena tasya eva aprakāśe tadāropyam na tu tad nāmaka mātrasya ati prasañjaka tvāt atas eva na vyadhikaraṇasya api sataḥ asataḥ vā bhedasya āgrahaḥ abheda āropa upayogī iti 
ĀTV_308.1–308.9	 na api nyāyat anya apoha siddhiḥ tad abhāvāt yad bhāva abhāva sādhāraṇam tad anyavyāvṛtti niṣṭham yathā amūrta tvam yat ca atyanta vilakṣaṇānām sā lakṣaṇya vyavahāra hetuḥ tad anya vyāvṛtti rūpam iti nyāyau staḥ iti ced na kāla atyaya apadeśāt na hi prathamānasya niṣṭhā nyāya sādhyāḥ nāma prathana śarīram tu cintitam eva iti niṣphalaḥ prayāsaḥ yadā ca analīkaḥ eva dhruvam nyāyasya anubhava ābhāsaḥ tadā kā eva kathā alīke na hi tasya apratīyamānam api kiñcid asti yat nyāyena sādhyam iti uktam 
ĀTV_309.16–310.10	 kiñ ca idam bhāva abhāva sādhāraṇyam na tāvat ubhaya rūpa tvam virodhāt na tad dharma tvam anabhyupagamāt na hi go tvam abhāvasya api dharmaḥ iti abhyupagamyate na tad dharmi tvam anaikāntāt vyaktiḥ api bhāva abhāva dharma śālinī na niṣedha eka rūpā iti na tad ubhaya sādṛśyam asambhavāt atannivṛttya eva tathā tve sādhya aviśeṣāt na api astināsti sāmānādhikaraṇyam virodhāt anyathā siddheḥ ca na hi yat asti tat eva na asti iti pratyaya gocaraḥ syāt prakāra antaram āśritya syāt eva iti ced evam tarhi tam eva prakāra bhedam upādāya vidhi vyavasthāyām kaḥ virodhaḥ yena pratibandhaḥ siddhyet tasya vidhi rūpa tāyām asti nāma kim adhikam upaneyam iti ced niṣedha rūpa tve api na asti nāma kim adhikam upaneyam iti samānam atas eva sādhāraṇyam iti ced tathā api kim tad ubhaya ātmaka tvam ubhaya parīhāraḥ vā iti aśkyam etat 
ĀTV_313.20–314.11	 tasmāt asti nāstibhyām upādhi antara upasamprāptiḥ prāpta upādhi niyamaḥ vā iti sārthaka tvam tayoḥ tat etat vidhau api tulyam śānta aśeṣa viśeṣa tvāt alīka pakṣe kva upādhi antara vidhiḥ tat niyamaḥ vā iti viśeṣa doṣaḥ tatas go śabdaḥ go tva viśiṣṭa vyakti mātra abhidhāyī paryavasitaḥ tāḥ tu viprakīrṇa deśa kāla tayā na artha kriyā arthi prārthanām anubhavitum īśate iti pratipattā viśeṣa ākāṅkṣaḥ sā ca tasya akāṅkhā asti goṣṭhe kālākṣī dhenuḥ ghaṭodhnī mahā ghaṇṭā nāndinī ityādibhiḥ niyāmakaiḥ vidhāyakaiḥ vā nivāryate iti vadhau na kaścid doṣaḥ go tva viśiṣṭa sada sahat vyakti mātra pratīteḥ tat eva asti ādi pada prayoga vaiphalyam iti ced tāvat mātra pratipatti artham eva tat aneka pratipatti artan tu tad upayogaḥ tasya prāc apratīteḥ iti uktam 
ĀTV_316.20–317.3–321.9–321.13	 yaḥ tu nipuṇam manyo vikalpam eva pakṣayati sma yat jñānam yad bhāva abhāva sādhāraṇa pratibhāsam na tena tasya viṣaya tvam yathā go jñānasya aśvena ityādi tat yadi go vikalpasya aśva viṣaya tvam eva tad bhāva abhāva sādhāraṇyam go vyapi bāhye tathā tatas sādhya aviśiṣṭa tvam atha asti ādi viśeṣa ākāṅkṣā tadā asādha araṇyam na hi udāhṛtaḥ go vikalpaḥ aśva astyādi viśeṣam ākāṅkṣati niyama vidhau tu virodhaḥ eva na hi atad viṣayasya tat viśeṣa niyama ākāṅkṣā nāma go jñānasya api viśeṣa niyama ākāṅkṣā prasaṅgāt tadīyasat asattva anupadarśnam ced tat yadi svarūpam eva tatas asiddhiḥ doṣaḥ na hi go vikalpaḥ go sva rūpam na upadarśayati iti mama kadāpi siddham tava ca adya api upādhi antaram ced ana ekāntaḥ na hi yaḥ yasya upādhi antaram na upadarśayet na asau tat api iti niyamaḥ 
ĀTV_323.1–323.13	 nanu niyamaḥ eva tathā hi yat na yat samaveta dharma bodhanam na tat tad svarūpa bodhanam yathā go vikalpa śabdau turage tathā ca tau govyapi nīlatva ādi apekṣayā iti vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ dharma bodhe api hi dharmāṇām kasyacid bodhaḥ kasyacid abodhaḥ ca iti upakāra bhedāt niyamaḥ syāt upakāra bhedaḥ ca śakti bhedāt bhavet na ca evam prakṛte anavsthā prasaṅgāt tatas śakteḥ abhedāt upakāra abhede sarva upādhi sahita bodhaḥ abodhaḥ vā iti dvayī gatiḥ iti pratibandha siddhiḥ duṣprayuktam etat upādhi tadvatām bhede pratiniyata sāmagrī bodhya tvāt eva tat ayaugapadye bodha ābodha upapatteḥ pratiniyata sāmagrī bodhya tvasya api svabhāva vaicitrya nibandhana tvāt tasya api sva kāraṇa adhīna tvāt tasya api anvaya vyatireka siddha tvāt tasya api kārya unneya tvāt iti 
ĀTV_326.15–326.18–327.9–327.19	 yat tu śakteḥ abhedāt ityādi tat tadā śobheta yadi dharmi mātra adhīnaḥ tad bodha mātra adhīnaḥ vā tāvat mātra bodha sāmagrī adhīnaḥ vā yāvat upādhi bheda bodhaḥ syāt na ca evam etena bhedāt dharmiṇaḥ pratītau api śabda liṅga dvārā dharmāṇām ced apratītiḥ indriya dvārā api mā bhūt iti ādikam tu karṇa sparśe kaṭi cālanam apāstam tad tad upādhi upalambha sāmagrī viraha kāle prasañjitasya iṣṭa tvāt vicitra śakti tvāt ca pramāṇānām liṅgasya prasiddha pratibandha pratisandhāna śaktika tvāt śabdasya samaya sīmavikrama tvāt indriyasya tu artha śakteḥ api apekṣaṇāt na tu sambaddhaḥ arthaḥ iti eva pramāṇaiḥ pramāpyate atiprasaṅgāt yasya tu upādheḥ upalambhaḥ eva yena pramāṇena dharmī upalabhyate tasya anupalambhe sa tena na upalabhyate iti param yujyate sarva upādhi anupalambhe vā tathā ca siddha sādhanam iti saṅkṣepaḥ 
ĀTV_330.6–330.20	 syāt etat yadi indriyeṇa samāna viṣayau eva liṅga śabdau tatas pratibhāsa bhedaḥ anupapannaḥ eka viṣaya tvam hi pratibhāsā bhedena vyāptam savya itara nayana dṛṣṭa vat dṛṣṭam na ca iha tathā yathā hi pratyakṣe cetasi deśa kāla avasthā niyatāni parisphuṭa rūpāṇi sva lakṣaṇāni pratibhānti na tathā śabde laiṅgika vikalpe api tatra hi vijātīya vyāvṛttam iva paraspara ākāra saṅkīrṇam iva asphuṭam iva pratyakṣa aparicitam kiñ cit rūpam ābhāsamānam anubhava viṣayaḥ na ca upāya bheda mātreṇa pratibhāsa bhedaḥ upapadyate na hi pratipatti upāyāḥ pratipatti ākāram parivarttayitum īśate na ca ekam vastu dvi ākāram iti pratibandha siddhiḥ asya prayogaḥ yaḥ ayam kvacid vastuni pratyakṣa pratibhāsāt viparītaḥ pratibhāsaḥ na asau tena eka viṣayaḥ yathā ghaṭa grahāt paṭa pratibhāsaḥ tathā ca gavi pratyakṣa pratibhāsāt viparītaḥ pratibhāsaḥ vikalpa kāle iti 
ĀTV_332.17–333.7	 idam api avadyam citrā citra pratibhāsābhyām mithas viruddhābhyām eka nīla viṣayābhyām anaikāntāt na hi citra adhyakṣe yat nīlam cakāsti tat eva paścāt na kevalam tadā eva vā puruṣa antarasya yena akāreṇa eka viṣaya tvam tayoḥ na tena eva virodhaḥ yena ca virodhaḥ na tena eka viṣaya tvam dharma antara ākāreṇa virodhaḥ nīla mātra ākāreṇa ca eka viṣaya tā iti ced nanu iha api dharma antara ākāreṇa virodhaḥ gotva vat piṇḍa mātra ākāreṇa ca eka viṣaya tā iti tāvat mātra nirākaraṇe asiddhaḥ hetuḥ pūrvatra siddha sādhanam na hi śabda laiṅgika vikalpa kāle deśa kāla niyama ādayaḥ api sarve eva dharma viśeṣāḥ viṣaya bhāvam āsādayanti iti abhyupagacchāmaḥ 
ĀTV_335.5–335.10–338.11–338.14	 nanu dharmaṇi eva sphuṭa asphuṭa pratibhāsa bhedaḥ katham na kathañcid yathā yathā hi dharmāḥ pratibhānti tathā tathā sphuṭa iti pratibhāna vyavahāraḥ yathā yathā ca dharmāṇām apratipattiḥ tathā tathā pratibhānasya māndya vyavahāraḥ dūra antika ādau pratyakṣe api lokānām na tu sarvathā eva apratipattau vidūra ādi pratyayaḥ api pakṣaḥ eva iti ced astu na tu tāvatā api dharma dharmi bheda siddhau pratyakṣa bādhasya tad sandehe api sandigdha anaikāntikasya vā parihāraḥ tāvatā api pratibhāsa bhedasya upapatteḥ yadi ca na evam dūratama ādi pratyayeṣu vaḥ samāśvāsa viṣayaḥ yasya arthaḥ labhyate iti ced nanu lābhaḥ api pūrva pūrva upalabdhān upamardanena eva na hi sattva dravya tva pārthiva tva vṛkṣa tva ādikam paribhūya śiṃśapā labhyate 
ĀTV_339.13–340.5–342.14–342.18	 yatra artha kriyā siddhiḥ iti ced sarveṣām anuvṛtteḥ kasya artha kriyā iti kim niścāyakam na kiñcid kintu saṅkīrṇa artha kriyā virahāt ekam eva tatra vastu na ca ekasmin pratibhāsa bhedaḥ iti ekaḥ eva pratyayaḥ tatra sa ālambanaḥ iti brūmaḥ iti ced tathā api katamaḥ iti aniścaye saḥ eva anāśvāsaḥ asaṅkīrṇā api ca artha kriyā na vyaktitaḥ sāmagrītaḥ sarva sambhavāt atas eva na santānataḥ na hi eka santāna niyatā kācid arthakriyā nāma kāñcid artha kriyām prati pratyakṣa anupalambha gocaraḥ eva tathā vyavasthāpyate iti ced tarhi dūratama ādi upalabdhāḥ api tathā vyavasthāpyāḥ sarveṣām eva teṣām tām tām artha kriyām prati prayojaka tāyāḥ anvaya vyatireka gocara tvāt iti syāt etat na dharma antara ākāreṇa pratibhāsa bhedaḥ bheda hetuḥ kintu parokṣa aparokṣa rūpa tayā sā hi na dharma bhedān api upādāya samarthayitum śakyāḥ teṣu api parokṣa aparokṣa jñāna udayāt tatra api dharma antara anusaraṇe anavasthānāt iti ced 
ĀTV_344.4–344.19	 na tayoḥ aviṣaya ākāra tvāt dvividhaḥ hi jñāna dharmaḥ viṣaya avacchedaḥ jāti bhedaḥ ca tatra viṣaya avaccheda bhedena viṣayasya bheda sthitiḥ abheda nirākaraṇam vā na tu dvitīyena tasya kāraṇa bhedena eva upapatteḥ śruti anumiti smṛti vat yathā ca viṣaya bhede api kāraṇa bhedāt eva aparokṣa jātīyam indriya jam jñānam tathā viṣaya bhede api kāraṇa bhedāt eva parokṣa aparokṣa jātīyam indriya liṅga jñānam bhavat kena vāryate vāraṇe vā kārya bhedam prati kāraṇa bhedaḥ aprayojakaḥ syāt tathā ca ākasmikaḥ saḥ āpadyeta jāti bhedaḥ ayam na tṛpādhi bhedaḥ iti kim atra niṣṭaṅkam kāraṇam iti ced anubhavaḥ eva na hi vyavasāya kāle pārokṣya apārokṣya smṛti tva anubhūti tvāni parisphuranti asau agnimān ayam agnimān saḥ agnimān iti sphuraṇāt anu vyavasāya kāle tu tad pratibhāsaḥ amum anuminomi imam paśyāmi tam smarām iti ullekhāt katham tarhi parokṣaḥ arthaḥ pratyakṣaḥ ca iti vyavahāraḥ yathā anumitaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ smṛtaḥ iti 
ĀTV_347.1–347.8	 yat api atyanta vilakṣaṇānām ityādi tat api sandigdha anaikāntikam vidhinā api tathābhūtena sā lakṣaṇya vyavahārasya nirvāhāt tathā hi ayam vyavahāraḥ na nirnimittaḥ na api aneka nimittaḥ na api aneka asaṃsarga eka nimittaḥ atiprasaṅgāt tatas aneka saṃsarga eka nimittaḥ ayam pariśiṣyate tathā ca tādṛśasya vidhi rūpa tve kaḥ virodhaḥ yena vyāptiḥ syāt pratyuta niṣedha rūpa tāyām eva virodhaḥ darśitaḥ prāk iti kṛtam pallava samullāsaiḥ 
ĀTV_348.4–348.8–349.6–349.10	 na api pravṛtti ādi vyavahāra nirvāhaka tvam apoha kalpanāyāḥ anya avabhāsāt anyatra pravṛttau atiprasaṅgāt adhyavasāyāt ayam adoṣaḥ iti ced atha kaḥ ayam adhyavasāyaḥ kim alīkasya vastu dharma tayā avabhāsaḥ kim vā vastu ātmaka tayā tatas bheda āgrahaḥ vastu vāsanā samuttham vā iti na prathamaḥ vikalpe tad anavabhāsanāt na dvitīyaḥ asādhāraṇa viṣaya tayā śabda vikalpayoḥ apravṛtti prasaṅgāt tasya asāmayika tvāt tasmāt vikalpa vastunoḥ cakṣūrasa vat sarvathā virodhaḥ eva sādhāraṇa viṣaya tve tu vastu tva apratibhāsanam tasya asādharaṇa tvāt 
ĀTV_351.1–351.17	 na tṛtīyaḥ pravṛtti sāmāna adhikaraṇya niyama anupapatteḥ bheda agrahasya sarvatra sulabha tvāt atebhyaḥ bhedaḥ gṛhītaḥ iti ced kim ateṣu gṛhyamāṇeṣu agṛhyamāṇeṣu vā na ādyaḥ ateṣām api sva lakṣaṇanām vikalpa agocara tvāt na dvitīyaḥ avijñāta avadheḥ bhedasya aprathanāt prathane vā adhyavaseya abhimata sva lakṣaṇāt api bhedaḥ gṛhyeta aviśeṣāt gṛhītāt agrahaḥ bhedasya agṛhītebhyaḥ tu tat grahaḥ iti ced yadi dharma lakṣaṇaḥ bhedaḥ tadā viparyayaḥ svarūpa lakṣaṇaḥ ced aviśeṣāt sarvatas tad grahaḥ anyatra tādātmya grahāt niḥsvarūpa tvāt tasya kva svarūpa lakṣaṇaḥ bhedaḥ iti ced agṛhītāt api tathā syāt aviśeṣāt niḥsvarūpam api svarūpam iva bhinnam iva prathitam iti ced tat kim adhyavaseya apekṣayā sa svarūpam iva na prathitam adhyavaseya svarūpam iva vā sphuritam ādye apratipattiḥ vā syāt aviśeṣāt niḥsvarūpa pratipattiḥ vā syāt ubhayathā api sāmānādhikaraṇya pravṛttī na syātām dvitīyaḥ tu prāk eva dūṣitaḥ 
ĀTV_356.3–356.8–358.1–358.6	 na api caturthaḥ nīla anubhava vāsanā samutthasya pīta anubhavasya nīle pravarttaka tva prasaṅgāt na anubhavaḥ pravarttakaḥ api tu vikalpaḥ sa ca yasmāt tasya eva viṣayaḥ iti ced yasmāt iti sākṣāt paramparayā vā prathame śābda laiṅgika jñānānām apravarttaka tva prasaṅgaḥ dvitīye tu saḥ eva atiprasaṅgaḥ anubhava vyāpāra puraskārāt niyamaḥ iti ced kaḥ puraskāra arthaḥ na tāvat anubhava eka viṣaya tvam vikalpena tad asaṃsparśāt na api anubhava tu a āropaḥ sva ātmani kalpanā poḍhā bhra anta tvāt viṣaye ca abhilāpa saṃsarga yogya pratibhāsa tvāt tathā anavasāse vā vikalpa tva vyāghātāt viśeṣa upalabdhau cāra upāsambhavāt 
ĀTV_360.11–360.14–362.9–362.13	 na api tad dharma prāmāṇya āropaḥ tasya aniyata viṣaya tve pravṛtti niyama anupapatteḥ parama artha sat viṣaya tve ca tasya vikalpa saṃsarga prasaṅgāt alīka viṣaya tve ca apravṛtteḥ alīkasya analīka tayā sphuraṇam tu niṣiddham na api anubhavāt sva ātmanaḥ bheda āgrahaḥ eva tad vyāpāra puraskāraḥ svarūpasya svatas avagateḥ viṣaya bhedasya ca prāk eva nirūpaṇāt na api apārokṣyam tasya api sva ātmani sarva jñāna sādhāraṇa tvāt viṣaye ca vikalpasya tad abhāvāt tathā abhāve api anyatra niyata pravṛtti anupapatteḥ 
ĀTV_364.5–364.14	 na api viṣaya sārūpyam tad abhāvāt kā hi parama artha sadalīkayoḥ samāna rūpa tā nāma yadi rūpa śabdaḥ dharmmi vācakaḥ samāna śabdaḥ ca eka paryyāyaḥ kva artha saṅgatiḥ prakṛte yadi vā rūpam dharmmaḥ samānaḥ ca ekaḥ vā eka jātīyaḥ vā iti tathā api kva artha saṅgatiḥ prakṛte atad vyāvṛttiḥ iti ced na tasya ca alīkā nalīka niṣṭhatayā ekatva eka jātīya tvayoḥ abhāvāt ābhimānikaḥ ayam sārūpya vyavahāraḥ na pāramārthikaḥ iti ced na abhimānasya eva cintyamāna tvāt na hi cintita prakārān paribhūya aparaḥ abhimānaḥ nāma 
ĀTV_366.12–367.3	 svabhāvāt eva kaścid vikalpaḥ kasmiṃścid eva asphurite api pravarttayati kim atra kriyatām sa ca asya svabhāva bhedaḥ sva kāraṇāt eva āyātaḥ tatra kaḥ paryyanuyojyatām iti ced tat kim apratyāsannaḥ eva vikalpaḥ tatra pravarttayati pratyāsatti antara abhāvāt svabhāva pratyāsannaḥ vā vyavahṛtiḥ eva vā pratyāsattiḥ na prathamaḥ atiprasaṅgāt dvitīye tu svabhāvena uttaram syāt kintu tat eva sphuraṇam na hi vyavahāre pravarttayitavye svabhāva pratyāsattim avadhūya jñāna jñeyayoḥ aparaḥ kaścid viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ sat asat anirvacanīya artha khyāti vādibhiḥ api svabhāva pratyāsatteḥ avarjjanīya tvāt iti vakṣyamāṇa tvāt tṛtīye tu vyaktam ātma āśrayaḥ sva vyavahāra niyamam prati eva nimitta anusaraṇāt 
ĀTV_368.5–368.8–369.5–369.12	 kāraṇa śakteḥ asat utpatti vat niyamaḥ iti ced satyam etat cintanīyam kāraṇa śaktyā api niyata jāti niyatayā bhavitavyam anyathā jvalana vikalpāt jale api pravṛtti prasaṅgāt dāha ādi samartha ākāra vikalpa jātīyam tāttvike vahnau pravarttayati iti jātiḥ vā upādhiḥ vā niyāmakaḥ iti ced na tarhi ratna marīci nicaye tatas pravartteta tad jātīyasya dahanaḥ eva pravarttana sāmarthyāt tādrūpyeṇa tasya eva prathanāt iti ced prathatām na tu tasya pravarttana yogya tā tatra prathana niyatāḥ vahni sva lakṣaṇe vahni vikalpāt apravṛtti prasaṅgāt svīkuru vā tasya api tatra sphuraṇam parihara vā vahni vikalpāt avahnau pravṛttim iti 
ĀTV_371.4–371.6–372.9–372.16	 etena ākāra sārūpyam niyama hetuḥ apāstaḥ arthanīya sārūpya abhāve api pravṛtti darśanāt anarthanīya sārūpya mātrasya ca ati prasañjaka tvāt na ca bāhya vāde jñāna jñeyayoḥ vivakṣita sārūpya sambhavaḥ sāmagrī vaiṣamyāt sāmye vā jāḍya caitanyayoḥ eka śeṣa prasaṅgāt na ca sāmye api avāntara viśeṣāt kāryya viśeṣa vyavasthā mithas sāmagrī ananuvidhānena jāyamāna tvāt na ca kāryya unneyam sāmagrī sāmyam bāhye dhūma ādi anuvidhīyamānasya kāraṇasya dṛśya tvāt dhūma jñānasya ca tad vyabhicāra upalambhāt na ca tat eva kāraṇam ekatra dṛśyam adṛśyam ca anyatra iti yuktam 
ĀTV_374.7–374.11–375.2–375.9	 yadi ca nīlim ādiḥ vijñānasya jāti viśeṣaḥ katham tat atipatya jñeyam spṛśet jñeyasya ced katham jñānam tad viśiṃṣyāt iti jāti saṅkara āpādana prastāve cintita prāyam tasmāt sphuritaḥ eva jñānam pravarttayati iti gale pādukayā api aṅgīkārayitavyaḥ gati antara abhāvāt tarhi sphurite su a ākāre eva pravarttayatu tatra pravṛttaḥ eva ca arthī tad sadṛśam artham āsādayati prabhāyām pravṛttaḥ maṇi vat iti ced na abhimata artha kriyā sāmarthya virahiṇyapravṛtteḥ na ca bāhye vikalpa ākārāra upasambhavaḥ tasya tena asaṃsparśāt na ca ākāre bāhya tva āropaḥ svarūpe sphurati asva rūpa aropāna vakāśāt prabhāyām tu maṇi buddhyā eva maṇi arthī pravarttate na tu tat abuddhyā iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ api ābhāsaḥ 
ĀTV_377.17–377.19–378.18–379.4	 na ca ākāra vāde asphurataḥ arthasya sattāyām pramāṇam api asti ākārakādācitka tvasya taimirika keśa ādi ākāreṇa anaikāntika tvāt artha kriyā samvādasya api sphuritasya ākāra mātra śarīra tvāt bāhyasya ca asiddheḥ nirālambana artha ākāra vat ca kvacid vāsanā vaśāt artha kriyā kāraḥ api nirālambana eva bhaviṣyati iti vipakṣe bādhaka abhāvāt pratibandhasya api asiddheḥ tasmāt bāhya siddhiḥ sa ākāram ca jñānam iti bāla lolupa tvam iti 
ĀTV_380.17–381.4	 astu tarhi bāhyam eva sva lakṣaṇam vikalpasya viṣayaḥ yadi api sva rūpeṇa asāmayika tayā tat na abhilāpa saṃsarga yogyam tathā api atad rūpa parāvṛtti pratyāsattyā sādhāraṇa rūpa tām āpannam sat tathā bhavati eva yathā hi ekaḥ gaura go vyāvṛttaḥ tathā apare api gāvaḥ iti ced atha kaḥ ayam agauḥ nāma kim ekasya go sva lakṣaṇasya anātmā āhosvit tad gata dharma virahī 
ĀTV_382.4–382.10	 prathame na gavā antare api go śabda vikalpau pravartteyātām aśva ādi vat anātma tva aviśeṣāt atiprasaṅgaḥ ca mahiṣa mātaṅga ādya go vyāvṛttyā aśve api go vyavahāra prasaṅgāt sa goḥ api vyāvarttate iti ced tat kim abhimataḥ gauḥ goḥ api na vyāvarttate vyāvarttate kintu svayam api asau gauḥ iti ced yadi ago vyāvṛttiḥ eva asya go tvam tad aśve api samānam anyat ced tat ucyatām 
ĀTV_384.8–384.9–384.18–385.4	 dvitīye tu tad gata dharmma virahi vyāvṛttaḥ tadvān eva syāt tatra ca na vivādaḥ mithas sambhinna ākārāḥ piṇḍāḥ eva sādhāraṇam rūpam astu kṛtam atad rūpa parāvṛttyā iti ced na sambheda abhāvāt sa hi na vāstavaḥ piṇḍānām viruddha dharmma adhyasta tvāt nābhimānikaḥ śabaleya ādeḥ bhedena eva prathanāt tad dharmmāṇām sambheda abhimānaḥ iti ced na dharmmi atirikta dharmma anabhyupagamāt abhyupagame vā paryyavasitam vivādena 
ĀTV_386.9–386.15	 syāt etat bhinnānām eva sva lakṣaṇānām samāna ākāra vikalpa janana sāmarthyam astu tad apekṣayā ca kecid gāvaḥ iti vyapadiśyante kecid agāvaḥ iti tatra sāmarthyam sva kāraṇa niyata tvāt aparyyanuyojyam anyathā sāmānyeṣu api sāmānya antaram kalpyeta anugata vyavahāra anurodhāt tathā gopiṇḍeṣu api go tvasya teṣu eva vyavasthiti anurodhāt ubhaya mukhī ca evam anavasthā syāt iti ced 
ĀTV_388.12–388.19	 yadi evam nimitta antaram anapekṣya eka vyavahāraḥ atyanta bhinnaiḥ evam bhinna vyavahāraḥ eva abhinnena ekena kenacid kim na sādhyate śakti svabhāva avalamba nasya ubhayatra api tulya tvāt atha evam sati eka vyavahāraḥ kvacid api na syāt nirnimittaḥ vā bhavet ubhayam api aniṣṭam tat etad tulyam aneka vyavahāraḥ api aniṣṭam tasmāt ekena eka vyavahāra vat anekanā api aneka vyavahāraḥ eva iti sāmarthya niyamaḥ 
ĀTV_389.17–390.9	 kā gatiḥ tarhi sāmānyeṣu anekeṣu eka vyavahārasya yā candramasi ekasmin aneka vyavahārasya bhrāntaḥ asau iti ced ayam api bhrāntaḥ eva bādhakasya ubhayatra api tulya tvāt sarvu atra bhrānaḥ astu iti ced bheda vyavahāraḥ api tathā kim na syāt artha kriyā sthiteḥ iti ced vyakti bheda abheda vyavasthāpaka artha kriyā bheda abheda vat sajātīyāsa jātīya tva vyavasthāpaka artha kriyā asā jāti a vaijātye api kim na paśyasi te api bhrānte iti ced artha kriyā bhedaḥ api bhrāntaḥ iti tulyam astu evam iti ced tyaja tarhi bāhya vyasanam ayam eva āśayaḥ iti ced tatra vakṣyāmaḥ 
ĀTV_392.4–392.10	 mā bhūt vā artha kriyā asā jāti a vaijātya avagamaḥ bhrānti anugamaḥ api ekam nimittam anādṛtya katham tat api hi kāryyam ājātyam sāmagrīsājātyam antareṇa ākasmikam āpadyeta anyathā tad paramparā ālambanam api viḍambanam eva bhinnaiḥ taiḥ taiḥ abheda vyavahāra siddhau vyaktibhiḥ eva tathābhūtābhiḥ abhimata siddheḥ tad anusaraṇa prayāsa vaiphalyāt tasmāt āropavyavahārasya api anāropita jāti anādare asambhavaḥ eva iti 
ĀTV_394.10–394.15–395.13–395.15	 astu tarhi jāti ādau bādhakāt apoha siddhiḥ iti ced vyavahārasya ananyathā siddhau kva bādhakam anyathā vipakṣe balavat bādhakam upanīyāt anyathā siddhi viśrāntaḥ api svabhāva hetuḥ bādhaka śaṅkayā api upahanyeta tatas bādhaka vyasanam apahāya anugama vyavahṛtiḥ anyathā api upapādyatām na ca etat śakyam gati antara abhāvāt na ca bādhakam api asti tat dhi svarūpataḥ vā syāt jñānataḥ vā syāt svarūpataḥ api anupalambhaḥ vā viruddha dharmma adhyāsaḥ vā 
ĀTV_396.7–396.13	 na prathamaḥ asiddheḥ sphurataḥ eva hi sādhāraṇa ākārasya śarīram cintayitum ārabdham na asphurataḥ adhyakṣe sādhāraṇa sphuraṇam vyāsedhāmaḥ na tu vikalpe tasya samāna saṅketa graha timira nikuramba karambita dṛṣṭibhiḥ eva upapādanāt na tu asmābhiḥ kalpanā koṣasya anantara prasara tayā tattva avyavasthāpaka tvāt iti ced na śabda anusandhāna virahe api jāyamāna tvāt 
ĀTV_397.16–398.5	 tathā api tad vāsanātaḥ eva iti ced kim eka saṅketa viṣaya abhāve api samāna śabda saṅketa graha vāsanā vaśāt eka ākāra parāmarśaḥ tad sadbhāve vā na tāvat ādyaḥ nānā sāsnā adimat vyakti vat svarga locana bāṇa ambu kuliśa ādiṣu api go śabda saṅketa graha vāsanā vaśāt tathāvidha pratyaya anugama prasaṅgāt iṣṭaḥ eva asau arthaḥ iti ced saḥ ayam sāsnādi matīṣu vyaktiṣu sādhāraṇam rūpam na paśyati paśyati tu go śabda vācyeṣu daśasu iti kim atra vaktavyam nūnam ruciḥ eva asya locanam iti 
ĀTV_399.1–399.2–402.5–402.8	 śakyam idam itareṇa api vaktum iti ced śakyam na tu vyavahāraḥ tad mūlaḥ viparyyāsayitum nanu etāvatā api vikalpaḥ siddhyatu anubhavaḥ tu katham sa vastuka vikalpa siddheḥ eva katham tasya sa vastuka tā iti ced śabda vāsanā ādi kāraṇa antara vidhvaṃsāt iti tūṣṇīm bhava antarāle kim iti na upalabhyate iti ced upalabdhi kāraṇa abhāvāt piṇḍe eva kuṇḍe badara vat kutas na upalabhyate iti ced na ananya deśa tvāt bhedena tu upalabhyate eva piṇḍa antara asaṃsargiṇi piṇḍe anubhūyamāne tad saṃsargi tayā anubhavāt 
ĀTV_403.11–403.17	 na api dvitīyam bādhakam avayavi samāna yogakṣema tvāt jāyamāna piṇḍa sambandha anupapattiḥ apratisaṅkamāt tatra asattvāt anutpādāt ca iti ced katham punar tatra asattvam tvayā vyajñāyi tatra sattve tatratyākāśa ādeḥ api go tva prasaṅgāt iti ced na ca etat paścāt api tatrati ākāśa ādinā sambadhyate yena ca piṇḍena sambadhyate na tatra kadāpi tat na asti tat kutas virodhaḥ 
ĀTV_406.3–406.6–408.1–408.6	 atha piṇḍam antargaḍum upādāya upalakṣaṇa tayā tatra iti vyavahāraḥ tadā tad upasarpaṇa apasarpaṇa utpatti vināśaiḥ eva tad upapattau na yāti ityādiḥ aparāt dheṣoḥ iva dhānuṣkasya kaṇṭha ḍambaraḥ tathā hi piṇḍam adhikṛtya upasarpaṇa apasarpaṇa abhāvaḥ tad upalakṣitam deśam adhikṛtya ca sattva asattve sāmānyasya iti kim kena saṅgatam atha api anutpanne piṇḍe tasya asattvam sulabham eva tat asattvāt iti hṛdayam tat na sva rūpa sattva asattvayoḥ dvitīya anapekṣa tvāt sambaddha tva asambaddha tve tu dvitīya apekṣe tatas tatra asati na asti iti kaḥ arthaḥ 
ĀTV_410.1–410.5–411.3–411.10	 tena asatā na sambadhyate iti ced tat ca evam etat paścāt katham sambadhyatām iti ced tasya sattvāt asambaddha tvasya tad asattva prayukta tvāt tatas prāk asan piṇḍaḥ paścāt katham upapadyatām iti ca udyaniṣṭhāḥ sā ca satkāryyavādam anupatati iti amukta vāntiḥ tathā api sāmānya tadvatoḥ atyanta bhede katham sāmānādhikaraṇyam iti ced kim idam samānena adhikaraṇena hi sambandhaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam tasya ca bhedena kaḥ virodhaḥ iti na adhigacchāmaḥ gavāśvayoḥ api tathā abhāva prasaṅgaḥ iti ced nanu vyatireka dṛṣṭānta sthānam tat na tu virodha sthānam tat ca maitra tanayoḥ api yadi kaścid aśyāmaḥ syāt paridṛśyamānānām api tathā abhāva prasaṅgaḥ iti kva nāma durlabham 
ĀTV_412.18–413.3–414.12–414.19	 tathā api viśeṣaḥ vācyaḥ iti ced asti svābhāvikaḥ viśeṣaḥ yat kiñcid eva kenacid sambaddham na sarvvam sarvveṇa iti tathā anugama niyamaḥ api svabhāvāt eva kim na syāt iti ced ekasya aneka sambandhe anekasya ca eka sambandhe avirodhāt eka anekayoḥ aneka eka vyavahāra virodhāt iti na api jñānataḥ bādhakam tad svarūpa pratikṣepasya anubhava bādhita tvāt kāraṇa pratikṣepasya ca janmanā eva apāsta tvāt eka tva pratikṣepasya ca viruddha dharmma adhyāsa viraha pratihata tvāt pārokṣya apārokṣya ādeḥ asiddheḥ viṣayam apratikṣipya tad prāmāṇyasya pratikṣeptum aśakya tvāt tad apratikṣepasya ca darśita tvāt indriya ja tu apratikṣepasya ca indriya anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāna bādhita tvāt sākṣātkāri tva viśrānte ca tad anuvidhānasya avyabhicārāt 
ĀTV_417.12–417.19	 anyathā nirvvikalpakasya api anindriya jatu aprasaṅgāt kāma ātura kāminī jñānasya tad antareṇa api upapatteḥ bādhaka abhāvāt ca darśana vyāpāra aupādhika tva kalpanāna vakāśāt avakāśe vā viparyyaya kalpanāyāḥ api prasaṅgāt indriyam anapekṣya sākṣātkāria samanantara pratyaya mahima mātreṇa sākṣātkāri vikalpa upapattau tad viparīta anutpatti prasaṅgāt prathamam autpatteḥ pūrvvasmaraṇa ādi sahakāri vaidhuryya nibandhana tvāt iti eṣā diś 
ĀTV_421.7–421.12–423.1–423.7	 astu tarhi prayojana anurodhāt apoha svīkāraḥ sarvu adharmma avācya tva siddhiḥ hi paramam prayojanam kalpanā jāla vidhūnanena gambhīra udāra samādhi samadhigamāt iti ced niṣpramāṇakam idam kaḥ śraddhadhyāt pramāṇam ca atra na pratyakṣa anumāne āgamaḥ ca na kiñcid vadati iti tvayā eva grāhitaḥ śiṣyaḥ na ca evam cetanaḥ grāhayitum api śakyate sva vāc virodhasya udbhaṭa tvāt tathā hi śabdasya kasyacid api vastuni māna siddha ābādhā vidhi vyavahṛtiḥ kvacid asti naḥ vā asti eva ced katham iyanti na dūṣaṇā ninā asti eva ced sva vacana pratirodha siddhiḥ iti tava eva viṣaya sañcāra mātreṇa ślokaḥ 
ĀTV_425.1–425.5–426.8–426.10	 na ca ātmakam iva tava api atra mūka tā eva śaraṇam sarvu athā vacana virodhe hi udāsīnasya sā śobhate na ca atra vidhau virodhaḥ kaścid na ca tvam udāsīnaḥ prayojane pravṛtta tvāt tasmāt alam aṅgulī dīpikayā dhvānta dhvaṃsa vidhim anuṣṭhāya iti āgamasya tattva artha parisparśi tva virodhe na svarga apavarga arthinām pravṛttiḥ siddhyati iti prayojanam asmad vicārasya eva param sundaram 
ĀTV_426.14–427.3	 tasmāt śabdaiḥ kim vācyam iti anuyoge kim pratibhāsāt atha adhyavasāyāt yat vā tattvataḥ iti vikalpe vikalpa sthaḥ anya apoḍha ākāraḥ anya apoḍha sva lakṣaṇam na kiñcid iti yat krameṇa pratyuktam tatra prathame samaya viparyyāsaḥ vikalpa ākārasya samayā viṣaya tvāt dvitīye tu pravṛtti viparyyāsaḥ adṛṣṭe niyāmaka abhāvāt tṛtīye svavāc nirodhaḥ asya eva arthasya anena tattvatā vacanāt avacane vā tattvataḥ anuttara tvāt iti upasaṃhāraḥ tat siddham etat na kṣaṇika tvam ātmani bādhakam iti 
ĀTV_429.2–429.6–434.3–434.5	 vijñāna vādini jāgarūke bāhyam eva na asti kutas ātmā iti ced sa tāvat idam pṛṣṭaḥ vyāvaṣṭām kim te grāhya grāhaka bhāgayoḥ paramārtha satoḥ eva abhedaḥ vivakṣitaḥ uta aho abhinna jātīya tvam atha grāhya aṃśasya alīka tvam iti tatra prathame sādhye yaḥ kaścid dhetuḥ upādīyate saha upalambha niyamaḥ vā grāhya tvam vā prakāśamāna tvam vā sa vyaktam ābhāsaḥ tathā hi nīla dhavala ādi paraspara viruddha ākāra nikara avagāhi vijñānam anubhūyate tat idam tasya svavadhāya kṛtyā utthāpanam yadi hi mithas pratyanīka dharmmān ullikhet katham ekam sat tad ātmakam bhavet na ced ullikhet katham tat ākāram nāma sva samvedanasya anullikhita rūpa abhāvāt 
ĀTV_435.9–435.16	 bāhyasya evamvidha viruddha dharmma adhyāsāt bhayam tathā tve api abhede artha kriyā acetana pravṛttīnām saṅkara prasaṅgāt vivecana anupapatti prasaṅgāt ca na tu vijñānasya na hi tasya artha kriyā adhīnam sattvam api tu pratibhāsa mātra adhīnam na api tatra artha kriyā arthinaḥ kācid pravṛttiḥ svarasa vāhi vijñāna pravāha atiriktāyāḥ artha kriyāyāḥ tad arthinaḥ ca abhāvāt vivecana abhāvaḥ ca paramaḥ nirvvāhaḥ sva samvidita rūpa tvāt iti ced 
ĀTV_438.3–438.5–438.14–438.19	 tat kim aṅgaḥ pariṇata śānteḥ āśrama padam iva vijñānam āsādya vyāla nakula ādeḥ iva nīla dhavala ādeḥ śāśvatika virodha tyāgaḥ nibhṛta vairāṇām tad phala tyāgaḥ vā na tāvat prathamaḥ paraspara niṣedha vidhinā antarīyaka vidhi niṣedhayoḥ avirodhe jagati virodha uccheda prasaṅgāt na ca evam astu iti uttare api nirvṛttiḥ katham api ukta rūpa tāyāḥ anivṛtteḥ tāvat mātra śarīra tvāt ca virodhasya tad siddhiḥ eva ca bheda siddhiḥ atas na dvitīyaḥ api 
ĀTV_441.6–441.10–443.9–443.12	 yaḥ tu bāhye virodha paripālanāya viśeṣaḥ darśitaḥ sa teṣām eva astu yadi hi viruddha dharmma adhyāsasya bheda sādhaka tvam prati samāśvāsaḥ kim artha kriyā pratiniyama upanyāsena na ced tathā api kim tena saḥ api hi artha kriyayoḥ viruddha dharmma adhyāsena bhede sati syāt anyat ca yathā bāhye artha kriyā pratiniyamaḥ na syāt iti daṇḍaḥ tathā jñāne api pratibhāsa niyamaḥ na syāt iti daṇḍaḥ eva kva pratibhāsā sāṅkarya niyamaḥ saha eva pratibhāsaḥ api syāt iti ced na saha anupalambham asāṅkaryam brūmaḥ kintu nīlasya eva pīta tvena pītasya eva nīla tvena anupalambham saḥ eva mūlam sarva virodhānām 
ĀTV_444.17–445.4	 anyathā upalambha anupalambhayoḥ api asiddheḥ eva yat api na upalabhyate iti ucyate tat api upalabhyate eva yat idam aśva ādikam upalabhyate tat na upalabhyate iti uktyā eva nirvṛtteḥ tena ātmanā na upalabhyate iti ced tat kim saha upalambhe api nīla ātmanā pītam upalabhyate yatas na virodhaḥ syāt tasmāt ubhau api virodhau samau kṣamau ca abheda visarjane kevalam ekasya prauḍhiḥ subhaga abhikṣuka nyāyena yadi syāt 
ĀTV_447.13–447.14–451.5–451.8	 etena vivecana abhāvaḥ api nirastaḥ ākārayoḥ asambhedena vedanasya eva vivecana tvāt api ca kṣaṇikatāyām eka puruṣa apekṣayā bāhyasya api kutas vivecanam nānā puruṣa apekṣayā api sandigdham pareṇa parasya āvedanāt kva sandehaḥ iti ced abhedena eva tattva vivecanam sādhyam tathā ca kim tena upanyaḥ tena api tad jātīyasya tu bāhya vat vijñānasya api vivecanam eva iti sva samvedana bādhitaḥ ayam viruddha dharmma adhyāsaḥ na bheda sādhakaḥ iti uṣṭralaguḍakam samvedanena eva asya sādhita tvāt
