ĀTV_453.3–453.9–454.14–454.18	 hinaḥ tu tarhi prakāśamānatā aneka tvam viruddha dharmma adhyāsaḥ api eka tām tathā api ekatva aneka tva vikala nīla ādi ākāra prakāśa svarūpe kim āyātam iti ced tat idam bhautaiḥ kṣetra nināyanam niyata ākāra tvam eva hi eka tvam aniyata ākāra tvam ca aneka tā tad nivṛttau ca na nīla ākāram na api nīla pīta ādi ākāram iti anākāram eva avaśiṣyate syāt etat pāramārthikaḥ viruddha dharmma adhyāsaḥ bheda hetuḥ ayam kālpanikaḥ iti ced evam tarhi suta rām ayatna siddham sphaṭika vat bodhasya nirākāra śuddha tvam ākāra nikaraḥ tu anātmā iva sphurati iti ubhayathā eva kāla atyaya apadiṣṭāḥ saha upalambha ādayaḥ 
ĀTV_455.12–456.6	 api ca āstām tāvat viruddha dharmma adhyāsa cintā yaḥ ayam grāhya grāhaka bhāga bhedaḥ grāhya nīla ādi bhedaḥ vā cakāsti sa kim satyaḥ asatyaḥ vā satya tve saḥ eva doṣaḥ astya tve na ayam ātmā vijñānasya iti anātmani api saha upalambha niyamāt ayogya tā iti anekāntāḥ bhedaḥ na prathataḥ eva iti ced evam tarhi astu tāvat sarva janīna pratīti virodhaḥ sva vāc virodhaḥ vā asiddhāḥ tarhi hetuvaḥ na hi bheda aprathane saha artham tat vyāpyatām vā paśyāmaḥ tat asphuraṇe api pakṣa ādi pravibhāgaḥ api katham kam ca bodhayitum pravṛttaḥ asi kim artham ca anvaya vyatireka apratītau kim ca hetoḥ balam kutas ca vipratipattiḥ kīdṛśe ca iti saḥ ayam vicāram ārabhate bhedam tu sāmvṛtam api na icchati nūnam unmattaḥ api anena jitaḥ 
ĀTV_458.1–458.3–459.5–459.13	 vikalpa ārūḍhaḥ eva bhedaḥ vyavahāra aṅgam na anubhava ārūḍhaḥ iti ced saḥ api satyaḥ asatyaḥ vā bhāsate na vā iti vikalpāt na ativartate asan eva asphuran eva adhyavasīyate iti ced adhyavasīyate iti vivaraṇa arham etat tad viṣaya vyavahāra jananam adhyavasāya arthaḥ iti ced vyavahāraḥ api yadi ajñāna rūpaḥ katham asan tena janyatām jñāna rūpaḥ ced katham niyāmakam vinā tad viṣayaḥ sva kāraṇa sāmagrī sāmarthyāt iti ced saḥ ayam vyavahṛti rūpa jñāna alīka bhedayoḥ niyāmaka antara abhāve api kāraṇa sāmarthyam āśritya viṣaya viṣayi bhāvam icchati na tu anubhava anubhāvyayoḥ iti kṣīram vihāya rucira rocakagraḥ tasya sauvīre 
ĀTV_461.17–462.6	 bhedaḥ api vikalpa ākāraḥ eva na tu bāhyaḥ iti ced yadi asan eva asau katham vikalpa ākāraḥ tad ākāraḥ ced katham asan iti paribhāvaya astu tarhi san eva iti ced nanu advaya darśi ced vijñānam katham bheda prathā ākāra dvaya darśi ced katham ekam sat dvaya ātmakam citra ākāram iti ced citram ekam anekam vā iti vikalpa gilitam eva tava paśyataḥ aneka tve kva eka vijñāna tadātmyam vijñānasya api yāvat ākāram aneka tve kva citra ākāra samvedanam sva sva mātram agna tvāt eka tve kva bheda pratītiḥ 
ĀTV_464.11–464.19	 anīladi aneka vyāvṛtti kṛtaḥ aneka tva adhyavasāyaḥ eva iti ced atādātmye katham vyāvṛttīnām ullekhaḥ tādātmye katham aneka tvam eka tve api kva tad kṛtaḥ api bheda adhyavasāyaḥ ullekhaḥ ayam asya vijñānasya yat aneka tvam nāma na punar tattva antaram iti ced sva rūpam asvarūpam vā iti vācyam ādye aneka svarūpam ekam iti kaḥ anyāḥ vadet asusthāt dvitīyaḥ tu iṣyate eva asmābhiḥ kim tu tvayā iṣyatām bhrāntiḥ asau iti ced tasyām api svarūpam asvarūpam vā prakāśeta prakāra antara abhāvāt iti 
ĀTV_467.11–467.18	 syāt etat yathā atat tad tayā parisphurat api na vastu gatyā tat eva tathā tat api atattayā parisphurat api na ātat eva tatas svarūpasya atat tayā prathane api na kācid grāhya lakṣaṇa kṣatiḥ iti ced yadi atat tā api parisphurantī svarūpam eva asya syāt syāt api asya upanyāsasya prastuta upayogaḥ asvarūpasya katham prakāśaḥ iti ced yadi api tathā vakṣyāmaḥ tathā api atattā katham tasya sva rūpam iti itaḥ api dīyatām dṛṣṭiḥ 
ĀTV_469.19–470.8	 kaḥ ca asvarūpa sphuraṇe doṣaḥ na ayam bhinnayoḥ vedya vedaka bhāvaḥ vyāpāra nibandhanaḥ niyatasya tasya abhāvāt na api tad jāti nibandhanaḥ kaścid kañcid pratijñeyaḥ iti vyavasthā anupapatti prasaṅgāt na hi nisarga siddhānām go tva ādīnām īdṛśī rītiḥ iti ced nanu ayam abhede api doṣaḥ tad avasthaḥ eva tathā hi svasya vedanam iti na ayam vyāpāra nibandhanaḥ vyavahāraḥ sva ātmani tad abhāvāt na api jāti nibandhanaḥ sādhāraṇya prasaṅgāt na hi jātyā eva gauḥ sva ātmanam prati na tu param prati iti niyamaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na ca jñānam svasya iva parasya api vedanam sarva sarvajñatva āpatteḥ 
ĀTV_472.13–472.17–475.1–475.3	 na tat kasyacid kim tu vedana mātram iti ced tathā api sva ātmani ajaḍa vat paratra api ajaḍam syāt parasmin andha vat svasmin api andham prasajyeta jātyā eva tad rūpa tvāt jātyā api sva kāraṇāt kvacin iyata rūpam eva tad utpannam iti ced na evam uccais brūyāḥ paraiḥ api kadācid evam śrūyeta abhedaḥ astu mā vā bhedam tu prakāśamāna tvena vyāsedhāmaḥ iti ced na vastuni bheda nivṛtteḥ eva abheda rūpa tvāt 
ĀTV_475.13–475.17–477.14–477.19	 astu tarhi bheda abheda vidhuram eva citram cetaḥ abhede prakāśamāna tva ayogāt abhede citratu anupapatteḥ iti ced na mithas aviruddha vidhi dvaya vidhi vat tad ubhaya niṣedhasya api ekatra viruddha tvāt na ca saḥ api astu iti vācyam syāt vāda avatāre tava api digambara tva prasaṅgāt astu tarhi catur śikharī śūnyam eva citram āścarya rūpa tvāt eka aneka tva virahe api sattvam iti āścarya arthaḥ hi citra śabdaḥ iti ced atha catur śikhara śekharam eva kim na syāt āścarya rūpa tā yukteḥ tulya tvāt ekaika pakṣa anupapatiḥ ca yathā tad niṣedha paryavasāyinī tathā tad itara vidhi paryavasāyinī api syāt iti 
ĀTV_479.12–479.17	 api ca atra vastutas catuṣkoṭi virahe cetasaḥ bhāṣa antareṇa idam uktam yat anātmānaḥ eva etāḥ catasnaḥ koṭiyaḥ bhāsante na vā pratibhānti iti tatra apratibhāsanam anuttaram pratibhāsane tu grāhya lakṣaṇa ayoge api grāhya bhāvaḥ iti citram etat tathā ca citrāt vaitāt varam citra dvaitam astu pratibhāsana anurodhāt iti 
ĀTV_481.1–481.12	 syāt etat bahis antar ubhayathā api grāhya lakṣaṇa kṣatiḥ astu prakāśamāna tvam tu nīla ādīnām aśakya apahravam tāvat mātram ca asmākam abhimatam iti ced tat etat vikrīta gavīra kṣaṇam kim idam prakāśamāna tvam yat sarvathā grāhya lakṣaṇa kṣatau api na kṣīṇam na prakāśa sambandhaḥ niyama anupapatteḥ iti uktam tasmāt nīla ādīnām prakāśamāna tvam paripālayatā grāhya lakṣaṇe yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ pariharttavyam vā prakāśamāna tvam anyathā tapanīyam apanīya vāsasi granthi kartāram upahasasi svayam ca kanakam upādāya gagana añcale granthim karoṣi iti sā iyam sarva prakāram asiddhiḥ sarva prakāram ca anaikāntika tvam iti 
ĀTV_484.17–485.3	 etena dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ pratyuktam na hi sajātīya tvena grāhya lakṣaṇa vaidhuryam utsāryate atiprasaṅgasya tādavasthyāt jaḍa tve prakāśa asambhāvanā eva iti ced na tulya tvāt yathā hi asvasam vedana vādinaḥ param prati prakāśam api jñānam ātmani jaḍam eva tathā sva samvedana vādinaḥ api sva ātmani prakāśam api jñānam param prati jaḍam eva kathañcid budhyantare api ajaḍam ced bāhye api tathā kim na syāt iti sandigdha vipakṣa vṛtti tvam 
ĀTV_486.17–487.3	 nanu bāhye sarvathā eva grāhya lakṣaṇa kṣatiḥ iha tu samāna upāda āna tā niyamena citra ākārāṇām parama artha bhinnānām eva vyativedana siddhiḥ na mithas prathā niyame hi upādāna mukhena sāmānyatas vā sāmagrī sāmarthyam eva vaktavyam anyathā tathāvidha kārya anutpatteḥ tathā ca bāhya grāhya niyata svabhāva jñāna utpattau api sulabham etat iti pūrvakaḥ eva doṣaḥ 
ĀTV_489.5–489.9–490.16–490.18	 astu tarhi tṛtīyaḥ sarvathā grāhya lakṣaṇa anupapatteḥ tad abhāve sāmagrī sāmarthyā api āśrayitum aśakya tvāt vicāra siddhe hi vastuni kāraṇa cintana avasaraḥ na tu avivecitaḥ iti ced kim grāhya lakṣaṇā nirvaktavyatayā prakāśamāna tvam amīṣām nivarttate sattvam vā na prathamaḥ na hi lakṣaṇa aparijñāna mātreṇa spaṣṭa dṛṣṭam api lakṣyam apahnotum śakyate aparijñānasya dūrūha tvena api upapatteḥ teṣām apratibhāse tad niṣedhasya anupapatteḥ 
ĀTV_491.16–491.19–492.11–492.18	 na dvitīyaḥ tadā hi tad lakṣaṇa anupapattiḥ sattvam nivarttayet yadi asattve lakṣaṇam upapadyeta ubhayathā api anupapattau kaḥ anurāgaḥ asattve tat eva lakṣaṇam iti ced sattvam eva kim na syāt atiprasaṅgāt iti ced tulyam vedanā adhīna vyavahāra gocara tvam iti ced astu tāvat idam tasya eva iti tu niyamaḥ kutas sāmagrītaḥ tathā vedanā utpattiḥ iti ced tat etat sambhāvyate sati na tu asatī iti viśeṣaḥ yathā hi sati jñānena abhilāṣaḥ tena yatnaḥ tena pravṛttiḥ tayā tad prāptiḥ kriyate na tathā alīke tasya prāptum aśakya tvāt śakya tve vā analīka tvāt vyavahāraḥ api ayam alīkaḥ iti ced tarhi sutarām lakṣaṇa abhāvaḥ tad dvārasya api abhāvāt 
ĀTV_494.8–494.13	 astu tarhi sarvathā vicāra asaha tvam eva viśvasya iti ced tat kim idānīm tattva upaplavaḥ eva kāṣṭhā śūnyatā vā na prathamaḥ iyatīm bhūmim ārūḍhasya api vicārasya niścala tāyām pramāṇa abhāvāt bhāve vā katham tattva upaplavaḥ asya eva vicārasya anupaplavāt tad samāna nyāyasya anyasya api tathā abhāva prāpteḥ niṣphala tvāt ca 
ĀTV_496.8–496.22	 na hi asya atipravṛttiḥ phalam gagana āsvādanena atṛpteḥ jvālā kalapa āliṅganena tāpa an apanodanāt na api ati nivṛttiḥ jaḍībhāva mātre api upanipāti duḥkha anivṛtteḥ na ca duḥkham api vicāra asaham iti aheyam eva tathāvidhasya vicāre api anadhikārāt na api yathālokam vyavasthitiḥ vicārāt prāk api tasyāḥ pāmara ādi vat ayatna siddhiḥ na api para loka mātrāt nivṛttiḥ tasya aihika tulya tvāt dṛśyate hi tāvat ayam iti ced yadi jñāna vacanaḥ dṛśiḥ tadā aparaḥ api tathā sākṣātkāra vacanaḥ ced iha eva anumāna ādeḥ apravṛtti prasaṅgaḥ tat api pratyakṣam iti ced āmuṣmikam api pratyakṣam eva tathā api kim vicāreṇa tam antareṇa api tasyāḥ sulabha tvāt tām eva ayam puṣṇāti iti ced tulya lakṣaṇa tvāt aruceḥ eva tatra na pravṛttiḥ iti ced aviśeṣāt iha api puṣṇīyāt iti 
ĀTV_499.10–499.17	 saḥ ayam pavana tanaya vārtām upaśrutya tad parddhayā bāla vānaraḥ kiyat api dūram utplutya mahā arṇave patitaḥ prāha apāraḥ eva ayam akūpāraḥ mithyā ramāyaṇam iti tat kim anena evam jñātum nirvaktum vā na śakyate kīdṛśam jagat iti etāvat mātram api pāmaradaśā vat niṣphalam eva na ca niṣphala tve api śraddheyam idam tā= arparāmarśa pāṭava abhāvena api upapatteḥ na hi jāti andhaḥ nīlam jñātum nirvaktum vā na śaktaḥ iti ajñeyānirvācyam eva tat lokaḥ iti 
ĀTV_501.9–501.17	 astu tarhi śūnyatā eva paramam nirvāṇam iti ced na sā hi yadi asiddhāḥ katham tad avaśeṣam api viśvam abhidhīyate vāc mātrasya sarvatra sulabha tvāt paratas ced siddhāḥ paraḥ api abhyupagantavyaḥ grāhya lakṣaṇam ca āvarjanīyam iti sa ca paraḥ yadi saṃvṛtiḥ eva viśva śūnyatayoḥ na kaścid viśeṣaḥ katham tat api avaśiṣyeta asaṃvṛti rūpaḥ ced paraḥ paratas eva tasya siddhau anavasthā svayam asiddhaḥ ced katham śūnya tvam api sādhayet svatas siddhaḥ ced āyātaḥ asi mārgeṇa 
ĀTV_503.15–504.12	 tathā hi svatas siddha tayā tad anubhava rūpam śūnya tvāt eva ca na tasya kāla avacchedaḥ iti nityam atas eva ca na deśa avacchedaḥ iti vyāpakam atas eva tat nirdharmmakam iti vicāra aspṛṣṭam tasya dharmma dharmmi bhāvam upādāya pravṛtteḥ atas eva viśeṣa abhāvaḥ iti advaitam prapañcasya apāram ārthika tvāt ca niṣpratiyogikam iti vidhi rūpam avicārita prapañca apekṣayā tu śūnyam iti vyavahāraḥ tathā api prapañca śūnyasya anubhava mātrasya prapañcena saha kaḥ sambandhaḥ na ca na ayam prakāśate iti ced vastu gatyā na kaścid saṃvṛttyā tu gagana gandharvanagarayoḥ ādhāra ādheya bhāvaḥ iva viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ sa ca yathā naiyāyikaiḥ samarthayiṣyate tathā eva vedya niṣṭhaḥ tu asau asmin darśanaḥ iti viśeṣaḥ avidyā eva hi tathā tathā vivarttate yathā yathā anubhāvyatayā vyavahriyate tad tad māyā upanīta upādhi bhedāt ca anubhūtiḥ api bhinnā iva vyavahāra patham avatarati gaganam iva svapna dṛṣṭa ghaṭa kaṭāha koṭara kuṭī koṭibhiḥ tadā āstām tāvat kim ārdraka vaṇijaḥ vahitra cintayā 
ĀTV_508.1–508.8	 tasmāt anubhava vyavasthitau anātmā api sphurati iti avarjanīyam etat tad siddhau tad lakṣaṇam api kiñcid asti eva tat ca bāhya avirodhe jñāna anitya tāyām tad niṣṭham ubhaya niṣṭham vā bāhya virodhe jñāna niṣṭham eva tat nitya tāyām tu grāhya niṣṭham eva iti tathā hi lakṣyaḥ tāvat atra viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ sa ca prakāśasya sataḥ tadīyatā mātra rūpaḥ svabhāva viśeṣaḥ svabhāva tvāt eva ca na upakāra antaram apekṣate tad mātrīya tvāt eva ca na anyadīyaḥ 
ĀTV_517.5–517.16	 kim asya phalam iti praśna prasaṅge api bahis tad gocara vyavahāra pravṛttiḥ āntaram api tena jñāna nirūpaṇam kutas ayam īdṛś iti anuyoge api sāmagrī śaktiḥ eva uttaram kārya kāraṇa vat anyathā tatra api upakāra antara apekṣāyām anavasthā tad anapekṣāyām vā sādhāraṇyam kena vāryam tena tat eva kriyate anena api etat eva viṣayīkriyate iti vivecanīyam viṣayīkriyate iti kaḥ arthaḥ kriyate iti api kaḥ arthaḥ iti vicāraṇīyam kārya utpādanam eva karaṇam tadīyatayā utpattiḥ eva viṣayīkaraṇam iti vivecanīyam upakāraḥ tu yathā atra vijñāna svarūpa atiriktaḥ na asti tathā atra api kārya svarūpa atiriktaḥ na asti iti pratisandheyam iti 
ĀTV_519.7–519.12	 atas eva kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ api upekṣitavyaḥ iti tu mahat sāhasam tathā sati hi syāt eva na syāt eva iti ādyāpadyeta tathā ca prakāśa tamasoḥ anyatarasya kauṭasthya prasaṅgaḥ sāṃvṛtaḥ astu iti ced viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ api evam astu yadi viṣaya kāryayoḥ balavatī bādhā iti sāṃvṛtaḥ noced evam iti dvayī gatiḥ 
ĀTV_522.1–522.8	 tat atra tattvam na tāvat ubhaya niṣṭham lakṣaṇam staḥ asataḥ vā sthirasya api sphuraṇāt na ca jñāna nityatāyām pāramārthika bāhya niṣṭham satkārya vāda vyāvṛtteḥ sāṅkhya prakriyā vidhvaṃsāt na khalu pūrvva apara tirobhau= a āvirbhāvau antareṇa vicārasya api avasaraḥ na api alīka grāhya tayā kṣaṇika jñāna niṣṭham iti tucchasya viśeṣa abhāvāt jñānasya ca nirākāra tvāt anyatra api asiddheḥ āropayitum aśakya tvāt 
ĀTV_524.12–524.19–526.1–526.3	 asantaḥ eva viśeṣakāḥ cakāsati iti ced na asantaḥ iti hi atad kālāḥ atad deśāḥ iti vai akiñcit rūpāḥ iti vā niyata vyāvṛtti mātra rūpāḥ iti vā prathame kāla deśa antarayoḥ sattva prasaṅgaḥ dvitīye tu aviśeṣa tā tṛtīye nīlasya alīkasya ānīla vyāvṛtti rūpa tāyām anīlānām pāramārthika tva prasaṅgaḥ teṣām alīka tve tad vyāvṛtti ātmanaḥ nīlasya analīka tva pattiḥ tathā api alīka tve aviśeṣa tvam tena rūpeṇa aviśeṣa tvam eva iti ced atha viśeṣaḥ kena nīla pīta ādinā iti ced tat kim tatas adhikam analīkam tarhi syāt anadhikam ced kutas tena api iti 
ĀTV_526.18–527.9–529.1–529.5	 vāsanā vaśāt viśeṣāḥ sphuranti iti ced sphurantu kaḥ kāraṇe vipratipadyate te tu nīla ādayaḥ yadi akiñcit rūpāḥ katham viśeṣāḥ tad itara rūpeṇa akiñcit rūpa tve tena rūpeṇa kiñcid rūpāḥ eva iti brūmaḥ vicārāsa hatā mātram alīka tvam iti ced tathā api bhāṣā parivarttana mātram vicāra asahatāyāḥ kiñcid rūpa tva virodhi tvāt avirodhe vā tvad vicāra asahanāḥ api kiñcid rūpāḥ eva nīla ādayaḥ iti vicārasya durvicāra tva prasaṅgaḥ tena nīla ādīnām chāyā mātrasya api anākrānteḥ praviśa vā anirvacanīya khyāti kukṣim tiṣṭha vā mati kart damam apahāya nyāyanayā anusāreṇa nīla ādīnām pāramārthika tve tasmāt na grāhya bhedam avadhūya dhiyaḥ asti vṛttiḥ tad bādhane balini veda naye jaya śrīḥ no ced anindyam idam īdṛśam eva viśvaṃtathyam tathāgatam atasya tu kaḥ avakāśaḥ 
ĀTV_530.8–531.6	 tatra alīkam vicāra asaham anirvacanīyam vā yam āśritya jagat udgīyate saḥ eva vicāraḥ cintyatām kaḥ asau kīdṛśaḥ ca iti sa tarkam pramāṇam eva vākya ārūḍham iti ced tat ced vicāra asaham kim tena bhauta vicāra kalpena tathā hi kenacid bhautena rāja dvāri dviradam avalokya vikalpitam kim ayam andhakāraḥ mūlakam atti āhosvit jalavāhaḥ balākān varṣati garjati ca yat vā bāndhavaḥ ayam rājadvāre śmaśāne ca yaḥ tiṣṭhati sa bāndhavaḥ iti parama ācārya vacanāt atha vā yaḥ ayam bhūmau dṛśyate tasya chāyā iti dūṣitan ca tatra na ādyaḥ śūrpa yugala prasphoṭana anupapatteḥ na dvitīyaḥ tasya stambha catuṣṭaya abhāvāt na tṛtīyaḥ tasya laguḍa bhrāmaṇa abhāvāt na caturthaḥ tasya nara śiraḥ śata udgiraṇa abhāvāt tatas na kiñcid idam iti kim etāvatā dvirada svarūpam nivartatām yat vā varam etasmāt yaḥ ayam saḥ ayam iti vādī dvitīyaḥ bhautaḥ tad vicāra saham iti ced evam tarhi svayam eva vilīnam alīka ādi vādaiḥ na uttara pratīkṣaṇam api 
ĀTV_533.1–533.12	 loka siddham iti ced tarhi tasya parikara śuddhiḥ api tathā eva grāhyā anyathā lokasya api vyatikrame vicārasya yādṛcchika vāc mātrava āpatteḥ loke ca ākāṅkṣa ayogya tā sattimattayā pratisaṃhitam aśliṣṭa artham pramāṇa antara apratihatam sva vacana sva kriyāsu ajñāna vyāghāta ādi doṣa rahitam sva artha pratikṣepaka yukteḥ anākṣepakam vākyam artha pratipatteḥ aṅgam yathā pūrvatas ayam vahnimān iti anaṅgam itarat yathā ayam pūrvatas gauraḥ iti jaladradaḥ vahnimān iti giriḥ devadattena bhuktam agnimān iti śvetaḥ ḍitthaḥ dhāvati iti śaśaḥ viṣāṇi iti mātā vandhyā iti aham mūkaḥ iti imam na jānām iti mama karṇe praviśya gajaḥ garjati bheṣajam ucyatām iti 
ĀTV_537.19–538.16^1	 tad arthaḥ ca sādhanam dūṣaṇam ca tatra sādhanam vyāpti pakṣa dharma taupayika rūpa pañcaka upetam liṅgam yathā viśiṣṭa dhūmavat tvāt iti liṅga ābhāsam itarat yathā jalāśaya tvāt iti tad parikaraḥ ca tarkaḥ saḥ api vyāpti balam ālambya aniṣṭa prasaṅga rūpaḥ aniṣṭam ca dvividham prāmāṇika parityāgaḥ aprāmāṇika parigrahaḥ ca yathā yat udakam pipāsā duḥkham na śamayet na pīyet yadi ca tat eva param antar t dahet tadā aciśiṣṭam mām api dahet itaraḥ tu tarka ābhāsaḥ 
ĀTV_537.19–538.16^2	 yathā yadi jalam pipāsā duḥkham na aśamayiṣyat rūpavat api na abhaviṣyat yathā ākāśam yadi ca tat eva param antara dhakṣyat mām api surabhim akariṣyat iti dūṣaṇam api sva pratikṣepaka yukteḥ anākṣepakam dūṣya asādhaka tva avinābhūtam siddham ca yathā agnimat tve sādhye prameya tvam anaikāntika tvāt ahetuḥ iti anyathā tu tad ābhāse yathā ayam dhūmaḥ na agni sādhakaḥ sarvathā anupalabhyamāna upādhi śaṅkā grasta tvāt prameya tvāt viruddha tvāt ca iti itarat api pramāṇam anumāna= chāyayā eva vicāra aṅgam tarkam ananyathā siddhim ca puraskṛtya pravṛtteḥ tatas tatra api eṣā eva rītiḥ anugantavyā iti 
ĀTV_541.1–541.8	 evam vyavasthite loka vyavahāre sādhana upakrameṇa yadi vicārayasi pratijñā eva tāvat na aṅgam dhārayati tathā hi na kiñcid asti na kiñcid satyam na kiñcitkārakam na kiñcid vicāra saham na kiñcid sā ālambanam na kiñcid darśanam na kaścid siddhāntaḥ iti ādau sva artha pratikṣepaḥ tāvat duruddharaḥ pratijñā api hi na syāt na satyā na kārikā na vicāra sahāḥ tad vijñānam api na sa ālambanam tad phalam api na darśanam tad arthaḥ api na siddhāntaḥ iti āpadyeta 
ĀTV_542.8–542.13	 iṣyate eva idam iti ced na icchā mātreṇa vyāghāta anivṛtteḥ yadi hi na jñātam kiñcid asti ityādi pratijñā arthaḥ pratijñām spṛśet katham ayam arthaḥ pratyetavyaḥ na ced katham sa anupapannā tad anupapanna tve ca katham punar pratijñā arthaḥ upapadyate tat idam āyātam sva viṣa mūrcchitā bhujaṅgī ātmānam eva daśati iti 
ĀTV_543.11–543.17	 tattvataḥ iti viśeṣaṇāt ayam adoṣaḥ iti ced tad vicāraḥ vā syāt loka maryādā atikramaḥ vā prathamaḥ pūrvam eva nirastaḥ tasya pratijñā rūpatayā kulīrasya iva sva prasūta yukti apatyena eva pratihata tvāt dvitīye tu sva= chāyā atikrama vat saḥ eva vyāghātaḥ yadi hi loka maryādā atikramaḥ na vicāra svarūpa sthitiḥ tad svarūpa sthitiḥ ced na tad atikramaḥ iti arthaḥ 
ĀTV_544.17–545.9	 pratiṣedhya siddhi asiddhi vyāghātaḥ ca yadi hi pratiṣedhyam siddham na atyantāya pratiṣedhaḥ na ced n atarām loka vyavahāra siddham iti ced siddham eva hi tarhi na hi anyatas api kiñcid siddhyati na ayam abādhyaḥ vyavahāraḥ iti ced na yadi na ekatra anyatra api tathā abhāva prasaṅgāt sarvatra bādhyate iti ced tad apekṣa siddhinā vyavahāreṇa anapekṣeṇa vā avyavahāreṇa eva vā iti yaḥ tāvat tad apekṣa siddhiḥ sa katham tam eva bādheta na hi anuṣṇa tva anumānena uṣṇa tva grāhi pratyakṣa bādhaḥ loke dvitīyaḥ tu asambhavī na hi niṣedhakam pramāṇam niṣedhya siddhi nirapekṣam bhavitum kṣamate tṛtīye tu tad viparīta āpattiḥ vicāra bādhya tvam upakramya avicāreṇa mudraṇāt 
ĀTV_547.14–547.17–548.12–548.20	 na ca etat api nirvyūḍham sa hi ayatna siddham adhyakṣam vā syāt aniṣṭi mātram vā ādye virodhaḥ asiddhiḥ ca dvitīye loka atikramaḥ para aniṣṭyā tvad aniṣṭi bādha prasaṅgaḥ ca iti etena hetavaḥ nirastāḥ te hi jñeya tvāt jñāva tvāt asattvāt vikalpa anupapatteḥ pratyaya tvāt karma anupapatteḥ mithas vyāghātāt ityādayaḥ ete hi sarve eva sva artha kriyā pratikṣepikām yuktim ākṣipanti niṣedhya siddhin ca apekṣante anaikāntikau ca prathama dvitīyau sva phalaḥ eva vyabhicārāt asiddhau tṛtīya caturthau anaikāntikaḥ ca pañcamaḥ pūrvavat asiddhau vyāghātena anaikāntikaḥ ca ṣaṭhaḥ asiddhaḥ anaikāntikaḥ ca saptamaḥ sarve eva kāla atyaya apadiṣṭāḥ iti 
ĀTV_552.4–552.18	 etena dṛṣṭāntāḥ api visarjanīyāḥ te hi rajju sarpa vat tat jñāna vat śaśa viṣāṇa vat darpaṇa mukha vat svapna pratyaya vat chedya anupapattau chidāvat mithas śoṣaka nirvāpaka anala salila vat ityādayaḥ yena ca tatra sarpasya asattvam tat jñānasya mithyātvam śaśa viṣāṇasya ākāraka tvam darpaṇa mukhasya vicāra asaha tvam svapna jñānasya nirālambana tvam chedya anupapattau chidā anupapattiḥ ca avadhāritāni tena eva tatra rajjoḥ sattvam asarpa jñānasya satya tvam śaśasya anyatra gavā ādeḥ viṣāṇaḥ eva kāraka tvam darpaṇasya vicāra saha tvam asvapna jñānasya sa ālambana tvam chedya niṣṭhā chidā siddhau jñānam karma ca upapāditāni tad anupapattau vā sādhya vikala tayā sarve eva ete dṛṣṭānta ābhāsāḥ antim astu sādhana vikalaḥ siddhāntānām vyāghātaḥ paraspara viraha rūpa tva lakṣaṇaḥ jala analayoḥ tu vadhya ghātaka svabhāva tva lakṣaṇaḥ na ca śabda sāmyena anumānam iti eṣā diś 
ĀTV_553.11–553.19	 astu tarhi dūṣaṇa upakrameṇa vicāraḥ iti ced tam api paśyāmaḥ kīdṛśaḥ asau iti na idam sthūlam viruddha dharmmā saṃsarga prasaṅgāt na asthūlam tathā pratibhāsa prasaṅgāt na para anapekṣam sadātana tva prasaṅgāt na ca vyāpakam niṣkriya tva prasaṅgāt na avyāpakam avidheya tva prasaṅgāt ityādiḥ iti ced na mithas avirodha mūla śaithilya iṣṭa āpādana anukūla tva viparyaya aparyavasānaiḥ tarka ābhāsa tvāt 
ĀTV_557.16–557.20–558.13–558.14	 yathā hi na ayam parvataḥ niragniḥ nirdhūma tva prasaṅgāt na api agnimān tathā upalabdhi prasaṅgāt iti anayoḥ ekaḥ ābhāsaḥ paraspara artha pratikṣepakayoḥ ubhayoḥ anābhāsatva anupapatteḥ tathā atra api na hi asthūlatā ādi niṣedhāt anyaḥ sthūla tā ādi vidhiḥ tad niṣedhāt vā anyaḥ asthūla tā ādi vidhiḥ iti śithila mūlāḥ ca ete pratibandhasya asiddheḥ siddhau vā vyāpya vyāpaka tad adhikaraṇānām siddhau vivāda niṛtteḥ iṣṭa āpādanam ca prathame anubhūtauvasite sthūle viruddha dharma asaṃsargasya iṣṭa tvāt tathā ca vakṣyāmaḥ 
ĀTV_559.4–559.13	 anukūlaḥ ca dvitīyaḥ asthūla tā pratikṣepasya sthūlatā upalambha anugrāhaka tvāt tad rūpa tā vyavahārasya tathā pratibhāsa vya āpta tvāt ca evam tṛtīyaḥ api anapekṣa tva pratikṣepasya sa apekṣa tva upalambha anugrāhaka tvāt anapekṣava vidheḥ sadātana tva vyāpta tvāt ca caturthaḥ tu aprasiddha vyāpakaḥ sat asat tvasya virodhena ekatra vidhivat niṣedhasya api anupapattaḥ pañcamaḥ tu anukūlaḥ eva anekatva abhimate vastuni akata apratikṣepasya anekatā upalambha upaṣṭambha katāt tādrūpya vyavahārasya tathā pratibhāsa vya āpta tvāt ca iti ṣaṣṭhaḥ tu iṣṭaḥ eva asmākam 
ĀTV_561.7–561.12	 nanu bhedaḥ svarūpam vā syāt itaretarābhāvaḥ vā dharma antaram vā na pūrvaḥ ghaṭaḥ bhinnaḥ iti saha prayoga anupapatteḥ na aparaḥ pratītau= ātma āśraya prasaṅgāt bhinna pratiyogi nirūpaṇāt dhi tad abhāvaḥ nirūpyaḥ tad nirūpaṇam eva ca bheda nirūpaṇam na uttaraḥ anavasthā prasaṅgāt tat katham asau vyavatiṣṭhatām iti ced 
ĀTV_563.4–563.13–564.11–564.15	 tat kim bheda jñānam eva na asti sat api vā nityam anityam api vā nirhetukam sa hetukam api vā nirviṣayakam sa viṣayakam api vā bādhyamāna viṣayakam iti tatra prathamaḥ sarvatas virodhāt anuttaraḥ dvitīyaḥ suṣupti avasthā anurodhāt upekṣaṇīyaḥ tṛtīyaḥ api virodhāt dheyaḥ caturthaḥ tu bheda ullekhāt eva tyājyaḥ pañcamaḥ tu cintyate kim eteṣu anyatam ātmā tasya viṣayaḥ tad anyaḥ vā iti tatra yadi anyaḥ eva kim etabhiḥ vyadhikaraṇa anupapattibhiḥ tasya bādhyeta evam hi caura apaprādhena vyaktam ayam māṇḍasya nigrahaḥ syāt atha anyatam ātmā tatra api yadi dharma antaram eva iti tattvam tadā anavasthā abhiyā tad adhikaḥ eva pravāhaḥ tyajyatām tasya kutas tyāgaḥ na hi anavasthā pratibhāsamānam artham nivarttayati kintu pravāham parihāpayati gandhe gandha antara vat 
ĀTV_565.12–566.5	 atha itaretarābhāvam eva bheda jñānam avalambate iti tattvam tatra api kva ātma āśrayaḥ tena hi bheda jñānam eva na syāt asti ca tat tatas hetu antaram ākṣipet na tu sva ātmani svayam ahetu tve svayam eva nivartate abidyā vaśāt iti ced kiñca atas na hi avidyā iti eva ātma āśraya nivṛttiḥ tathā sati ghaṭa ādayaḥ api kulāla ādi nirapekṣāḥ svayam eva bhaveyuḥ atha ātma āśraya doṣa upahata tayā tat na svasya eva kāraṇam tatas yatas kutas cit tasya janma tat ca durnirūpam atas avidyā iti ucyate iti vicāra arthaḥ nāmni tarhi vivādaḥ na ca tat api durnirūpam pratiyogi rūpa tvena apratītau adhikaraṇa pratītiḥ adhikaraṇa svabhāva tvena asmṛtau pratiyogi smṛtiḥ ca itaretarābhāva grahaṇa kāraṇam iti nirūpaṇāt 
ĀTV_568.11–568.17	 atha svarūpam eva bheda pratibhāsaya viṣayaḥ iti tattvam tathā api saha prayogaḥ eva anupapannaḥ tyajyatām bhedena tu kim aparāddham saḥ api dṛśyate iti ced naimittikaḥ tu syāt na svarūpataḥ na hi ghaṭam ānaya paṭam avalokayā ityādau bheda padam api prekṣau anupādatte vyākhyāyām tu mūḍha prabodhanāya ghaṭaḥ kumbhaḥ iti vat saha prayoge api na doṣaḥ 
ĀTV_569.6–569.16	 tathā api kaḥ parama arthaḥ yathāyatham trayam api paṭasya hi ghaṭa ātmanā apratītiḥ aghaṭa ātmanā ca pratītiḥ tatas vaiśiṣṭya pratītiḥ ca iti anubhava siddham tatra abhāvasya prathama mātram abhāva antara dharma antarayoḥ abhāvāt dravya ādiṣu triṣu trayam trayasya api sambhavāt bhavati paṭaḥ ayam na ghaṭaḥ tantum ayaḥ ca iti gandhaḥ ayam na rūpam surabhiḥ ca iti gatiḥ iyam na utkṣepaṇam tiryak ca iti lakṣaṇam ca svarūpa bhedasya tādrūpyeṇa apratītau pratītiḥ itaretarābhāvasya tu abādhitaḥ samāna adhikaraṇaḥ niṣedha pratyayaḥ vaidharmyasya tu virodhaḥ sa ca eka dharmya samāveśaḥ iti eṣā diś 
ĀTV_582.18–582.20–583.4–583.9	 saptamaḥ api anukūlaḥ eva ghaṭa ādau vyāpaka tā pratikṣepasya avyāpaka tā upalambha upaṣṭambhaka tvāt vyāpaka tvasya niṣkriya tva vyāpta tvāt ca aṣṭam astu kvacid iṣṭaḥ eva yatas eva hi kvacid avidheyaḥ atas eva kvacid vidheyaḥ avyāpakaḥ iti vyavahriyate sarvatra iti ced na vyapti asiddheḥ virodhāt ca na hi yat avyāpakam tat sarvatra avidheyam iti pratibandhaḥ kvacid asti iti avyāpaka arthaḥ sarvatra na asti iti ca avidheya arthaḥ tava abhimataḥ tad anayoḥ virodhaḥ api syāt 
ĀTV_584.20–585.6–586.11–586.12	 yat viṣaya svabhāvam tat katham pratiṣedhyam iti ced na pratiṣedha svabhāva tā hi vidheyasya viruddhāḥ na tu pratiṣedha pratiyogitā api atha yaḥ asti katham tasya pratiṣedhaḥ api asti iti ce kaḥ doṣaḥ anayoḥ avirodha prasaṅgaḥ iti ced prakāra bhedena prasaṅgaḥ api na doṣam āvahati tad abhedena tu vidhi niṣedhau kena svīkṛtau yam pratyavirodhaḥ prasajyeta iti etena kāla bheda ādinā api avirodhaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ astu tarhi sthūla ghātī viruddha dharma adhyāsaḥ grahaṇa agrahaṇa ādiḥ pañcavidhaḥ na asiddheḥ 
ĀTV_587.3–587.10–588.3–588.7	 tathā hi yaḥ yena yatra eva yadā eva upalabhyate sa tena tatra eva tadā eva na upalabhyate iti na anubhavaḥ na api abhyupagamaḥ eka avayava sahitasya upalambhaḥ anya avayava sahitasya anupalambhaḥ iti ced evam tarhi avayavini upalabhyamāne kaścid avayavaḥ upabhyate kaścid na iti vākya arthaḥ sa viśeṣaṇe hi vidhi niṣedhau viśeṣaṇam upasaṅkrāmate iti nyāyāt tathā ca avayavānām upalambha anupalambhau avayavini sañcārya prasaṅgaḥ tad alam anena etena āvṛta tva anāvṛta tvam vyākhyātam anāvaraṇa daśā vat katipaya avayavāraṇe api tathāvidha sthailya upalambhaḥ kim na syāt iti tu avaśiṣyate tat api asat tasya parimāṇa gata sāmānya viśeṣasya tatas anyasya niyata sāmagrī vedyasya tad abhāve tad upalambhe api anupalambhāt 
ĀTV_589.10–589.19	 etena kampā kampa saṃsargaḥ nirastaḥ sāmagrī bhedena avayava niyata kampa utpāde tasyām daśāyām avayavinaḥ niścala tvāt evam tarhi kampā kampayoḥ avayavayoḥ vibhāgāt saṃyoga nāśe dravya nāśaḥ syāt iti ced tatas kim apasiddhāntaḥ iti ced na evam api kvacid abhyupagamāt sarvatra evam prasaṅgaḥ iti ced tathā api avayavinaḥ kim atyāhitam na ca evam api karmaṇaḥ dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga pratidvandi vibhāga janana niyama anabhyupagamāt kāraṇa viśeṣāt kasya cit eva karmaṇaḥ tathābhūta viśeṣa upalabdheḥ 
ĀTV_592.11–593.6	 etena pāṇau calati tad mūla bhūtaḥ paramāṇuḥ api calet tatas acalat tad bhuja paramāṇoḥ vibhāgaḥ tatas yaḥ yena saṃyujyate vibhajyate vā sa tad kārya dravyeṇa api iti nyāyena bhuja pāṇyoḥ api vibhāgaḥ tatas saṃyoga nāśaḥ tatas śarīra nāśaḥ iti nirastam na hi pāṇi paramāṇu kriyā bhuja paramāṇu vibhāgam ārabhate niyamena tad anārambhaka tve karma lakṣaṇa kṣatiḥ iti ced na ākāśa ādi deśa vibhāga jananāt api tad upapatteḥ nudya karma vat kutas ayam viśeṣa yadi avayava kampe api akampaḥ eva avayavī hanta avayava saṃyogi vibhāgibhyām ākāśa ādi deśābhyām na saṃyujyeta na vibhajyeta iti ced na avayava saṃyoga vibhāgābhyām eva tad siddheḥ etat ca samyak avaboddhum vaiśeṣikam anusandheyam tarhi calat avayava samāśritaḥ api acalan eva avaya vi upalabhyeta iti ced na idam aniṣṭam pāṇau kampamāne śarīram na kampate iti pratyayāt 
ĀTV_595.10–596.3	 athavā yaḥ yat āśrita tayā upalabhyate sa tasmin calati acalaḥ api cala eva vibhāvyate darpaṇa mukha vat jala candra vat ca iti api draṣṭavyam kṛtam pratīti kalahena evam api sarvatra calaḥ eva upalabhyeta iti ced calati avayave sarvatra tathā eva iti na kiñcid anupapannam acale tu katham tathā upalabhyatām tathā api cala acala āśrayasya calācala tayā pratītau cala acala jala candra vat dvaita pratyayaḥ api syāt iti ced syāt api yadi āśraya vicchedaḥ syāt na hi ekasmin eva jale avicchinna avayava bhedena dvicandra bhramaḥ nāma kintu saḥ eva ekaḥ cale calaḥ upalabhyate acale tu acalaḥ iti vīciṣu saḥ api sahasri nimaḥ iti ced evam etat na āsām vicchedena akalanāt 
ĀTV_598.1–598.9	 astu tarhi cala acalayoḥ yuta siddhi prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na svayam pratibandha asiddheḥ na ca prasaṅge vyāptau api para abhyupagamaḥ śaraṇam na ca evam para abhyupagamaḥ api vastra udaka ādau dṛśyate tāvat ayam iti ced na tantu vastra ādau viparyayasya api darśanāt idam mithyā iti ced tat katham satyam abādhāt iti ced iha tarhi bādhaka antaram vācyam cala acala tvam eva iti ced na yuta siddhau api kim iti na idam bādhakam iti viparyayasya api vaktum śakya tvāt iti 
ĀTV_600.11–600.19	 rakta ārakta virodhaḥ iti ced na bhrānta tvāt tad mūla rāgi dravya saṃyoga asaṃyoga virodhaḥ astu iti ced na paramāṇu vādinam prati prāk eva parihṛta tvāt itaram prati kā vārttā iti ced sā eva tāvat tathā eva avirodhāt prakāra bhedena api virodha abhyupagame vyāpteḥ asiddheḥ saṃyoga tadabhāvayoḥ eva asiddheḥ siddhau vā prakāra bheda aviruddha svābhāva sādeśya aparityāgāt na ca evam padārtha antara vaidharmyeṇa saṃyogaḥ eva nirākarttavyaḥ tad vaidharmyeṇa teṣām eva nirākaraṇa prasaṅgāt 
ĀTV_602.17–603.5	 na ca evam eva nyāyyam niyamavatā hi satya vaidharmyeṇa itaran nirākriyate asatya vaidharmyeṇa satya tvasya eva nirvāhāt niṣedhya pratītinā antarīyaka tvāt ca niṣedha siddheḥ śaśa viṣāṇa ādau kalpitena niṣedhyena niṣedha siddhiḥ iti ced na nirākṛta tvāt saṃyogasya vāc mātreṇa kālpanika tva siddhau atiprasaṅgāt ca śaśaśṛṇga nyāyasya ca yogyā anupalambha abhāvena asiddheḥ itas eva bādhakāt tad siddhau itaretara āśraya tvam 
ĀTV_604.18–605.9	 śabda pratyabhijñāna vat saṃyoga pratīteḥ anyathā upapatti mātreṇa bādha kara vṛttiḥ iti ced na anubhavasya tad anurūpam upādhi mukha piṇḍam adatvā bhrānta tvena anyathā upapattau tad viparīta anumāna pravarttate agnau anuṣṇa tva anumāne pravṛtti prasaṅgāt na ca pratyabhijñānasya sāmānya vat saṃyoga pratyayasya tad anurūpam upādhi antaram asti evambhūtam aryādā atikrame tu tvad abhipreta pratibandha pratyayasya api bhrānta tvena anyathā siddhi prasaṅgaḥ katham vāryaḥ tad avāraṇe śithila mūlaḥ tarkaḥ katham pravartteta yathā loka vyavasthānām ca adhyakṣa antara vat saṃyogasya api śabda pāka ja ādi artha kriyā sthiteḥ tad adhyakṣasya api prāmāṇya siddheḥ na bhrānta tva śaṅkā avakāśaḥ iti 
ĀTV_607.14–608.3	 astu tarhi tad deśa tvāt atad deśa tva rūpaḥ virodhaḥ na virodha lakṣaṇa abhāvāt na hi tad deśa saṃsarga vidhau niyamena deśa antara saṃsarga niṣedhaḥ tad deśa tva tada deśa tvayoḥ tu syāt tad saṃsargaḥ tu kena iṣyate adhyakṣam eva eka saṃsarga paricchedakam tad abhāva vyavaccheda mukhena tad anya vyavaccheda phalam imam virodham udgirati iti ced syāt api evam yadi niyamena eka saṃsṛṣṭasya anya saṃsargam pratikṣipat adhyakṣam udiyāt na tu etat asti yugapad ekasya aneka saṃsarga pravṛttam adhyakṣam aviśeṣāt sarva saṃsargam vā pratikṣipet na vā kam api sva ātmānam eva vā sarvathā na virodham dīpayet antatas paramāṇoḥ api ekasya anekaiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ saṃsarga svīkārāt ca iti 
ĀTV_609.18–609.19–611.1–611.7	 etena vṛtti vikalpaḥ nirastaḥ parama aṇu vṛttyā avavaya vi vṛtteḥ tulya yogakṣema tvāt astu tarhi citre nīla ānīla ādi virodhaḥ na hi tat ekam rūpam citra tva virodhāt na api anekam eka avayavi samavāya virodhāt na ca anekam vyāpakam tathā anupalambha virodhāt na ca avyāpkam svābhāva videśa jātīya tva virodhāt anyathā virodha avirodha vyavasthā virodhāt na ca arūpaḥ eva avayavī cākṣuṣa tva virodhāt iti ced na 
ĀTV_612.14–613.8	 citra tvam hi nānātvam vā mithas viruddha nānā jāti samavāyam vā abhipretya yadi eka tva abhyupagame virodhaḥ udbhāvyate tadā evam etat na tu tathā abhyupagamaḥ na khalu aneka tvam citra tvam śukleṣu api anekeṣu citra pratyaya prasaṅgāt na api ekasmin viruddha aneka jāti samavāyaḥ virodhena eva nirākṛta tvāt api tu nīlatva ādi vat citra tvam api jāti viśeṣaḥ eva sa ca avayava vṛtti vijātīya rūpa samāhāra abhivyaṅgya tvāt na eka rūpa avayava sahitasya avayavinaḥ upalambhe api upalabhyate atas eva tri aṇuke citre api citra pratyayaḥ na kadāpi tathā api acitre pārśve citra pratyayaḥ mā bhūt dhavala pratyayaḥ tu kutas iti ced avayava rūpa sañcāreṇa avayavinaḥ api tathā pratyayāt atas eva yatra avayava rūpam na pratyakṣam tatra trasareṇa a etat api na asti dṛśyam eva hi āloka rūpam āropya piñjarasvasa reṇuḥ ālokyate 
ĀTV_615.16–616.5	 syāt etat yadi citra tvam nāma jāti viśeṣaḥ katham tarhi viruddha jātīya rūpa samāhāra mātre citra tva pratyayaḥ iti ced na vai nīla dhavala aruṇeṣu paṭeṣu kvacid api kārbura arthaḥ citra pratyayaḥ kasya api vaidharmya nimittaḥ tu kena vāryate citra śabdasya akṣāt pada vat aneka artha tvāt nīla pīta ādiṣu mithas saṃsṛṣṭeṣu anārabdha dravyeṣu api karbura pratyayaḥ bhavati iti ced satyam dravya antara utpāda abhimānāt sthailya atiśaya pratyaya vat upapatteḥ iti 
ĀTV_617.5–617.11	 astu tarhi paramāṇu nivṛtteḥ sarva vilopaḥ tathā hi bahubhiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ saṃsṛjyamānaḥ paramāṇuḥ pratyekam kim eka deśena saṃyujyate kārtsnyena vā prakāra antara abhāvāt na prathamaḥ tasya eka deśa abhāvāt bhāve vā parama aṇu tva vyāghātāt na dvitīyaḥ paramāṇu antareṇa asaṃsarga prasaṅgāt na hi asti sambhavaḥ ekatra eva parisamāpta vṛttiḥ anyatra api varttate iti 
ĀTV_618.1–618.13	 na buddhyā samāna yogakṣema tvāt tathā hi buddhiḥ api santam asantam vā aneka viṣayam ālambamānāḥ ākāram vā bibhratī kārtsnyena vai eka deśena vā na prathamaḥ pīta ādi viṣaya ākāra vilopa prasaṅgāt na hi asti sambhavaḥ nīlaḥ eva viṣayaḥ ākāre vā parisamāpta ātmā pīta ādi sampṛkta ātmā ca iti na dvitīyaḥ tad abhāvāt evam anākāra tvam aviṣaya tvam ca buddheḥ iṣyate eva iti ced tat kim yat pratibhāsate tat asat āhosvit na pratibhāsate eva kiñcid na ādyaḥ asati api nīla pīta ādau jñāna vṛtti vikalpasya tad avastha tvāt na hi kṛtsnam eva vijñānam nīla ullekhi pīta ādi anullekha prasaṅgāt na api tat eka deśaḥ tad abhāvāt iti ukta tvāt na dvitīyaḥ bāhye api vṛtti vikalpasya anupapatteḥ iti 
ĀTV_619.7–619.13	 syāt etat niḥśeṣa samudāyī kṛtsna śabdasya arthaḥ samudāye kaścid eva samudāyi eka deśa padārthaḥ na ca buddhiḥ samudāya svabhāvāḥ tasyāḥ eka rūpa tvāt tat kutas kṛtsna eka deśa vikalpa utthānam katham tarhi tad viṣayiṇī tad ākāravatī vā prakāra antara abhāvāt iti yadi tadā svarūpeṇa iti brūmaḥ iti ced sphuṭam niraṭaṅki tārkika vedikā viṭaṅkena kevalam asmabhyam abhyasūyatā dūraṅga tvā iti 
ĀTV_620.13–621.7	 etena tad atad deśa tvam nirastam tathā hi buddheḥ nīla ākāra tām paricchindat adhyakṣam tad abhāva vyavaccheda mukhena tad avinābhūtām pīta ādi ākāra tām api vyavacchindyāt tathā ca katham ekā buddhiḥ nīla pīta ādi ākārā syāt iti tulyaḥ anuyogaḥ bhavet evam yadi nīla ādi ākāra tāyāḥ pīta ādi ākāra tva abhāva avinā bhāvaḥ syāt saḥ eva tu kutas nīla pīta ādi ākārāyāḥ buddheḥ aikātmyena eva niścayāt pratyākāra niyata tve citra pratipatteḥ api anupapattiḥ iti ced tat etat tulyam paramāṇu avayavi ādiṣu api na hi tatra api aneka paramāṇu saṃsṛṣṭasya kadāpi na syāt iti tulyā eva artha gatiḥ vāci vaicityam tu kva upayujyate iti 
ĀTV_622.5–622.6–625.16–626.2	 saṃyoga vyavasthāpanena eva ṣaṭkena yugapad yogāt diś deśa bhedāt chāyā vṛttibhyām iti ādayaḥ nirastāḥ paramāṇu siddhi asiddhibhyām eva mūrtta tva ādayaḥ niravakāśitāḥ ākāśa vyatibheda ādayaḥ tu asambhāvitāḥ eva sarvatra ca atra hetu daśāyām pratijñāpadayoḥ vyāghātaḥ kāla atyaya apadeśaḥ ca prasaṅga daśāyām āśraya asiddhiḥ vyāpti asiddhiḥ ca dṛṣṭānta asiddheḥ anavasthā lakṣaṇa viparīta tarkasya tad upaṣṭambhaka tayā truṭeḥ ameya tva prasaṅgasya ca vidyamāna tvāt 
ĀTV_627.15–627.19–629.1–629.5	 na ca pralayaḥ paramāṇoḥ asattva sādhakasya pramāṇasya abhāvāt sāvayava tva āpādakānām ca hetūnām anavasthā utthāpaka tvāt iti tat anyaḥ eva ayam paramāṇuḥ raktabījaḥ yasya bhāgāḥ yukticā muṇḍa udaram api bhitvā niṣpatanti iti na ca kalpita āśrayāḥ kalpita pratibandhāḥ ca prasaṅgāḥ bhaviṣyanti iti yuktam icchā kalpitena vyavahāreṇa sarva vidhi niṣedha vyavahāra vilopa prasaṅgāt loka vyavasthā apekṣaṇe tu tad virodhena uttarasya niṣedhasya ātma lābha abhāvāt iti asakṛt āvedita tvāt 
ĀTV_629.15–630.3–630.11–630.12	 anyathā sarvam etat buddhau api samānam sā api hi ṣaṭkena yugapad yoga ādibhiḥ sa avayavā prasajyeta tasyām asiddhāḥ te iti ced na anumāna siddha tvāt tathā hi buddhiḥ ṣaṭkena yugapad yoginī mūrttimatī ca sattvāt vyavaharttavya tvāt vā bodhya vat iti śakyate viparyayasya api dharmi grāhaka māna sādhita tvāt anavakāśam idam iti ced evam anyatra api pratisanda dhīthā iti eṣā diś anyaḥ tu cakṣuṣī nimīlya nirbhayī bhavitum icchan āha astu tarhi buddheḥ api vilopaḥ iti 
ĀTV_631.3–631.11	 atra tu kim vaktavyam yatra hetu ādi vyavahāraḥ na asti astu param sāmvṛtaḥ iti ced bhavet evam yadi samvṛtiḥ api parama artha satī syāt anyathā tu yathā na vāstavaḥ tathā na sāmvṛtaḥ api samvṛtiḥ api samvṛtisatī iti ced asyāḥ api asattve na kiñcid adhikam uktam para samvṛteḥ tu parama artha sattva svīkāre sā eva buddhiḥ apariheya iti satī ca bādhakavatī ca iti samvṛti satī ca iti ced sati eva yadi tat katham bādhakam tathā ced katham tadālīḍhasya sattvam iti 
ĀTV_633.1–633.11	 dṛśyate tāvat evam iti ced sattva eka artha samavāyinaḥ bādhaka tvam eva tarhi heyam bādhaka eka artha samavāyinaḥ sattvam eva kid na hīyate iti ced na bādhakasya api tyāga prasaṅgāt ubhayam api avarjanīyam eva tarhi evam etat mithas virodhaḥ tu heyaḥ na hi viruddhayoḥ eka artha samavāyaḥ tathābhūtayoḥ vā virodhaḥ śakyaḥ upapādayitum ṛte sva samayāt na ca vicāra avasare sva samaya avatāraḥ iti yathā yathā ca buddhi nivāraṇāya bodhavyam eva iti tat etat āyātam pradīpa antareṇa pradīpam nirvāpya timira āpādanam iti 
ĀTV_634.17–635.3–636.14–636.17	 etena hetu phala bhāva anupapatteḥ sarva vilopaḥ iti nirastam tad nirākaraṇa prayāsasya sāphalya vaiphalyābhyām tad nirākaraṇa anupapatteḥ satkārya dūṣaṇasya iṣṭa tvāt asat kāya dūṣaṣasya ca pratyakṣa bodhita tvāt tat prati pādanasya asataḥ eva utpattau anaikāntika tvāt sattve vā prayāsa vaiphalyāt iti syāt etat mā bhūvan etāni dūṣaṇāni avayavini anupalambhaḥ tu syāt na hi paramāṇu sañcayāt aparam kiñcid upalabhyate iti ced vailakṣya viṣṭambhikeyam sthūla eka anubhavasya sarva jana siddha tvāt 
ĀTV_637.7–637.12	 vikalpa mātram tat iti ced na spaṣṭa pratibhāsa tvāt aupādhikam asya spaṣṭa tvam iti ced tathābhūta anubhavam antareṇa upādheḥ api abhāvāt anyathā nīla ādi vikalpānām api tathā eva spaṣṭa tva upapattau sarva pratyakṣa uccheda prasaṅgāt gṛhīta niścitaḥ eva arthe pratyakṣa prāmāṇyāt niścaya upaplave tasya api upaplavāt iti 
ĀTV_639.3–639.10–640.13–640.17	 na ca paramāṇavaḥ eva sthūlāḥ tattva vyāghātāt na ca tad samudāyaḥ tathā tasya samudita sthānasya tvayā anabhyupagamāt abhyupagame vā avayavinā kim aparāddham na ca samuditāḥ eva tathā pratibhāsitum arhanti teṣām pratyekam asthūla tvāt na ca nānā diś deśa vyāpitā eva sthaulyam paramāṇuṣu pratyekam asambhavati na ca nānātva eka artha samavayinī eva sā sthaulyam iti sāmpratam sthūlaḥ ekaḥ iti pratyaya niyamāt na ca bhāgeṣu eva āropitena eka tvena idam upapattim atas tad asambhavāt na hi kara caraṇa cibuka nāsikā ādi paramāṇūnām aikyam kaścid kvacid āropayati na ca teṣu bhedena prathamāneṣu na sthūla prayayaḥ na ca tattve sphurati eva tad viparītā tattva samāra upasambhavaḥ 
ĀTV_641.9–641.18	 api ca evam eka paramāṇu ātmanā paramāṇu koṭiḥ api āropitā paramāṇu mātra tayā eva parisphuret na sthūla tayā na ca nānā diś deśa vyāpi tu asya eṣa mahimā iti sāmpratam virodhāt yadi hi nānā ādikkāḥ paramāṇavaḥ deśa tayā avabhāseran na ekatayā deśitayā ca āropyeran tathā ca kasya nānā diś deśa vyāpitā deśinaḥ aparisphūrtteḥ atha tathā tvena āropyeran na nānātvena deśa tvena vā avabhāseran tathā ca kasya nānā diś deśa vyāpitā deśinaḥ aparisphūrtteḥ tasmāt eka tva ārope paramāṇu mātra avabhāsaḥ eva syāt iti 
ĀTV_643.12–643.15–644.12–644.13	 evam tarhi anārabdha dravya rāśiṣu kā vārttā iti ced na tāvat deśa vyāpti sāmyena tāvat parimāṇa dravya tva āropaḥ na ca iha api tathā syāt anyatra api asiddheḥ na ca āsan eva ekaḥ sthūlaḥ parisphurati bādhakānām apāsta tvāt etena pratibhāsa dharmaḥ api nirastaḥ saḥ api hi asan bauddhaḥ vāstavaḥ vā iti trayīm gatim na ativarttate iti 
ĀTV_645.9–645.12–646.6–646.8	 atīndriyāḥ ca pratyekam aṇavaḥ katham militāḥ api dṛśyeran atīndriya samūhasya api atīndriya tvāt viśiṣṭa utpādāt aindriyaka tvam iti ced kim adya api svapne hastam prasārayasi astu vā evam tathā api kṣaṇa bhedāt jāti bhedaḥ nirākṛtaḥ jāti saṅkara prasaṅgāt tad abhedena tu utpāde api tat vā tādṛś vā iti tattva dṛśā na kaścid viśeṣaḥ 
ĀTV_647.4–647.9	 bhavatu vā jāti viśeṣaḥ api tathā api sthūla tvam eva aindriyaka tvam prati prayojakam mantavyam anyathā sthūla tām anāpnuvan ekaḥ api paramāṇuḥ kadāpi tathā utpannaḥ pratyakṣa tām iyāt niyamena tu tad viparītasya pratyakṣatā tathāvidhasya apratyakṣatāyām eva viśrāmyati anvaya vyatireka phala tvāt dhetu phala bhāvasya 
ĀTV_648.3–648.13	 na ca sañcitāḥ api sthūla tayā utpannāḥ na ca bahu tvam eva sthailyam tad viparyayaḥ eva sūkṣma tā vitata deśānām api pratyakṣa tva prasaṅgāt nairantaryam api vivakṣitam iti ced na tasya prakṛte api asambhavāt rūpa paramāṇūnām rasa ādi paramāṇubhiḥ antarita tvāt na ca āropyate nairantaryam itaretara āśraya prasaṅgāt nairantarī ārope teṣām sthūlānām grahaṇam tad grahaṇe ca sati nairantari āropaḥ iti tasmāt aindriyaka tve sthūla tāyāḥ prayojaka tvāt aprayojaka tve vitata deśānām api pratyakṣa tva prasaṅgāt teṣām ca pratyekam asthūla tvāt atīndriyāḥ eva paramāṇavaḥ tathā ca sarva agrahaṇam avayavi asiddheḥ iti 
ĀTV_649.7–649.10–652.19–653.3	 astu tarhi kṣaṇa mātra sthāyī sthūlaḥ arthaḥ iti ced na bhāga bhāginoḥ yugapad upalambha bādhita tvāt ghaṭa paṭa ādi bhaṅge tantu kapāla ādīnām utpāde samāna upādāna tayā sa pratigha tva vyāghātāt ca iti saḥ ayam adhikaraṇa siddhānta nyāyena sthūla tva siddhau kṣaṇa bhaṅga bhaṅgaḥ etena yat sat tat niravayavam yathā vijñānam san ca vivāda āspadībhūtaḥ ghaṭa ādiḥ iti nirastam viparyaye bādhaka abhāvena vyāpti asiddheḥ yat sat tat sa avayavam yathā ghaṭaḥ sat ca vijñānam iti cārvāka parivarttasya api avakāśāt ca samaḥ vā samādhiḥ 
ĀTV_653.10–653.15	 nanu niravayavam eva vijñānam sva samvidita rūpam ghaṭasya ca sāvayavatāyām adya api vivādaḥ eva tat katham parivarttaḥ katham vā samaḥ samādhiḥ iti ced śuṣka vivādasya vijñāne api durvāra tvāt na hi kaścid kaṇṭha oṣṭha pārśva jaṭhara ādi parihīnam piṭharam anubhavati astu vā sattvāt sa pratigha tva siddhiḥ buddhau apratigha tvam vā ghaṭa ādau iti 
ĀTV_654.10–654.17	 api ca svatantra sādhanam idam prasaṅgaḥ vā na prathamaḥ ghaṭa ādi śabdena sthūla itarāṇām rūpa ādīnām paramāṇūnām vā pakṣīkaraṇe siddha sādhanāt sthūlam ekam abhyupagamya pakṣa vidhau kāla atyaya apadeśāt anabhyupagame tu āśraya asiddheḥ iti nanu prāmāṇike abhyupagame bādhaḥ syāt sarvathā anabhyupagame ca āśraya asiddhiḥ syāt na ca evam atra iti ced tat etat nabhaḥsthala kamala parimala sādhanasya api sa āśrayatām āpādayat āśraya asiddhi doṣa moṣāya iti alam anena 
ĀTV_655.12–656.3	 parvata ādi vat loka pratīti siddhān ghaṭa ādīn upādāya niravayavatva anumānam syāt anyathā brahma vivartta ādi vipratipatti vihata tayā dahana anumānam api parvata ādau na syāt iti ced na evam avirodhāt na hi brahma vivartta ādi siddhau api āśraya ādayaḥ anya prakārāḥ sambhavanti tathā hi sarvatra svapna parvate svapna dhūmena svapna vahniḥ eva sādhyate kevalam sāmvṛte api vyavahāre satya anṛta vyavasthā asti iti tasyām nirbharaḥ karttavyaḥ iha tu ghaṭa ādi vyapadeśena sthūlaḥ eva yadi pakṣīkṛtaḥ katham niravayava tvena sādhyena na virodhaḥ 
ĀTV_657.8–657.18	 atha paramāṇuḥ eva katham na siddha sādhanam vipratipannam prati na tathā iti ced na vai kaścid paramāṇūnām nirvayava tve vipratipadyate loka vyāmoha nibarhaṇāya sādhanam iti ced tathā api yam lokaḥ sthūlam ekam upalabdhavān tasya pakṣa tve virodhaḥ eva tatas anyasya pakṣa tve siddha sādhanam eva ekaḥ sthūlaḥ ayam iti mithyā iti ced etat eva tarhi sādhyatām kim anena ajāgala stana kalpena sattvena na ca tatra eva idam śakyam upasaṃharttum vyadhikaraṇa tvāt tasmāt yena rūpeṇa yasya pakṣa tvam vivakṣitam tena siṣā dhayiṣita dharma virodha vivādābhyām tatra anumāna pravṛttiḥ na atas anyathā iti 
ĀTV_659.10–659.15–661.5–661.7	 na api dvitīyaḥ viparyaya aparyavasānāt na ca vivāda viṣayaḥ niravayavaḥ tasmāt na san iti viparyayaḥ na ca evam sāvayava tvam pakṣasya anicchatā pravarttayitum śakyate na ca tat tvayā iṣyate na tasya iṣṭau tena asattvam śakya sādhanam āśraya asiddheḥ virodhāt asādha araṇyāt vā na ca viparyayaḥ api pareṣṭyā pravarttate iti kaḥ punar avayavini nyāyaḥ tat kim pratyakṣān nyāyaḥ garīyān yadi evam buddhau eva kaḥ asau tasmāt asāram etat 
ĀTV_661.17–662.4	 tathā api yat nirasta samasta viruddha dharma adhyāsam tat ekam eva vyavaharttavyam yathā vijñānam tathā ca vivāda adhyāsitaḥ eka sthūlaḥ anubhava gocaraḥ iti svabhāva hetuḥ tāvat mātra anuvandhi tvāt eka tā vyavahārasya na hi ayam eka vyavahāraḥ nirnimittaḥ aniyama prasaṅgāt na api anya nimittaḥ drava kaṭhina śāta uṣṇa ādau api tathā avyavahāra prasaṅgāt 
ĀTV_662.14–663.2	 astu tarhi bāhyeśu artheṣu nitya sandehaḥ tathyā tathya vibhāgasya aśakya tvāt iti ced na tāvat sarvasya yathārtha tvāt eva vibhāgaḥ anupapannaḥ uttara virodhāt tathā hi viparītam avagatam mayā iti laukikī pratipattiḥ anyathā khyātiḥ iti ca vainayikī yathārthāḥ na vā ubhayathā api uttareṇa na sarva yāthārthya siddhiḥ 
ĀTV_664.11–664.16	 śabda saṃlāpa mātram etat na pratītiḥ iti ced na vivāda anupapatteḥ na hi vyavahāra mātre parīkṣakāṇām vivādaḥ na ca na ayam asti iti śabda arthe vivādaḥ iti ced evam satya pratītasya niṣeddhum aśakya tvāt para abhiprāya niṣedha artha tvāt ca vivādasya abhyuoagantṛ pratiṣeddhroḥ pratiṣedhya pratītiḥ katham na asti iti 
ĀTV_666.3–666.12	 na ca anya jñānāt anyatra pravṛtti sambhavaḥ ati prasaṅgāt na ca tad jñāna sānnidhyam niyāmakam atiprasaṅgāt eva na ca tad sahitaḥ bheda āgrahaḥ agraha prādhānye bheda avivakṣāyām nivṛtteḥ api prasaṅgāt tad hetoḥ abheda agrahasya api vidyamāna tvāt na asau nivarttakaḥ api tu bheda grahaḥ iti ced na rajate eva na idam rajatam iti kṛtvā na nivartteta bheda grahasya tad kāraṇasya abhāvāt bhāve vā viparīta khyātiḥ abhinne bheda pratyayāt tasmāt pravarttaka vat nivarttakaḥ api agrahaḥ eva teṣām svīkarttum ucitaḥ tathā ca sa doṣaḥ tad avasthaḥ eva 
ĀTV_669.5–669.7–674.17–674.20	 atha bhedaḥ pradhānam aṅgam agrahaḥ tadā sati arajata jñānāt rajate na pravartteta idam aṃśa rajata aṃśayoḥ bheda abhāvāt iti svayam ūhanīyam pravṛtti vat pratipattau api ubhayāgrahaḥ tulyaḥ iti ced na agrahasya avivakṣita tvāt sāmagrī viśeṣāt eva tad siddheḥ tattve aparisphurati iti tu niyamaḥ na ca kvacid api bheda abhedau ubhau api tattvam yatas tathā syāt iti eṣa diś na api sarvasya ayathārtha tvāt tad grāhakasya yathārtha tva ayatha artha tvābhyām uttara virodhāt tat kiñcid pramāṇam kiñcid apramāṇam iti vibhāgaḥ eva vastu gatiḥ na ca asau pratīti gatim avadhūya vyavahāra gocaraḥ 
ĀTV_675.17–676.6–681.4–681.7	 kathantā tu nirūpyate svatas paratas vā iti ādye api svayam sva grāhakeṇa iti vā tatra na prathamaḥ sva samvedanasya asiddheḥ prakāśa tvasya asādhāraṇa tvāt śabda sāmyena anumāna apravṛtteḥ na ca adhyakṣam eva atra pramāṇam sandigdha bheda tvāt apratyakṣa upalambhasya na artha dṛśṭiḥ prasiddhyati pareṇa para vedane anavasthā syāt na ca kriyā sva jātīya kriyā karma bhāvam aśnute cchidāvat iti tarka puraskārāt na eṣa doṣaḥ iti ced na upalambha apara paryāyāyāḥ dṛśṭeḥ siddhiḥ niṣpattiḥ vā syāt pratītiḥ vā ādye anāgata upalambha vedana prasaṅgaḥ anupalabdhasya aniṣpatteḥ na ca avidyamānena avidyamānasya upalambhaḥ iti sva samvittau asamvittiḥ eva iti 
ĀTV_682.3–682.12	 dvitīye tu siddha sādhanam na hi anupalabdhaḥ upalabdhaḥ bhavati na ca evam sati arthaḥ api na upalabhyeta na hi upalambha pratītiḥ artha vedanam api tu upalambha niṣpattiḥ upalambha adṛṣṭau upalambha niṣpattiḥ iti eva vyavahāraḥ kutas iti ced mā bhūt na hi avyavahārāt eva niṣpannasya vastunaḥ nivṛttiḥ tathā ca tad nibandhanaḥ artha vyavahāraḥ durvāraḥ eva na ca anavasthā avaśya vedya tva anabhyupagamāt niścaya vat anyathā tu aniścita niścayasya artha niścayaḥ api na siddhyet na ca asau sva ātmani api niścayaḥ iti tat idam vadhūmāṣa m āpana vṛttāntam anuharati 
ĀTV_685.6–685.13	 cchid ādi vat iti tu dṛṣṭānta mātreṇa na asmat avadhānam jñānam na jñāna antara karma tad jātīya kriyā tvāt yā yat jātīyā kriyā na asau tad kriyā akarma yathā chidā chidāntarasya iti tu nyāya viplavaḥ chidāvat sarvathā sajātīya akarma tve sādhye bādhita viṣaya tvāt puruṣa antara jñānasya ca puruṣa antara jñāna vedya tvāt svayam api smṛti ādi gocara tvāt ca sva karva tve sādhye dṛṣṭāntasya sādhya vikala tayā hetoḥ viruddha tvāt iti 
ĀTV_687.12–687.14–690.1–690.8	 na api sva grāhakeṇa vivecana anupapatteḥ na hi pramāṇa grahaṇam yathārtha tva eka niyatam apramāṇe api pramāṇa abhimānāt anyathā viparyaya jñānāt apravṛtti prasaṅgāt ca tatas yadi prāmāṇyam āpātataḥ sphuret api tathā api niyama hetoḥ abhāvāt pramāṇam eva idam iti niścayaḥ kutas sa ca mṛgyate pāralaukika vyavahāra aṅga tvāt śaṅkā nivarttanena tat apratyūham niścitam eva iti ced tad nivṛttiḥ eva kutas pramāṇa antarāt iti ced tat api niścaya phalam anyathā vā iti anyathātve na śaṅkā vicchedaḥ niścaya sādhya tvāt tasya niścaya phala tve tu yaḥ mṛgyate na asau svatas iti 
ĀTV_691.12–692.3	 sphuraṇa mātram api tāvat astu svatas iti ced kim tena na ca etat api ananu saṃhita upādheḥ upahita pratyaya ayogāt na ca viṣaya upādhāna mātram prāmāṇyam tad ābhāsa sādhāraṇyāt api tu anubhavasya sataḥ bhūta artha anusandhānam na ca artha anusandhāne api tasya bhūta tvam anusandhīyate āropita tva vyāvarttaka viśeṣaṇa ananusandhānāt ananu saṃhitasya cāra upasādhāraṇyāt kvacid viśeṣaḥ api anusandhīyate iti ced na kvāpi prathamikena anyathā anabhyāsa daśāyām tatra api saṃśayaḥ na syāt abhyāsa daśa utpanne tu anusandhānam vyāpti graha janita saṃskāra samudbhava smaraṇa balena bhavat pramāṇa antara śarīraḥ eva praviśati iti paratas eva avaśiṣyate 
ĀTV_697.8–698.2	 tatra api anavasthā iti ced na tāvat asau dṛṣṭānta dvārikā prāk eva tad niścayāt phaladvārikā tu syāt api yadi prāmāṇyam avaśya niśceyam abhyupeyate ajñāta prāmāṇyena katham para prāmāṇya vedanam iti ced yathā viṣaya saṃvedanam astu tarhi dharmi liṅga dvārikā tābhyām aniścitābhyām ananumānāt tad niścayasya ca prāmāṇya niścayam antareṇa anupapatteḥ na dvaita abhāvāt yatra hi liṅga jñāne dharmi jñāne vā tathyā tathya bhāvena dvaitam upalbhyate tatra tathyatva aniścaye liṅgam ābhāsa śaṅkā ākrānta tayā na niścīyate yatra tu tat jñānam tat eka niyatam tatra tāvatā eva liṅga niścayaḥ tad ābhāsa śaṅkā anutthānāt eka koṭi niyataḥ hi anubhavaḥ niścayaḥ jñāna tad dharma grāhiṇi ca jñāne na dvaitam iti vyavasthitiḥ eva prāmāṇya niścayaḥ tu tasya api paratas eva iti nyāya sampradāyaḥ itas eva viśeṣāt tādṛśasya svatas eva iti tātpari ācāryāḥ 
ĀTV_701.15–702.4	 syāt matam etat eva tu katham niśceyam yat evambhūtam eka koṭi niyatam eva yāvatā tatra api anavasthitiḥ iti ced na vyāpti jñānasya sākṣāt ātmani apravṛttau api sarva upasaṃhāreṇa yam upādhim ādāya pravṛtti s tad dharmavat tvāt tad jātīya tvam hi tatra upādhiḥ tat ca tatra api aviśiṣṭam anuvyavasāya tvāt na ca sāmānyatas niyama niścaye tadāliṅgite viśeṣe dvaita śaṅkā avakāśaḥ yathā vācakaḥ śabdaḥ iti sva ātmanaḥ vācaka tvam na sākṣāt vidhatte vṛtti virodhāt tathā api sāmānyena yam upādhim adhikṛtya pravṛttaḥ śabdaḥ tadvat tvāt śabda śabdaḥ vācakaḥ na vā iti śaṅkayā na paribhūyate na api anavasthā iti evam iha api iti 
ĀTV_703.19–704.5	 tarkāḥ ca atra bhavanti yadi dharma jñānam vyabhicaret nirālambanam asat ālambanam vā bhavet niṣiddham ca tat yadi anuvyavasāyaḥ vyabhicāret tadā artha karmakaḥ api na syāt jñāna itarasya artha prāvaṇya abhāvāt yadi tat jātīyam vyabhicaret avyabhicāraḥ na kvacid vyavatiṣṭheta tat avyavasthitau vyabhicāraḥ api na syāt anyathā ākhyāti rūpa tvāt tasya tattva sthiau ca anyathātvam syāt tad avadhika tvāt 
ĀTV_705.16–705.19–706.13–706.19	 etena svapna jāgara avasthayoḥ aviśeṣaḥ iti nirastam asat khyāteḥ ātma khyāteḥ ca nirākṛta tvāt anyathā ākhyāteḥ ca tattva khyāti vyavasthām antareṇa anupapatteḥ iti sā ca jāgare api yadi na syāt na syāt eva iti tathā api katham anayoḥ avasthayoḥ vibhāgaḥ karttavyaḥ iti ced na loka siddha tvāt kim anayoḥ lakṣaṇam iti ced kartṛ karma karaṇa deśa kāla prabandha bādhaḥ kākatālīya samvādavān svapnasya prabandhe kākatālīyaḥ kasya cit eva viṣayasya bādhaḥ jāgarasya iti etena bādhya prabandhaḥ avasthā viśeṣaḥ svapnaḥ prabandha bādhaka ādiḥ vādhyamāna prabandha antaḥ jāgaritam iti api draṣṭavyam iti eṣā diś 
ĀTV_708.10–708.15	 tasmāt tathyam eva viśvam manda prayojana tvāt tu sa tvaraiḥ mumukṣubhiḥ upekṣitam iti yuktam utpaśyāmaḥ tarhi naiyāyikānām jagat parirakṣaṇe kaḥ ayam abhiniveśa atiśayaḥ iti ced sahasā eva tad upekṣāyām nyāya ābhāsa avakāśe pramāṇa mātra viplavaḥ bhavet tathā ca nyāya ruciḥ prekṣāvān na tattvam adhigacchet iti bhiyā iti 
ĀTV_710.2–710.7–714.14–714.15	 astu tarhi guṇa guṇinoḥ abhedāt nairāmyam kṣaṇika jñāna mātra pariśeṣāt iti ced ucyate asti tāvat iha darśana sparśanābhyām eka artha anusandhānam tat idam ekaika viṣayam vā syāt samudāya viṣayam vā tad atirikta viṣayam vā vastu ananurodhi ākāra viṣayam vā alīka viṣayam vā na tāvat adyaḥ na hi yat eva rūpam saḥ eva sparśaḥ iti na ca rūpam tvac indriya grāhyam andhasya api nīla ādi pratyaya prasaṅgāt na ca ekam eva vastu karaṇa bhedena anyathā prathate iti yuktam anātmaka tva prasaṅgāt bheda abheda vyavasthā anupapatteḥ ca na api dvitīyaḥ sa hi eka deśa tayā vai eka kāla tayā vai eka kārya tayā vai eka kāraṇa tayā vā iti 
ĀTV_715.4–715.17	 na tāvat upādāna rūpa eka deśa sambhavaḥ tayoḥ pratiniyata upādāna tvāt sambhave vā tat eva dravyam iti paryavasitam vivādena na api adhikaraṇībhūta bhū tala ādi a ādhāra tayā tad sambhavaḥ cakṣuṣā hi upalabhyamāne bhū tale rūpa viśeṣe ghaṭaḥ api cakṣuṣā eva upalambhyamāne bhū tale rūpa viśeṣaḥ tad ādhāraḥ iti śakyate niścetum tayoḥ adhara uttara bhāvena eka jñāna saṃsargi tvāt tad adhikaraṇāḥ sparśa ādayaḥ api iti tu kasya pramāṇasya viṣayaḥ na hi sparśa ādayaḥ cākṣuṣe cetasi cakāsati tvacaḥ ayam vyāpāraḥ iti api na asti tayā api bhū tala ghaṭa sparśayoḥ ādhāra ādheya bhāva pratīteḥ na ca samudāyayoḥ tad sambhavaḥ paraspara āśraya tva prasaṅgāt eka ādhāra tāyām hi samudāya anusandhānam samudāya anusandhāne ca eka ādhāra tā anusandhāna sambhavaḥ iti anavasthā prasaṅgāt ca bhū talasya api samudāya tvam kiṅkṛtam iti anuyoga anivṛtteḥ 
ĀTV_717.8–717.10–719.14	 atas eva na eka kāla tayā api tayoḥ eka kāla tāyām pramāṇa abhāvāt bhāve vā rāsabha kara bhayoḥ api eka kāla tayā samudāya tva prasaṅgaḥ bheda āgrahasya prakṛte api asambhavāt atas eva na eka kārya tayā api upādeya rūpasya eka kāryasya abhāvāt ekodaka āharaṇa lakṣaṇa artha kriyā ityādi api na yuktam rūpa ādi atiriktasya udakasya anabhyupagamāt ekaikasya aneka āhārya tve pramāṇa abhāvāt samudāyasya ca asiddheḥ atas eva na eka kāraṇa tayā api iti nimittam antareṇa tu samudāya vyavahāre ati prasaṅgaḥ tṛtīye na vivādaḥ na api caturthaḥ sa hi vijñānanayam āśritya vā syāt dvi candra ādi vat visamvādāt vā ādye tu rūpa ādiṣu kaḥ pakṣapātaḥ 
ĀTV_720.1–720.12	 prāpteḥ artha kriyā sthiteḥ ca na dvitīyaḥ api te dve rūpa ādīnām iti ced na teṣām kintu tasya eva iti kim na syāt bādhakāt iti ced na tāvat krama yaugapadya virodhaḥ rakta ārakta virodhaḥ vā bādhakam niṣiddha tvāt kṣaṇika paramāṇu rūpa dravyeṇa ākrānteḥ ca sambandha abhāvaḥ iti ced asambandhaḥ tāvat astu katham tadvat pratīyate iti ced asambandhaḥ tu katham tadvat pratīyate iti ced teṣām tathā utpādāt iti parihāraḥ astu tava eva yathā śarīram cetanā vat iti rūpa ādibhiḥ eva samasta artha kriyā siddheḥ kim tad atirikta dravya kalpanayā iti ced na tāvat mātreṇa eva samasta artha kriyā siddheḥ kim rūpa ādi kalpanayā iti asya api vācāṭa vacasaḥ avakāśa prasaṅgāt pratīyamāna tvāt iti ced tulyam 
ĀTV_721.18–723.17–728.2	 etena alīka viṣaya tā api nirastāḥ abheda sādhanam bādhakam iti ced kim tat saha upalambha niyamaḥ iti ced na sama saha upalambha niyamasya asiddheḥ pīta śaṅkha upalambha ādau śvaitya anupalambhe api śaṅkha upalambhāt na asau śaṅkhaḥ kintu śaṅkhaḥ iva taimiraka keśa vat iti ced aho guṇavat viveṣaḥ yat taimirika keśāḥ kara tala parāmarśa pratiniyata artha kriyayoḥ apārān na sambhavanti iti vyavasthāpayati iha tu tad sambhave api śubhra tā mātra anupalambhāt iti 
ĀTV_724.7–724.15–725.11–725.12	 vyāpaka tvāt iti ced vastunoḥ vyāptiḥ upalambhayoḥ vā ādye na vipratipattiḥ na ca vyāpaka anupalabdhi mātreṇa vyāpya tad upalabdhī nivarttete dahana anupalabdhau dhūma tad upalabdhyoḥ api nivṛtti prasaṅgāt tatra api vā kim na parikalpayasi dhūmaḥ iva asau na dhūmaḥ iti pāvaka vat tā anupalabdheḥ iti tasmāt na vyāpaka anupalabdheḥ vyāpya nivṛttiḥ kintu vyāpaka nivṛtteḥ sā ca atra asiddhā iti vācyam tat etat tulyam prakṛte api upalabdheḥ tu vyāptiḥ iha eva bhagnāḥ śvaitya anupalambhaḥ api śaṅkha upalambhāt iti uktam syāt etat pītaḥ eva śaṅkhaḥ utpannaḥ iti ced na puruṣa antareṇa śvaityasya eva upalabdheḥ 
ĀTV_725.16–726.13	 na api asamaḥ eva saha upalambha niyamaḥ hetuḥ anaikāntāt abhāsvaram rūpam bhāsvareṇa saha niyamena upalabhyate bhinnam ca iti deśa avicchedaḥ iti ced na asiddheḥ deha dehibhyām anaikāntāt ca na tayoḥ avicchedaḥ tad upalambhe api upalambhāt iti ced tulyam rūpa ādi anupalambhe api tadvatām upalabdheḥ tathā api na viparyayaḥ kadā api iti ced tulyam na hi deha ādi anupalambhe dehi anupalambha vat dehi anupalambhe api dehasya upalambha sambhavaḥ tava darśane pratipatti niṣpatti sāmagrī sāhitya niyamena saha upalambhaḥ vā deśa avicchedaḥ vā syāt niyamena viruddha dharma adhyāsāt bhedaḥ ca iti kaḥ virodhaḥ dharma virodhaḥ eva kaḥ atra iti ced tad upalambhe api anupalambhaḥ tad abhidhāne api anabhidhānam tat niṣedhe api aniṣedhaḥ ityādi nīlam utpalam calati ityādau ca vyāvṛtti bheda nirākaraṇe pūrvakaḥ eva nyāyaḥ anusandheyaḥ anyatra upādhi bhedāt 
ĀTV_730.10–730.16	 abhede ca dharma dharmiṇoḥ dūrādūra tayā grahaṇe paṭu apaṭunī kutas na ca puruṣa bhedena tathā eva anyasya utpādaḥ ekasya dvairūpya abhāvāt na ca anyānyaḥ eva asau eka deśa tayā tattvena pratisandhānāt na ca sā bhrāntāḥ bhinna deśasya tathābhūtasya pratyāsīdatā api anupalambhāt na ca nirālambaḥ eva tad upalambhaḥ vṛkṣa ādi deśa pratiniyama anupapatteḥ 
ĀTV_732.12–732.19	 na ca adhipati pratyaya tvāt tasya iti yuktam anubhavānām tad deśa ullekhān anurodhāt ullekhe vā saḥ eva ālambana pratyayaḥ tāvat mātra anubandhi tvāt avalambana vyavahārasya na ca deśaḥ astu ālambanam na tu vṛkṣa ādiḥ iti sāmpratam anupalabdha viśeṣa tayā deśa deśinoḥ aviśeṣāt na ca dvitīyāṃsaḥ api viśeṣāḥ sphuranti eva na tu niścīyante iti yuktam na hi yoga vimala añjana dhauta dṛṣṭeḥ anyasya tārā vyūha gatayaḥ pratibhānti iti śakyam pratipādayitum 
ĀTV_735.17–735.21–736.16–737.3	 aniścaya anupapatteḥ ca anubhūtaḥ hi ātmā na niścīyate iti atra hetuḥ vācyaḥ vāsanā anudbhavaḥ iti ced na niḥśeṣa viśeṣavantam dharmiṇam upalabhya vidūra varttinaḥ tad akhila smaraṇe api anubhava vyāpāra anusāri niścaya anudayāt tathā api ca anubhava kalpanāyām sarvaḥ sarvadā sarvam jānāti na tu niścinoti iti kim na syāt bhrānti vaśāt tad viparīta viśeṣa niścaye anubhūta viśeṣā niścayaḥ iti ced na anubhava vaiparītye niścayasya sarva tra anāśvāsa prasaṅgāt yatra ca viparītasya api aniścayaḥ tatra kā vārttā yathā parācīnaiḥ bhāgaiḥ arvācīnānām saṃyoga vibhāgayoḥ iti 
ĀTV_739.2–739.10	 astu tarhi nairāmyma anupalabdheḥ iti ced na sarva adṛṣṭeḥ ca sandehāt svādṛṣṭeḥ vyabhicārataḥ dṛśya tva viśeṣaṇāt na evam iti ced na tat asiddheḥ para upagama siddheḥ adoṣaḥ iti ced na svatantra sādhana tvāt yadi paraḥ sahasā eva na evam abhyupagacchet nūnam sādhanam idam mūrcchet yadi ca parādṛṣṭim avadhūya dṛśyantam abhyupagacchet evam api sambhavet na ca evam śakyam tasya tad upahita rūpa tvāt iti saṅkṣepaḥ vistaraḥ tu asantaḥ akṣaṇikāḥ iti vat ūhanīyaḥ 
ĀTV_743.5–743.13	 atha ātma sadbhāve kim pramāṇam pratyakṣam eva tāvat aham iti vikalpasya prāṇa bhṛt mātra siddha tvāt na ca ayam avastukaḥ sandigdha vastukaḥ vā aśābda tvāt apratikṣepāt ca na ca lauṅgikaḥ ananu saṃhita liṅgasya api sva pratyayāt na ca smṛtiḥ iyam ananubhūte tad anupapatteḥ anādi vāsanā vaśāt anādiḥ ayam avastukaḥ vikalpaḥ iti api na yuktam nīla ādi vikalpa sādhāraṇyāt iha vāsanām upādāya anāśvāse pramāṇa antare api kaḥ samāśvāsaḥ yatas nīla ādi vikalpeṣu samāśvāsaḥ syāt 
ĀTV_745.15–745.21–746.16–746.18	 tasmāt vāsanā mātra vādam vihāya āgantukam api kiñcid kāraṇam vācyam tat ca āptān āpta śabdau vā liṅga tadābhāsau vā pratyakṣa tad ābhāsau vā iti tatra yathā prathama madhyama prakāra abhāvāt nīla vikalpaḥ caram kalpam ālambate tathā aham iti vikalpaḥ api tatra ayam pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvi tve sākṣāt eva sa vastukaḥ tad ābhāse tu mūle asya pāramparyāt sa vastu tā iti na ca bāhya pratyakṣa nivṛttau eva nirmūla tvam buddhi vikalpasya api tathā tva prasaṅgāt tatra sva samvedanam mūlam iha api mānasa pratyakṣam iti na kaścid viśeṣaḥ 
ĀTV_747.14–748.4	 śarīra ādi vastukaḥ bhaviṣyati iti ced na nirupādhi śarīra indriya buddhi tad samudāya ālambana tve ati prasaṅgāt sva sambandhi śarīra ādau ayam syāt iti vācyam tatra kaḥ sva arthaḥ iti vacanīyam ananya tvam svatavam sarva bhāvānām tathā ca yadā tena eva tat anubhūyate tadā pratyetuḥ pratyetavyāt avyatirekāt aham iti syāt atas eva ghaṭa ādayaḥ na kadācid ananyānnubhavitṛkā iti na kadā api aham āspadam iti ced evam tarhi tvad mate api aham pratyayaḥ śarīra ādau āroparūpaā iva tatas pratyetuḥ anya tvāt 
ĀTV_749.15–750.6	 buddhau mukhyaḥ eva iti ced na tasyāḥ kriyā tvena anubhūyamānāyāḥ bhinnasya karttuḥ aham cchinadmi iti vat aham jānāmi iti anubhavāt nīla ādi pratyeta vyākāra vat pratipatti ākāraḥ api pratipatteḥ eva ayam ātmā bhāsate iti ced tarhi pratyetavya pratipatti ākārayoḥ tulya yogakṣema tvāt siddham naḥ samīhitam astu sva upādāna mātram iti ced na tad pratibhā āsane tad ākārasya api pratibhāsa prasaṅgāt ākāram antareṇa ākāriṇaḥ anavabhāsāt pravṛtti santānānyaḥ buddhi santānaḥ pratipattā vayam tam ālaya vijñānam ācakṣmahe iti ced astu tarhi pravṛtti vijñāna upādānam anādi nidhanaḥ pratipattā sa kim santanyamāna jñāna rūpaḥ tad viparītaḥ vā iti cintā avaśiṣyate niḥśeṣitā ca asau prāk iti 
ĀTV_752.8–752.18	 kaḥ punar atra nyāyaḥ pratisandhānam tathyam idam iti asiddham atathyan ca viruddham aviśiṣṭam anaikāntikam iti ced na hetu artha an avabodhāt na hi pratyabhijñāna mātram atra vivakṣitam tat kim kārya kāraṇayoḥ eka santāna pratiniyamaḥ saḥ api viruddhaḥ iti ced eṣaḥ api na vivakṣitaḥ naḥ kaḥ tarhi pūrva apara dhiyām eka kartṛ tayā vinaścayaḥ eṣaḥ api tāsām upādāna upādeya bhāvenā api upapadyate iti ced na sthairya sthitau tad abhāvāt kṣaṇika tve api na eka jātīya tve sati tad utpattiḥ eva upādāna upādeya bhāvaḥ śiṣya ācārya dhiyām api tathā abhāva prasaṅgāt 
ĀTV_757.8–757.15–760.15–760.18	 bheda agrahe sati iti ced na prakṛte api tad abhāvāt śarīra bheda āgrahaḥ tāvat asti iti ced na bhinna janma jñāna avyāpteḥ anupalabdha pitṛkeṇa api bālena atiprasaṅgāt ghaṭa kapālakṣaṇayoḥ atathā bhāva prasaṅgāt ca eka dhāratayā niyamaḥ iti ced na tasya vāstavasya kṣaṇika tva pakṣe api viṣam asamayānām kṣaṇānām abhāvāt kālpanikasya tu ati prasañjaka tvāt śarīra buddhyoḥ api samāna deśatā abhimānāt etena abhrānta samatā eka avasāyaḥ prakṛti vikriye tatau hetu phalasya upādāna upādeya lakṣaṇam iti nirastam 
ĀTV_762.1–762.13	 kāṣṭhasya tu prakṛteḥ vikṛtiḥ aṅgāraḥ iti kutas niścitam bhavatā yāvatā vahneḥ eva ayam vikāraḥ kim na syāt vahni sambandhi kāṣṭhāt eva tad utpatteḥ iti ced na kāṣṭha sambandhena vahneḥ eva tad utpattiḥ iti api kim na kalpyeta pārthivam pārthiva upādānakam iti niścayāt iti ced kutas etat sa bhāgeṣu sva lakṣaṇeṣu tathā adarśanāt iti ced atha kā iyam samatā nāma yadi sājātyam sādeśyam vā tat prāk nirastam eka santāna tvan ced tat api tad utpatti mātran ced nimitta naimittikayoḥ api tathā abhāva prasaṅgaḥ upādāna upādeya bhāvaḥ ced katham tena eva tad vyavasthāpyeta jñāneṣu tad pratisandhānam eva upādāna upādeya lakṣaṇam iti ced na ātma āśraya prasaṅgāt 
ĀTV_764.10–764.17	 tat yogya tā iti ced sā eva kā iti cintyam śakti viśeṣaḥ iti ced sa tāvat na pratikṣaṇa niyataḥ yathā hi tena tat kartavyam tathā tādṛśā api tat kartavyam iti api niyamaḥ eva anyathā tena tat kṛtam iti api na niścīyeta kṣaṇasya durnneya tvāt tathā ca nirīham jagat jāyeta ākasmikan ca kāryasya tādṛśa tvam āpadyeta tathā ca na niyamaḥ upalabhyeta na api pratisantāna niyataḥ śakti viśeṣaḥ viśeṣa abhāvāt 
ĀTV_767.12–768.10	 astu vaijātyam iti ced na anupalabdhi bādhita tvāt na hi śiṣya ācārya nīla dhiyoḥ mātrayā api jāti kṛtam viśeṣam upalabhām ahe adṛśya tvāt ayam adoṣaḥ iti ced na dṛśya samavāyinyāḥ jāteḥ adṛśya tva anupapatteḥ upapattau vā dhūma ādau api avakāśa prasaṅgāt tathā ca avāntara sattva vat avāntara dhūmaḥ eva vahneḥ kāryaḥ syāt iti śaṅkā kalaṅkita tvāt na ca dhūma sāmānyam agnim gamyet evam etat ādyasya eva tathā abhāvāt iti ced na tatra api śaṅkāyāḥ tad avastha tvāt tasmāt kāraṇasya vaijātye pramāṇa siddhe kāryasya sausādṛśye api avāntara jāti bhedaḥ kalpyate hetu vaijātyasya phala vaijātyam prati prayojaka tvāt aprayojaka tve tasyāḥ ākasmika tva prasaṅgāt kāraṇa sājātye api kāryasya vaijātyam saha kāri vaijātye paryavasyati iti yuktam utpaśyāmaḥ anyathā prakṛte para lokaḥ api na siddhyet acetana upādānakam api jñānam avāntara jātīyam syāt acetanam api avāntara jātīyam jñāna upādānam bhavet dṛśya jāti abhede api kiñcid eva nimittam bhaviṣyati iti śaṅkāyāḥ samutthāpayitum śakya tvāt iti 
ĀTV_772.7–772.16	 astu tarhi sahakāri bhedāt niyamaḥ iti ced saḥ eva ekaḥ kartā iti gīyate atha ekaḥ eva kartā na tu tādṛś sahakāri paramparā iti kutas viśeṣāt iti ced na tad kartṛka tvam bhinna kartṛkebhyaḥ vyāvartate na tu tādṛś sahakāri tvam iti atas viśeṣāt kutaścid evam api syāt iti ced na tu saḥ eva viśeṣaḥ cintyate sa ca tad svabhāva tvam vā tad jātīya tvam vā tad sahakāri tvam vā tādṛś sahakāri tvam vā iti atas na atiricyate tatra prathamaḥ asambhavī dvitīyaḥ ati prasañjakaḥ caturthe niyāmaka abhāvaḥ tatas tṛtīyaḥ eva pariśiṣyate gati antara abhāvāt iti 
ĀTV_774.12–775.11^1	 athavā sambhavan api na ayam upādhiḥ tatra tāvat mātrasya anibandhana tvāt tathā hi sarvajñaḥ sva pratyaya aneka kartṛka tayā pratisandhattena vai ādye tad pratisandhānāt eva pratisandhātuḥ eka tvam siddham jñānāt bhedaḥ ca dhiyām asthaiḥ yasya sarvaiḥ eva pratīteḥ pratisandhātuḥ kṣaṇika tāyāḥ sarvajñenā api anākalanāt atha na pratisandhatte na tarhi kārya kāraṇa bhāva mātra nibandhanam pratisandhānam na hi asti sambhavaḥ yat anvaye api yasya ananvayaḥ tat tāvat mātra nibandhanam iti 
ĀTV_774.12–775.11^2	 pratisandhatte na tu satyam tad pratisandhānam atas na tāvat mātrāt eka kartṛka tva siddhiḥ iti ced tat kim sarvajñasya api viparyayaḥ āhāryaḥ na doṣa āvahaḥ iti ced na nibandhanāḥ abhede api katham ekaḥ āhāryaḥ anyaḥ tu svarasa vāhī iti vācyam bheda darśana adarśanābhyām iti ced na pravṛtti vijñānānām bhedasya asarva jñaiḥ api darśanāt viṣayāḥ eva bhinnāḥ pratibhānti na buddhayaḥ iti ced na tāsām api bheda niścayāt viṣaya bheda aprathane api jñānāḥ abhyāsa darśanāt yadi ca bheda grahe api buddhitā mātreṇa tat agrahaḥ abheda āropaḥ upapadyate pārthiva tayā vṛkṣāt kāṣṭham kāṣṭhāt aṅgāraḥ tatas bhasma api abhedena pratisandhīyeta na ca evam 
ĀTV_779.6–780.6^1	 syāt etat ālaya bheda agrahāt pratisandhānam iti ced na sa hi aham āspadam pravṛtti santānāt anyaḥ eva vā syāt tad antar pātikāt ācitka aneka aham pratyaya rūpaḥ vā na tāvat ādyaḥ na hi aham ahamikayā mithas svatantram santānāt vayam anubhūyate sati api vā parasparam anupādāna upādeya bhāvāt na parasparam pratyākalita artha anusandhāna bandhaḥ tathā tve api vā caitra maitra ādiṣu api prasaṅgaḥ ubhayoḥ vā ubhaya upādāna tve ekam api aneka āśrayam iti kim aparāddham avayavi saṃyoga ādibhiḥ na ca ālaya vijñāna upāttam pravṛtti vijñānam na kiñcid upādattaḥ iti yuktam tathā tve nimitta tām api na yāyāt upādāna tva vyāpta tvāt nimitta tāyāḥ 
ĀTV_779.6–780.6^2	 anyathā nimittata mātram upagamya ekasya nivṛttau sarva santāna ucchedaḥ aviśeṣāt om iti bruvataḥ cara makṣaṇānām akiñcit karaṇe śakti vihateḥ asattva prasaṅgaḥ tathā ca pūrvakṣaṇānām api iti anena paryāyeṇa akiñcitkaram jagat āpādyeta iti sādhu kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ pratisandhāna nibandhanam samarthitaḥ syāt tasmāt anyat eva nimittam kiñcid upādadīta tathā ca na pratisandhānam apūrva ananta santāna pravṛttiḥ ca prasajyeta iti evam ca aśaktiḥ anupādānāt anyāt ānāt ananta tā mithas na pratisandhiḥ ca saṅkare aneka saṃśritiḥ iti saṅgrahaḥ 
ĀTV_787.12–788.2–790.5–790.10	 na api dvitīyaḥ tasya api bheda āgrahaḥ svarūpataḥ vā syāt viṣayataḥ vā ādye pūrvā aham iti pratyaya mātrāt vā pravṛtti vijñānebhyaḥ api vā na prathamaḥ aham iti ajñāsiṣam aham iti jānāmi aham iti jñāsyāmi iti traikālya ullekhasya bheda niścayam antareṇa anupapatteḥ kathañcid upapattau tad arthasya eva pratisandhiḥ ucitaḥ na pravṛtti vijñāna arthānām api na ca tebhyaḥ api bheda āgrahaḥ iti ca uktam eva na api viṣayataḥ sa hi ākāraḥ vā vastu antaram vā alīkam vā iti na ādyaḥ dūṣita tvāt na dvitīyaḥ svayam anabhyupagamāt yaḥ api abhyupagacchet saḥ api viruddha dharma adhyāsāt bhedam icchet tad nivṛttau ca tad nivṛttim na tṛtīyaḥ aham iti vikalpasya sa vastuka tāyāḥ prāk eva prasādhanāt avastuka tve api na tatra prakṛta upayogi bhedāḥ agraha sambhavaḥ sat asat āropita sattva āropitā sattva vyadhikaraṇa avyapadeśya bhedena ṣadvidhasya api bhedasyā agrahaḥ abhedāra upaupayika tayā tatra na sambhavati iti ukta tvāt iti 
ĀTV_791.1–791.14	 athavā iha anubhavaḥ kāla antara bhāvinīm smṛtim janayet tat janitaḥ vā saṃskāraḥ saḥ api atīndriyaḥ pratyakṣa siddhaḥ vā atīndriyaḥ api tāvat kāla avasthāyī santanyamānaḥ vā adhyakṣa siddhaḥ api tad uttara buddhi dhārā rūpaḥ tad anyaḥ vā tad viśeṣaḥ vā viśeṣaḥ api anubhava prabhava tva mātram vā anubhavitṛ santāna vaijātyam vā tatra na prathamaḥ anutpannān anvaya dhvastayoḥ aviśeṣāt na api dṛśyaḥ anyaḥ tasya anupalabdhi bādhita tvāt na api anubhava prabhava tva mātram viśeṣaḥ na hi karmakara kara upanītam eva bījam kṣitim āsādya aṅkuram kutute na tu pramāda patitam tathā nīla ādi anubhava prabhava santānaḥ pīta ādi anubhavena eva upanīyatām nīla ādi anubhavena eva vā iti na kaścid viśeṣaḥ evam ca ananubhūte api smaraṇa prasaṅgaḥ na ca anubhūte api iti 
ĀTV_794.5–795.3	 śāli prabhavasya bījasya śāli tva praisaṃdhānavan iyam iti ced na kṣīra jambū rasa pāyi nīla dhavala kala rava janita viparīta pārāvata vat aniyama darśanena tasya aprayojaka tvāt vaijātyantu viśeṣaḥ bhavet yathā kṣīta avasekāt amla tvam parihṛtya mādhuryam upādāya anuvartamānā āmalakī kāla antare api phale mādhuryam unmīlayati lākṣā rasa avasekāt vā dhavalimānam apahāya rakta tām anuvartamānam kārpāsa bījam kusumeṣu rakta tām na ca evam prakṛte japā kusuma ādi upadhāna sannidhāne api tad rūpa tām anādāya dhavalimanam eva saṃdadhānasya sphuṭikasya iva vijñānasya viṣaya upadhānam apagamya cit rūpa tā mātreṇa anuvṛtteḥ sarva ākāra tvam eva sarva jñānānām kintu kaścid ākāraḥ paṭuḥ anye tu apaṭavaḥ iti sva darśana śraddhau atas viruddha dharma adhyāsāt api na bhīḥ na hi saḥ eva paṭuḥ apaṭuḥ ca iti saṃbhavati na ca sva saṃvidita rūpasya apāṭava artham paśyāmaḥ 
ĀTV_797.18–798.7–801.5–801.10	 nirākāra pakṣe api yāvān arthaḥ buddheḥ viṣayaḥ tāvati sphuṭā eva sā yatra ca asphuṭāḥ na asau tasya viṣayaḥ tathā tve vā viṣaya itara vyavasthā na syāt sa aṃśe tu arthe yuktam etat iti darśitam prāk tasmāt atīndriyaḥ saṃskāraḥ pariśiṣyate sa ca na saṃtanyamānaḥ smṛti ādi prasaṅge pravṛtti saṃtāne phala anavakāśa prasaṅgāt anyatra saṃskāre anyatra phale ati prasaṅgāt paramparayauka upādāna tayā niyame saṃskāra antara santāne api smṛti prasaṅgāt tasmāt sva upādānaḥ eva smṛtim karoti iti gati antara abhāvāt āpāta tiktam api upeyam eva tathā ca smṛteḥ kāla antara sambandhāt saṃskāra tad upādānayoḥ sthairyyam ayatna siddham avarjjanīyan ca iti etena dharma adharma rūpaḥ saṃskāraḥ vyākhyātaḥ tathā ca yaḥ yaḥ saṃskāraḥ kvacid santānaḥ āhitaḥ sa tatra eva phala ādhāna yogyaḥ na anyatra iti ādi api nirastam atirikta saṃskāra pakṣe hetoḥ vyadhikaraṇa tvāt viśeṣa lakṣaṇasya ca svarūpa asiddha tvāt aviśiṣṭa uttara kārya pravāha mātrasya ca viruddha tvāt iti 
ĀTV_804.11–805.3	 na ca atīndriyaḥ api saṃskāraḥ saugatanaye saṃbhavati tasya jñāna tve parokṣa tva anupapatteḥ ajñāna tve jñāna upādānaka tva ayogāt santāna antara tve jñānasya api pārokṣye tad antaḥpātinaḥ smṛti mukha ādeḥ api tathā bhāva prasaṅgāt iti tat idam ukta rūpam pratisandhānam nimitta tayā vyāptam animittaka tve niyama anupapatteḥ tat ca aneka kartṛka tve na asti iti vyāpaka anupalabdhyā vipakṣāt nivartamānam nimittavatī eka kartṛka tve viśrāmyati iti pratibandha siddhiḥ evam ca sati anvayaḥ api na tarkī bhrū latā ākṣepa ādau draṣṭavyaḥ sā eva hi bhrū latā te eva vā paramāṇavaḥ pratisaṃdhīyamānāḥ na ajñāna nimitta tve avasthitāḥ viruddha dharma virahi viṣaya tvena tu viśeṣaṇīyam atra pratisandhānam anyathā yaḥ eva bālaḥ tvayā dṛṣṭaḥ saḥ eva yuvā mayā dṛśyate iti anenāḥ anaikāntāt 
ĀTV_808.12–809.11^1	 na ca asiddham idam viśeṣaṇam dehasya eva cetana tvāt mā evam deha tva mūrta tva bhūta tva rūpa ādi mattva ādibhyaḥ na ca bhūtānām samudāye paryavasite caitanyam pratidinam tasya anya tve pūrva pūrva divasa anubhūtasya asmaraṇa prasaṅgāt na api pratyeka paryavasitam kara caraṇa ādi avayava viśleṣe tad anubhūtasya smaraṇa ayogāt dehasya cetanatve bālasya prathamam apravṛtti prasaṅgāt ca icchāt veṣau antareṇa prayatna anupapatteḥ iṣṭa abhyupāya tā pratisandhānam vinā ca icchā anupapatteḥ 
ĀTV_808.12–809.11^2	 iha janmani ananubhūtasya pratibandhasya asmṛttau pratisandhānā yogāt janma antara anubhūte ca anubhavitari bhasmasāt bhūte anyena smaraṇa ayogāt anubhava ādīnām ca pravṛtti antānām kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya iha eva janmani niścita tvāt tathā ca tad abhāve tad abhāvasya sulabha tvāt anyathā tu atiprasaṅgāt atas eva na indriyāṇi cetayante darśana sparśanābhyām eka artha grahaṇāt ca na ca manaḥ tathā tasya karaṇa tvena eva anumānāt iti pratibandha siddhiḥ para lokya ātma siddhiḥ ca anādiḥ ca asau vīta rāga janma adarśanāt anantaḥ ca sataḥ anādi tvāt dravyam ca samavāyi kāraṇa tvāt vibhuḥ ca nitya dravya tve sati amūrta tvāt amūrtaḥ ca niṣkriya tvāt niṣkriyaḥ ca nitya tve sati asmad ādi pratyakṣa tvāt pratyakṣa dharma āśraya tvāt ca iti 
ĀTV_811.18–812.11	 tarkāḥ ca atra bhavanti ādimattve prathama pravṛtti anupapattau sarvathā eva apravṛtti prasaṅgaḥ sānta tve anādeḥ sattva anupapatti prasaṅgaḥ adravya tve nirguṇa tva prasaṅgaḥ avibhu tve dahana pavana ādeḥ kriyā anupapatti prasaṅgaḥ na ca saṃyukta saṃyogāt tad utpattiḥ sākṣāt kriyāvat dvārakasya tasya abhāvāt atathābhūtasya ca tad hetu tve ati prasaṅgāt mūrttta tve nityasya asmad ādi pratyakṣa dharmān ādhāra tva prasaṅgaḥ viśeṣa guṇavatām ārambhaka tva prasaṅgaḥ ca sa kriyatve mūrta tva prasaṅgaḥ iti śāstra artha saṃgrahaḥ aṇuḥ eva asau vijñāna asamavāyi kāraṇa saṃyoga ādhāra tvāt manaḥ vat aṇīyāṃsa m aṇoḥ api iti bādha pratirodhau iti kaścid tat ayuktam ātman avibhau manasaḥ aṇu tva asiddheḥ tat saṃyoga kramāt eva kriyā krama upapatteḥ āgamaḥ tu mahataḥ api mahīyāṃsam iti prathama pādam apahāya upanyaḥ tas tad alam anena 
ĀTV_814.7–815.8^1	 syāt etat siddhaḥ api ayam īdṛśaḥ heyaḥ eva ātma darśī hi tad upakāriṇi rajyate tad apakāriṇam ca dveṣṭi rāga dveṣau ca mūlam saṃsārasya yaḥ tu na tam paśyet na asau tad upakāra apakāriṇam api tatas na rajyeta na dviṣyāt na saṃsaret iti jāṅgalikena viṣa vidyāvatā nairviṣya vat mumukṣuṇā api nairāmtyam eva bhāvanīyam iti ced na anātma darśinaḥ mumukṣu tva vyāghātāt na hi ātmānam apratisandhāya kaścid duḥkham hātum icchet sukham vā avāptum mayā svarga apagarphala bhāginā bhavitavyam iti abhiprāyasya yāvat abhiyogam anuvṛtteḥ ananuvṛttau abhiyoga nivṛttau phala asiddheḥ 
ĀTV_814.7–815.8^2	 iyam ca nairāmya dṛṣṭiḥ nāstikyam draḍhayet tat ca prabala viṣaya tṛṣṇā niṣṇātam anartham anantam prasuvīta na ced evam kutas yāvat jīvet sukham jīvet iti ādayaḥ api niḥśaṅkam ullāpāḥ yat uktam upakāriṇi rajyeta apakāriṇam dviṣyāt iti tat evam etat iti yaḥ hi mokṣam upakāram manute sa tad hetau raktaḥ tam upādadānaḥ tat panthinam dveṣāt alaṃpratyayāt vā pariharan eva samīhitam samāsādayet na tu viparyayāt yaḥ tu bhogam saḥ api tathā iti anukūlam eva pratikūla tvena gṛhītam mandaiḥ anyatra anurajyeta anyatra api dviṣyāt iti tu na dṛṣṭam go vaidyake api iti 
ĀTV_817.3–817.15	 tathā api duḥkha hetu tvāt indriya ādi vat asau hīyatām iti ced yādṛśaḥ duḥkha hetuḥ tādṛśaḥ heyaḥ eva sa upādhiḥ ca tathā nirupādhiḥ api hīyatām iti ced na aśakya tvāt niṣprayojana tvāt ca na hi tasya hānam vināśaḥ nitya tvāt na api viprayogaḥ vyāpaka tvāt na api apratipattiḥ yathā yathā tad artham yatnaḥ tathā tathā pratipatteḥ upekṣātaḥ iti ced kṛtā eva etāvantam kālam upekṣā tathā api tad dhānā siddheḥ niṣprayojanam ca etat sa upādheḥ hi tyāgaḥ duḥkha hānāya nirupādheḥ tu kim artham punar sa upādhi tva śaṅkayā iti ced na bīja abhāvāt iti kutas punar upādeyaḥ tathā sati bhāvanā krameṇa niḥśreyasa siddheḥ kim asya upādānam vivekaḥ kutas anātmanaḥ śarīra ādeḥ 
ĀTV_819.7–819.18	 kim punar atra pramāṇam nyāyaḥ āmnāyaḥ ca śarīram eva hi tāvat mūrdhābhiṣiktam anātmānam ātmānam manyamānasya tad upādāya tad anukūla trailokya viṣayā tṛṣṇā vijṛmbhate tathā tad pratikūla viṣayaḥ dveṣaḥ na ca etat kevala ātma darśinaḥ sambhavati nirupādheḥ putra vitta lobha abhāvāt taiḥ anupakāryya tvāt cheda kleda dāha śoṣa ādi anupapatteḥ vidhi niṣedha anadhikārāt ca janam jāti vayaḥ vitta saṃskāra ādi upagraheṇa tad pravṛtteḥ tatas anātmani ātma grahaḥ nidānam saṃsārasya mithyājñānam ca tattva jñānāt nivartate tat ca śravaṇa mananā ādi krameṇa utpadyate kāraṇa nivṛttau ca kāryam na jāyate utpannaḥ ca dharma adharma pracayaḥ bhogena kṣīyate iti nyāya artha sāra saṅkṣepaḥ 
ĀTV_823.14–824.4	 āmnāya sāra saṅkṣepaḥ tu aśarīram vāvasantam ityādi tad prāmāṇyam prapañca mithyātva siddhānta bheda tattva upadeśa paunaḥ punyeṣu anṛta vyāghāta punar ukta doṣebhyaḥ iti ced na satātparyatvāt niṣprapañcaḥ ātmā jñeyaḥ mumukṣubhiḥ iti hi tātparyam prapañca mithyātva śrutīnām ātmanaḥ ekasya jñānam apavarga sādhanam iti advaita śrutīnām durūhaḥ ayam iti paunaḥpunya śrutīnām bahis saṃkalpa tyāgaḥ nirmanaskaśrutīnām ātmā eva upādeyaḥ iti ānanda śrutīnām gāruḍa vat anuṣṭhāne tātparyam prakṛti ādi śrutīnām tad mūlānām sa aṅkhya ādi darśanānām ca iti na iyam anyathā jaiminiḥ yadi veda jñaḥ kapilaḥ na iti kā pramā tau= ubhau yadi veda jñau vyākhyā bhedaḥ tu kim kṛtaḥ iti 
ĀTV_825.8–825.10–831.7–831.17	 prāmāṇyam tu tasya kutas iti ced āpta ukta tvāt tat asiddham iti ced na viśvasya kartuḥ anumāna siddha tvāt vivāda adhyāsita kartṛkam sa kartṛkam kāryatvāt iti viśeṣa viruddhaḥ ayam hetuḥ iti ced na virodhi viśeṣa apratītau virodhasya pratyetum aśakya tvāt tad pratītau vā saha upalambha niyamena virodhasya bādhita tvāt sarvathā eva apratītasya abhiprāya gocara tvam api katham iti ced na sva artha anumāna siddha tvāt tatas api katham sidhyatu iti ced apratīta pratyāyakam pramāṇam na tu apratītena virodhaḥ śakya niścayaḥ iti atas viśeṣāt kā punar anumānasya evambhūta pratyāyane śaktiḥ asti iti ced ākāṅkṣa anupapatti niyama bhedena trividhaḥ sambandhaḥ tatra ākāṅkṣā niyamābhyām anvayī anupapatti niyamābhyām vyatirekī iti vibhāgaḥ 
ĀTV_834.18–835.2	 astu tarhi sat pratipakṣa tvam śarīra ajanya tvāt iti ced na asamartha viśeṣaṇa tvena asiddha bhedasya atulya bala tvāt asiddhi parihāre viśeṣaṇam samartham iti ced na ekām asiddham pariharataḥ dvitīya āpatteḥ anyathā vivāda adhyāsitam na adṛṣṭa hetukam śarīra ajanya tvāt iti anena api janya tvasya sat pratipakṣa prasaṅgāt iti
