ĀTV_836.13–837.11^1	 tarhi tarkkā pariśuddhiḥ astu dūṣaṇam śarīra nivṛttau buddhi nivṛtteḥ buddhi nitya tve śarīra anupayoga vat prayatna nityatāyām jñāna icchā anupayogāt iti ced na prayatnasya dvi dharmaka tvāt sa hi jñāna kāryaḥ jñāna eka viṣayaḥ ca kartṛ tvam tatra kāryatva nivṛttau kāraṇa tayā jñānam mā pekṣiṣṭaḥ viṣaya artham tu tad apekṣā kena vāryate na ca asya sva rūpeṇa eva viṣaya pravaṇa tvam jñāna tva prasaṅgāt ayam eva hi jñānāt prayatnasya bhedaḥ yat ayam arthāpravaṇaḥ iti na ca nirviṣayaḥ eva astu iti vācyam akāraṇa tva prasaṅgāt 
ĀTV_836.13–837.11^2	 tathā ca saḥ api ekaḥ katham siddhyet mā sautsīt iti ced na tatra sādhanasya nidoṣa tvāt doṣe vā saḥ eva bādhaḥ sarva viṣaya tvāt tasya kim viṣaya niyama arthena jñānena iti ced na tasya sva rūpeṇa artha pravaṇa tva abhāvāt bhāve vā jñāna tva prasaṅgāt iti uktam jīvana yoni prayatna vat viṣaya vyavasthā bhaviṣyati iti ced na jāti antara tvāt eka jātīya tve tasya api icchā pūrvakatva prasaṅgāt icchāyāḥ vā tad kāraṇa tvam na syāt tām antareṇa api tad jātīyasya utpatteḥ tasmāt kṛti jātīyasya jñāna icchābhyām eva sa viṣaya vyavasthā sa ca sādhayitum iṣṭaḥ iti 
ĀTV_839.5–840.10^1	 tārkika garva vāhaḥ tu āha nanu sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ darśanāt adarśana mātrasya śataśas pravṛttau api vyabhicāra upalambhāt tad lakṣaṇasya anupalabdha vyabhicārasya api tathā abhāva saṃbhāvanā krāṃta tvāt lakṣaṇa antaram pratibaṃdhasya vaktuḥ vā vipakṣe bādhakam vā iti saṃkṣepaḥ tatra na prathamaḥ adṛśya upādhyabhāva niścaya upāya abhāvāt dṛśyena eva upādhinā bhavitavyam iti ca niyama anupapatteḥ na api dvitīyaḥ sā hi anvaya vyatirekābhyām niścīyate tau ca dṛśya śarīra vat cetana niṣthau vā syātām upādhividhuḥ adṛśya adṛśya sādhāraṇa cetana mātra niṣṭhau vā na prathamaḥ viṭapa ādau vyabhicārāt prakṛta asiddheḥ ca na dvitīyaḥ ghaṭa ādi kārya vyatireka samaye tad prayojaka kulāla vyatireka vat dṛśya cetana mātra vyatirekasya niścetum aśakya tvāt 
ĀTV_839.5–840.10^2	 na hi kulāla ādi dṛśya vyatirekasya avaśyam vyatirekaḥ viṭapa ādau api tathā abhāva prasaṃgāt tarhi santāna antara anumānam api katham kambhakāra vyatireke dṛśya adṛśya cit mātra vyatirekām iddhi vat sva citta vyatireke api kampam prati cit mātra vyatireka asiddheḥ iti ced na vāda antara tvāt yadā api tat prastāvaḥ tadā api sva dehe sva para santāna sādhāraṇa cit mātrā vinirbhāga vṛtti dṛśya deha mātrasya eva pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām kampam prati kāraṇa tva pratīteḥ para cittasya api kāraṇa tvam pratīyate iti na api tṛtīyaḥ vipakṣe bādhaka abhāvāt deśa kāla niyama ādīnām sva kāraṇa āyāta sannidhinā kādācid kena pratiniyata śaktinā kāraṇena acetanena api upapatteḥ iti 
ĀTV_842.11–843.6	 uttāna ullapitam etat vikalpa trayasya api upapatteḥ tathā hi catvāraḥ jagati bhāvāḥ bhavanti virodhī bahis vṛttiḥ saha vṛttiḥ antar vṛtttiḥ ca iti na ca paṃcamaḥ prakāraḥ kāṅkṣitum api śakyate virodha avirodhayoḥ sa ahityāsā hityayoḥ ādhikya ana ādhikyayoḥ paraspara niṣedha rūpa tvāt tatra dvayam atra na upādhi tvena śaṅkanīyam kāryasya iva akāryasya api vā sa kartṛka tva prasaṅgāt na ca idam iṣṭam akāryasya kāraṇavat tā mātreṇa sahaja virodhe kāraka viśeṣasya kartuḥ anavakāśāt na api tṛtīyaḥ tulya yogakṣemayoḥ aviśeṣāt vyabhicāra śaṅkā na āpādaka tvāt ca caturthaḥ tu syāt saḥ api na śarīra antarbhūta vṛttiḥ ceṣṭamāna śarīra hetukasya api kasyacid acetana pūrvakatva prasaṅgāt na ca idam iṣṭam ceṣṭā cetanayoḥ avinā abha ava bhaṃga prasaṃgāt na api saha vṛttiḥ dehanyān upādhi tve tasya api anupādhi tvāt tayoḥ tulya yogakṣema tvāt atatha abhāve vā saha vṛtti niyama anupapatteḥ 
ĀTV_845.10–846.12^1	 śarīrasya ca na upādhi tvam kartṛ avyāpaka tvāt tad kāryatvasya upādheḥ vidyamāna tvāt na api āyatana tayā tathā bhāva ubhoga upādhi tvāt na api upakaraṇa prāpaka tayā sākṣāt prayatna an adhiṣṭheyatā upādhi tvāt anyathā api tad prāpteḥ iti na api adhika vṛttiḥ śarīra vinākṛtasya kartuḥ svayam anabhyupagamāt astu pākṣikaḥ abhyupagamaḥ tena na kāryatva mātrāt kartṛmatva siddhiḥ śaṃkita upādhi tvāt na ca upādheḥ eva tad siddhiḥ tasya svayam saṃdigdha asiddha tvāt iti ced na ubhayathā api aśarīri kartṛ vyavasthiti niyamāt kim tu kathaṃcid upādhim ādāya sa vyavatiṣṭhatām yat vā kāryatvam eva iti sandehaḥ pariśiṣyate gati antara abhāvāt iti saḥ api nivāryate 
ĀTV_845.10–846.12^2	 na tāvat deha vyatireke anitya jñāna sambhavaḥ tayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva niyamāt tatas nityam bhavet tatas sarva viṣayam ca niyata viṣaya tāyāḥ anitya tvena vyāpanāt viṣaya niyamasya sāmagrī śakti samavadhāna adhīna tayā nityāt tasyāḥ sa vyāpyam upādāya nivartamānāyāḥ anitye viśrāmāt sarva gocare ca jñāne cikīrṣā prayatnayoḥ api tathā abhāvaḥ tat eka viṣaya tvāt tayoḥ tathā ca kaṃcid upādhim ādāya aśarīra pūrvakam api kiṃcid eva kāryam kartṛ pūrvakam bhaviṣyatīit śaṃkāpiśācyā kva avakāśaḥ evam anyatra api anayā diśā upādhiśaṃkā nirākaraṇīya iti nirupādhi sambandha siddhiḥ vipakṣa sambhave ca sādhana prayukta sādhya sadbhāva siddhau sādhya abhāva prayukta sādhana abhāva lakṣaṇasya vyatirekasya api siddheḥ na tad artham pṛthak apekṣā iti 
ĀTV_849.3–851.4^1	 dvitīye api śravaṇa sampuṭam avadhāya kalakalaḥ tyajyatām tathā hi daṇḍa ādiṣu udāsīneṣu dṛśyaḥ adṛśyaḥ vā nānā kāraka vyāpārā vinirbhāga vṛttiḥ cetanaḥ nivṛttaḥ na vā iti tvam eva praṣṭavyaḥ na ced kutas kāraṇāni udāsate nivṛttaḥ ced katham adṛśya vyatireka saṃśayaḥ tathā api yādṛśasya anvayaḥ tādṛśasya vyatirekaḥ api upayujyata iti ced kaḥ atra vipratipadyate kāraka prayoktar ubhayatra api tulya tvāt dehī tādṛśaḥ iti ced kaḥ asya arthaḥ kim deha dvārā eva sarvāṇi kārakāṇi prayuṅkte cetanaḥ āho deham prayuñjānaḥ eva iti 
ĀTV_849.3–851.4^2	 na pūrvaḥ dehasya api kāraka tayā deha antara prayojya tāyām anavasthānāt na dvitīyaḥ viṣa śakala cālana ādau vyabhicārāt deham dhārayan iti ced saḥ ayam dehaḥ dhāryaḥ kim kāraka tayā tad kāraka antara prayoga artham atha sva karma upāttatā mātreṇa prathame na virodhaḥ dehasya kvacid kārya kāraka tayā adhiṣṭhāna niyamāt yarta tu na tat kārakam tatra api tat adhiṣṭheyam iti kaḥ cetanaḥ abhidadhyāt dvitīye api yaḥ sākṣāt adhiṣṭhātum aśaktaḥ sa sākṣāt adhiṣṭheyam upādāya tat prayuñjīta na tu ekasya sākṣāt adhiṣṭhāna ayogyam anyasya api tathā iti niyamaḥ 
ĀTV_849.3–851.4^3	 dehaḥ eva vyabhicārāt tṛtīye tu ajāgala stana kalpaḥ kāyaḥ na upayukta aṃśa vivecane svam niveśayati yathā dhūma mātram prati tārṇa dahana anvaya vyatirekayoḥ āloka vat tā iti yadi ca ākārakasya api atad prayoga dvāra jakasya api avaśyam apekṣā syāt yaḥ eva kulālakāyavān ghaṭasya karttā saḥ eva karabha śarīravān api daṇḍa ādīn prayuñjīta na khalu sva karma upāttatā mātreṇa karabha kumbha kāra śarīrayoḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ kārya viśeṣe kāya viśeṣaḥ anupayogi apekṣaṇīyaḥ ca iti vyāghātaḥ avyāghāte vā kumbhe karvavye karabha śarīram api avaśyam apekṣaṇīyam aviśeṣāt iti 
ĀTV_849.3–851.4^4	 tasmāt sandaṃśa vat ayaḥ piṇḍa vat kāraka tad prayojaka tayā eva śarīra adhiṣṭhāna niyamaḥ na tu śarīra tvena eva na ca śarīrasya sarvatra kārye kāraka tvam tad prayojaka tvam vā iti evam tarhi na pratiniyata deha adhiṣṭhātṛ siddhiḥ aṅkura ādi kāraka adhiṣṭhātrā api tad siddheḥ iti ced na vāda antara tvāt yadā api tad prastāvaḥ tadā api na kārya mātreṇa kāraka adhiṣṭhāna mātreṇa vā tad anumānam tatas kartṛ mātra siddheḥ kim tu harṣa bhaya śoka smita ādi liṅgaiḥ tān unniīya taiḥ bhoktuḥ anumānam iti na kiṃcid etat 
ĀTV_854.1–855.2^1	 tṛtīye api īrṣyā kaṣāye cakṣuṣī nimīlya nyāya anusāraḥ śrūyatām iha jagati na asati eva tat kāryam nāma yad kāraka cakram avadhīrya ātmānam āsādayet iti avivādam tat ca sarvam cetanā upahitam aryādam anyathā tad lakṣaṇa vyavasthā anupapatteḥ tathā hi ādheya kāraka upahitam aryādam adhikaraṇasya rūpam ādhāra tvāt apaneya apa gantṛ kāraka upahitam ca svarūpam apādānasya tad avadhi tvāt tad abhipreya tvāt karaṇa upahitam ca rūpam karmaṇaḥ tad vyāpya tvāt kartṛ u pahitam ca rūpam karaṇasya sākṣāt tad vyāpāra viṣaya tvāt samasta kāraka upahitam ca rūpam kartuḥ tad prayojaka tvāt jñāna cikīrṣā prayatna ādhāra tva vyavasthiteḥ ca na cakra ka itaretara āśraya doṣaḥ 
ĀTV_854.1–855.2^2	 evam sati kartṛ vyāvṛtteḥ tad upahita sīma samasta kāraka vyāvṛttau akāraka kārya utpatti prasaṅgaḥ iti sthūlaḥ pramādaḥ bhavet evam yadi kartrā kāraka mātrasya vyāptiḥ syāt sā eva tu kutas iti ced kutas punar avyāptiḥ na hi ṣaḍbhyaḥ anyat kartṛ anupahitam kārakam asti na ca eṣām eva kartṛ upadhāna śūnyam lakṣaṇam asti ekaikam apohya śeṣatas kārya sambhāvanāyām sarva apoha sambhāvanā prasaṅgāt na ca samasta viśeṣa apohe sāmānya sthitiḥ yatas ṣaṣ kāraka vyāvṛttau api kāraka mātrataḥ kārya pratyāśā syāt eka pravṛttau tu sarva pravṛttiḥ apratyūha iti śṛṅkhalā bandhena vyavasthiteḥ 
ĀTV_858.1–858.20	 atha matam tava eva iyam prakriyā asmākam tu kāryeṇa anuvihita bhāva abhāvam cetanam acetanam vā kāraṇam ucyate saṃhatau tu sarvam sva pradhānam upādāna itara vyavasthā tu kathañcid iti ced na tathā api nirupādāna tva prasaṅgāt jāti pratiniyata hetu tvena tat avaśyam abhyupeyam tasya pramāṇa siddha tayā apahnotum aśakya tvāt iti ced na upādāna mātrasya tad hetu tve nimitta vaicitryepi eka jātīya tva prasaṅgāt nirnimittam vā prasajyeta upādānāt eva tathāvidhāt tad upapatteḥ na kiñcid ekam ekasmāt sāmgryāḥ sarva sambhavaḥ iti ced na dṛśya mātra viṣaya tvāt tayoḥ dṛśta tvam tasya kathañcid avivakṣitam iti ced na cetane api tathā kim na syāt iti tasmāt upādāna nimittayoḥ yathā paraspara sahitayoḥ eva kārya śakti s tathā cetanā cetanayoḥ api iti eka nivṛttau itara nivṛtti prasaṅgaḥ api ca mṛd piṇḍa daṇḍa ādiṣu sva vyāpāre pāratantryam tāvat niyamena uplabhyate tat idam daṇḍa ādi tva mātra anubaddham vā syāt adṛṣṭa viśeṣa upagraha anubaddham vā acaitanya mātra anubandham vā iti nipuṇam nirūpaya 
ĀTV_860.13–861.10^1	 tatra na prathamaḥ vema ādīnām svātantrya prasaṅgāt teṣām vema ādi tva mātra anubaddham iti ced na daṇḍa ādīnām svātantrya prasaṅgāt na ca etad kārya viśeṣa niyatam gavā abhyājana ādau daṇḍa ādīnām svātantrya prasaṅgāt na dvitīyaḥ tasya jāti viśeṣa aniyata tve ghaṭa artham api teṣām kadācid svātantrya prasaṅgāt tat niyata tve saḥ eva ucyatām na ca ghaṭa paṭa śakaṭa kaṭāha ādi gatam daṇḍavema vāsī sandaṃśa ādi gatam vā sāmānya viśeṣam upalabhāmahe asti asau yatas śarīri kartṛkatva anumānam iti ced na ghaṭa tva ādeḥ eva tathā abhāvāt 
ĀTV_860.13–861.10^2	 astu vā saṃsthāna viśeṣaḥ na ca saḥ eva atra nibandhanam tasya abhāve api jala anala ādīnām cetana prerya tu a darśanāt na ca śarīra prayojyam yat tat eva cetana preryam iti niyamaḥ śarīrasya eva svātantrya prasaṅgāt iti ukta prāyam tasmāt acaitanya mātra nibandhanam etat daṇḍa ādiṣu tathā ca paramāṇu adṛṣṭa ādiṣu api tasya bhāvāt tathā abhāvaḥ durvāraḥ tat etat kāryam kāraṇa vat tayā vyāptam sā ca vipakṣe asaṃbhavantī sva vyāpyam upādāya vyāvartamānā sa pakṣe viśrāmyati iti ubhaya mukhī pratibandha siddhiḥ 
ĀTV_863.10–864.2	 kaḥ punar ayam pratibandhaḥ svābhāvikaḥ saṃbandhaḥ kaḥ svābhāvika arthaḥ nirupādhi tvam kaḥ punar upādhiḥ sādhya prayojakam nimitta antaram kim asya lakṣaṇam sādhana avyāpaka tve sati sādhya vyāpaka tvam katham punar evam lakṣaṇakaḥ arthaḥ pratyetavyaḥ nirākartavyaḥ vā viparyaya avirodha bādhakābhyām kim bādhakam anvaya vyatireka bhūyas darśana sāhāyakam ācaran anuttaraḥ tarkaḥ sa ca ātmā āśraya ita retara āśraya cakrakānavasthā aniṣṭa prasaṅga bhedena pañcavidhaḥ api kvacid vyabhicāram nirākurvāṇaḥ kvacid tad nibandhanam upādhim avadhūn van sahāyībhavati iti phalataḥ na kaścid viśeṣaḥ tad udāharaṇāni ca atra eva yathāyatham pariceyāni iti 
ĀTV_866.11–867.12^1	 atha nyāya durbalasya pratibandīkaraṇam yat uta evam śaśa viṣāṇasya api siddhiḥ syāt dṛśya mātra niyata tvāt pratyakṣa bādhasya na ca dṛśya tva nivṛtteḥ eva viṣāṇa tva nivṛttiḥ avyāpaka nivṛttau avyāpya nivṛtteḥ ayogāt viṣāṇa gata kārya tva prayukta tvāt ca dṛśya tva vyāpteḥ tena tad nivṛttau api na akāryasya śṛṅgasya nivṛttiḥ iti tat ca mahārtha sidhyā kṛtakṛtyasya na paribhraṃśāya niṣprayojana viṣaya tvāt tathā api sambhāvitasya akīrtibhiyā na upekṣām arhati pratibandhiḥ iti ced tarhi mā bhaiṣīḥ iyam unmocyate tathā hi arthataḥ sva śiraḥ śṛṅga sādhana pravṛttaḥ idam praṣṭavyaḥ kim te viṣāṇa śabdena anyat eva kiñcid abhipretam roma ādi viṣāṇa jātīyam vā dravyam 
ĀTV_866.11–867.12^2	 prathame siddha sādhanam loka virodhaḥ ca loke tad viparītasya eva arthasya viṣāṇa śabdena abhidhānāt dvitīye tu anvaya vyatirekābhyām saṃsthāna viśeṣa kārya tvāt vyavahāra lakṣaṇāya as tad abhivyakteḥ katham tat rahiteṣu paramāṇu ādiṣu tad sambhavaḥ sambhave vā katham na tatra ghaṭa tva ādikam api om iti bruvataḥ katham na jāti saṅkara prasaṅgaḥ kāraṇam vinā kārya sambhava prasaṅgaḥ vā na vā anvaya vyatirekau kārya kāraṇa bhāve pramāṇam iti sarvam samākulam eva ākula mateḥ tasmāt atīndriyam nityam vā viṣāṇam eva na bhavati yat ca viṣāṇam tat pratyakṣa bādhitam eva kutas tad anumāna avakāśaḥ 
ĀTV_869.6–869.17	 evam tarhi nityam jñānam iti api vyāhatam indriya ādi vikāra mātra vyakti mātra vyaṅgya tvāt jñāna tva sāmānyasya iti ced na atadbhāva tvāt atadākṣepaka tvāt ca na hi mātṛ tvasya vandhyā tva vat nitya tvasya abhāvaḥ jñāna tvam acetanānām api cetanatva prasaṅgāt na api nitya tvam jñāna tva abhāvam ākṣipet jñāna tvena avirodhāt virodha mūlasya vipakṣe bādhakasya abhāvāt darśana ādarśayoḥ ca artha pravaṇa tva apravaṇa tva upādhi grasta tvāt na ca indriya ādi vikāraḥ jñāna tva abhivyakti hetuḥ artha pravaṇa vyakti mātrasya eva tad nirapekṣasya tathā abhāvāt etat anapekṣasya tasya ati prasañjaka tvāt iti 
ĀTV_872.6–872.12	 atha kṣudra upadravāḥ kevalasya kartṛ tve viśvasya vaiśvarūppa vyāghātaḥ satata utpatti prasaṅgaḥ ca adṛṣṭa apekṣāyām kalpanā gauravam tatas eva tad utpatteḥ sva artham pravṛttau anīśvara tva prasaṅgaḥ para artham pravṛttau aduḥkha maya sarga prasaṅgaḥ evam eva pravṛttau acaitanyam eka tve pramāṇa abhāvaḥ aneka tve tu asārvajñyam pratiniyata sāmagrī vijña tvāt iti evam ādayaḥ 
ĀTV_873.9–873.20	 tatra kāraṇa cakrasya ekam upādāya śeṣa vaiyyarthya prasañjane sarva vaiyarthya prasaṅgaḥ anvaya vyatirekābhyām siddha kāraṇa bhāvasya na vaiyarthyam iti ced anumita kāraṇa bhāvasya api evam pramāṇa siddha tva aviśeṣāt yat ca yat anuguṇa tvena kalpitam tasya tena eva viphalīkaraṇe sarvatra adṛṣṭam upādāya dṛṣṭa vaiphalya prasaṅgaḥ tathā ca tat api na syāt pramāṇa abhāvāt dṛṣṭena hi adṛṣṭam unnīyate para artham ca pravṛttiḥ sva artha abhāvāt na ca duḥkha sṛṣṭyā kāruṇya apavādaḥ janaka adhyāpaka cikitsā ādiṣu vyabhicārāt atha daurjanyāt eva kid na evam iti ced na doṣa abhāvāt tad abhāvaḥ ca moha abhāvāt tad abhāvaḥ api sarvajña tvāt iti 
ĀTV_875.18–876.12	 ekadvaṇuka kārī ca paramāṇumat dṛṣṭam upakārya tri aṇuka ādi bhoga paryantam dravya ādi padārtha ṣaṭkam ca jānāti nānam iti avivādam eṣām upādāna ādi rūpa tvāt avacchedya avacchedaka bhāvā parijñānena vā upādāna ādi parijñāna anupapatteḥ yaḥ ca yat jātīyam ekam kartum jñātum vā samarthaḥ sa tat jātīyam sarvam eva iti niyamaḥ sāmarthyasya jāti niyata tvāt kevalam samarthaḥ api saha kārya sannidheḥ na kuryāt na jānīyāt tatra prathamam iṣyate kāryasya kāla deśa niyama upalambhāt na ca tat tathā katham iti ced śarīra apāye tad āśritānām indriya ādīnām apāyāt na ca anvaya vyatireka siddha hetu bhāvasya abhāve api hetu antarāt kārya janma nirhetuka tva prasaṅgāt na ca ahetukam kāryam nāma tatas svatas siddhā eva asya jñāna cikīrṣā prayatna śaktiḥ yat gocarā tad jātīya samasta gocara iti sārvajñya siddhiḥ 
ĀTV_878.3–879.2^1	 śarīra apāyaḥ eva katham iti ced dṛśyasya pratyakṣa bādhita tvāt adṛśyasya api sāvayava tayā mūrta tayā ca niviḍatara pāṣāṇa madhya vartini bheka ādau kārye kartavye na abhagnasya praveśaḥ na ca paramāṇu rūpam tat śarīram anantarāla tvena nirmanaskatayā indriya āśraya tva anupapatteḥ na ca bahis vṛttiḥ mataḥ jñāna janana upayogi śarīra vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt na ca daviṣṭhaḥ eva sūrya ādiḥ tat kuryāt iti sāmpratam kārakān adhiṣṭhānāt śarīrasya tad āyātana tayā prayatnasya avyāpaka tvāt tathā api vyāpaka tve tu asamavāyi kāraṇān anurodhena akāraṇaka tayā tat eva nitya tvam 
ĀTV_878.3–879.2^2	 na ca uddeśa mātra saṃbandhena kriyā hetu tvam asmad ādi prayatnasya api tathā abhāva prasaṅgāt na ca saṃyukta saṃyogāt adhiṣṭhānam sākṣāt adhiṣṭhānasya vivakṣita tvāt viṣa apanoda ādau katham iti ced na tatra asmad ādeḥ jñāna mātram pratiyatnasya avirodhāt viṣa apanoda ādau tu tad sahakāriṇaḥ tad janya adṛṣṭa sahakāriṇaḥ vā anyasya eva tatratyaḥ yatnaḥ kriyā hetuḥ iti sarga ādau tu na śarīra gandhaḥ api iti sarvathā kalevara vigamāt akāraṇa tayā buddheḥ sarvajña tvam anivāryam viśveṣām kartuḥ ekasya iti 
ĀTV_881.14–882.7	 astu tāvat asau sarvajñaḥ karttā vaktā tu katham iti ced na vacana śaktau satyām para artha eka tāna tvāt yaḥ hi hita ahita vibhāgam vidvān para artham abhiprāyaḥ saṃsthāna karaṇa pāṭave satya viduṣe avaśyam upadiśet yathā andhāya dakṣiṇena yāhi vāmena mā gāḥ iti pṛthagjanaḥ api tathā bhagavān iti sthāna karaṇa pāṭavam asiddham deha abhāvāt teṣām tālu ādi vivṛta ādi rūpa tvāt na ca tad antareṇa varṇa niṣpattiḥ tad upatteḥ avadhāraṇāt na ca tad kāraṇāni anidhi tiṣṭhataḥ tad kartṛ tvam īśvarasya api iti ced na yasya kāryasya yat kāraṇam anvaya vyatireka siddham tad kāraṇa adhiṣṭhānayoḥ sthūla siddhi artham tad avayava paramparā kāraṇa adhiṣṭhāna vat avaśyambhāva niyamāt nanu sarvatra kārye kāyaḥ kāraṇam iti prāk upekṣitaḥ pitṛ tvāt vā upadeśa anumānam tathā api katamaḥ āgamaḥ tena praṇīti iti ced veda āyurveda ādiḥ iti ari karikarṇa jvaraḥ siṃhanādaḥ 
ĀTV_883.8–883.22	 tathā hi na tāvat ayam āyurvedaḥ apramāṇam saṃvādasya prāyika tvāt visaṃvādasya kākatālīya tayā kartṛ karma sādhana vaiguṇya hetuka tvāt punar tad sādguṇye tatas eva phala siddheḥ na ca nirmūlaḥ tathā bhavitum arhati atiprasaṅgāt na ca anvaya vyatireka bhāvaḥ asya mūlam āvāpa udvāpena yogānām ananta tayā arva acīnena aśakya tvāt viṣa ādau tathā akaraṇe bahutara anartha prasaṅgāt kaḥ prekṣāvān anākalita vastu tattvaḥ pāṭava poṣaṇa= chedana kṣāraṇa śirā vedhana laṅdhana ādi yogyāyai kārayet karyāt vā na ca upadeśasya upadeśa pāramparya mātram mūlam avaśyam upadeśasya kvacid pramāṇe viśrānteḥ iti hi vyāpteḥ na ca nitya āgama sambhavaḥ vākya tvāt tasmāt atīndriya arha darśi pūrvakaḥ ayam iti pariśeṣaḥ tathā ca anena dṛṣṭāntena mahā jana parigṛhīta tvāt vedāḥ api sarvajña pūrvakāḥ iti unnīyate 
ĀTV_885.6–886.14^1	 nanu mahat śabdaḥ atra yadi prāmāṇika vacanaḥ tadā sandigdha asiddha viśeṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ atha bahu arthaḥ tadā sugata ādi āgamaiḥ arana ekāntaḥ teṣām api vā sarvajña pūrvaka tvam iti ced na bahutva atiśayasya vivakṣita tvāt kaḥ atiśayaḥ sarva darśana antaḥpāti tvam kaḥ taiḥ parigrahaḥ tad artha anuṣṭhānam svīkṛta vyavahāra vyākaraṇa ādi pālanīya tvam svīkṛta prāmāṇi āyurveda ādi svīkṛta artha tvan ca tathā hi na asti eva tad darśanam yatra sāṃvṛtam iti uktvā api garbhādhāna ādi anti eṣṭi paryantām vaidikīm kriyām janaḥ na anutiṣṭhati spṛśya aspṛśya ādi vibhāgam vā na anumanute vyatikrame ca ācamana ādi snāna ādi prāyaścittam vā na anutiṣṭhati na sarvatra sarvaḥ janaḥ evam iti ced mā bhūt na hi sarvaiḥ rogibhiḥ āyurveda arthaḥ na anuṣṭhīyate iti na tasya mahā jana parigrahaḥ api tu sarva darśana antar pātibhiḥ iti eva 
ĀTV_885.6–886.14^2	 tathā api na sarvaḥ veda arthaḥ evam iti ced mā bhūt na hi vaidyaka arthaḥ evam api tu kaścid kena api evam tarhi saugata ādi āgama arthaḥ api kaścid ahiṃsā ādiḥ sarva darśana antar pātibhiḥ anuṣṭhīyate eva kaiścid iti saḥ api mahājana parigṛhītaḥ syāt na sandehāt kim ayam ahiṃsā ādivaiḥ dikaḥ eva arthaḥ viḍālavrata nyāyena śrāddha āpādanāya śauddhodani prabhṛtibhiḥ upanibaddhaḥ āho svayam dṛṣṭaḥ eva iti na tāvat svayam dṛṣṭaḥ śramaṇaka ādi āgama sādhāraṇa tvāt yaḥ tu asādhāraṇaḥ maṇḍalīkaraṇa ādiḥ keśa ulluñcana ādiḥ vā na asau sarvaiḥ anuṣṭhīyate vaidikaḥ tu asādhāraṇaḥ eva niṣeka ādiḥ tathā iti api ca vācaka apabhraṃśa vibhāgaḥ astu na vā tat yu avahāraḥ tāvat sarvaiḥ eva tīrthikaiḥ avigānena svīkṛtaḥ tathā śikṣā jyotiḥ chandaḥ nigama nirukta ādi arthaḥ ca teṣām ca veda rakṣā eva paramam prayojanam iti 
ĀTV_890.1–890.20^1	 syāt etat vyākaraṇa ādīni tāvat sarvaiḥ abhyupagata arthāni vedāḥ api taiḥ pālanīyāḥ bhavantu te eva iti tu kutas saṃsāra mocaka āgamaḥ api tad pālanīyaḥ kid na syāt iti ced na tad kartṛbhiḥ tathā anabhyupagamāt avyutpādanāt asādhāraṇa liṅga abhāvāt viruddha liṅga sadbhāvāt ca na hi veda śabda arthau iva sugatāt yāga māsa ādhāraṇa śabda arthau anurudhya teṣām pravṛttiḥ yatas evam annīyeta pratyuta virodhaḥ eva taiḥ tad aprāmāṇya vyutpādanāt tasmāt sarva abhyupeta vyavahāra vyākaraṇa ādi pālanīya tvam api vedānām eva na anyeṣām 
ĀTV_890.1–890.20^2	 sarva abhyupeta prāmāṇyaiḥ āyurveda ādibhiḥ svīkṛtaḥ ca eṣām arthaḥ pratipadam tadīya śāntika pauṣṭika prāyaścitta tapaḥ ja padāna homa ādi upadeśāt na ca eṣa bhāgaḥ tatra apramāṇam eva tulya yogakṣema tvāt etat eva asiddham prakṣepasya api saṃbhavāt iti ced na adhyetra dhyā payitṛ saṃpradāya avicchedāt anyathā karaṇe ca asya bahubhyaḥ syāt nivāraṇam iti nyāyāt tasmāt evaṃrūpaḥ api mahā jana parigrahaḥ vedānām iti saḥ ayam īdṛśaḥ mahā jana parigrahaḥ asarvajña pūrvaka tve asaṃbhavan sarvajña pūrvaka tvena vyāpyate 
ĀTV_893.10–893.18	 yathā hi pūrva viruddha apūrva vyākaraṇa ādi vaidyaka ādiṣu vigānāt aparigrahaḥ tathā tathāvidhe dharma śāstre api vyāmohāt bhavan api kasyacid eva na tu sarveṣām atha pūrva aviruddham ced tathā api pūrvasya pūrvavat aparigrahe kenacid parigrahe vā katham tad mūlasya anyasya sarvaiḥ parigrahaḥ na ca na āsīt eva pūrvam dharma śāstram māna antarasya atra vastuni kuṇṭha tayā anuṣṭhāna abhāva prasaṅgāt tathā ca dharma abhāve tad kāryasya sukhasya api abhāve rāga anutpattau loka samīha ucchede loka uccheda prasaṅgaḥ 
ĀTV_895.1–895.8	 tasmāt mahā jana parigṛhīta pūrva pūrva āgama pūrvaka tvāt pravāha nitya tvāt vā pralaya vicchede sarga ādau sarva anuvidheya puruṣa dhaureya pūrvaka tvāt vā mahā jana parigrahaḥ na tu pūrva āgamān apekṣāḥ vācīna puruṣa paśu pūrvaka tvāt pūrva āgama prāmāṇya aprāmāṇyayoḥ ubhayathā api tasya vipralambhaka tvāt prāmāṇye hi tat viruddha abhidhānam vipralambhaḥ eva aprāmāṇye api upāyam aviduṣaḥ ananuṣṭhāne tad ābhāsa anuṣṭhāne vā asarvajñasya upadeśaḥ vipralambhaḥ eva iti 
ĀTV_896.7–897.14^1	 tatra na prathamaḥ veda paramparā anupalambhāt arvācīnānām pāṭha pāratantrya mātreṇa pravāha upapattau tad kalpanāyām pramāṇa abhāvāt na api dvitīyaḥ vedahrāsa darśanāt yatas idānīm aśrūyamāṇasya api vedasya arthaḥ anuṣṭhīyate nibadhyate ca manu ādibhiḥ puruṣāṇām apacīyamāna śaktika tvāt ca yathā hi aśvam edha rāja sūya ādi anuṣṭhāna śakteḥ apacayaḥ tathā adhyayana śakteḥ api na ca pūrvam api na anuṣṭhitāḥ eva rājasūya ādayaḥ tad arthasya veda rāśeḥ vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt na ca nitya anumeya veda sambhavaḥ varṇānām nitya tve api ānupūrvyāḥ pāṭhā āśraya tvāt na ca ānupūrvī śūnya varṇāḥ padam nāma na ca akāṅkṣa ādi upeta pada kadambāt anyat vākyam nāma iti guruḥ api laghuḥ eva tasmāt puruṣāṇām anuṣṭhāna śakti vat adhyayana śaktiḥ api yuga krameṇa apacīyate tatas vedānām śākhā ucchedaḥ tad arthānām anuṣṭhāna ucchedaḥ varṇa āśrama ācāra vyavasthā viplavaḥ ca iti 
ĀTV_896.7–897.14^2	 atas eva bhagavataḥ vyāsasya puruṣa śakti apacayam avekṣya vacanāni alpa āyuṣaḥ alpa sattvāḥ ityādīni veda ucchedam avekṣya pratimanvantaran ca eṣā śrutiḥ anyā vidhīyate ityādīni anuṣṭhāna utmādam avekṣya dānam ekam kalau yuge ityādīni ācāra viplavam avekṣya prajāḥ tatra bhaviṣyanti śiśna udara parāyaṇāḥ ityādīni tathā ca śrūyamāṇāḥ api vedāḥ ucchedam upayāsyanti veda tvāt vākya tvāt vai ucchinna śākhā vat iti nyāyāt yathā ca etat tathā parvatāḥ api cūrṇībhaviṣyanti pārthiva tvāt ghaṭa vat samudrāḥ api śoṣam eṣyanti jalāśaya tvāt sthalī palvala vat sūryaḥ api nirvāsyati taijasa tvāt pradīpa vat brahmā api praiṣyati śarīra tvāt asmad ādi vat iti āgama avirodhena anumīyatām 
ĀTV_900.7–900.21	 syāt etat bhaviṣyan ucchedaḥ anumitaḥ sa tu bhūtaḥ api iti kutas iti ced yatas eva uccheda anantaram punar sargeṇa bhāvyam anyathā saṃsāriṇām kṛta hāna prasaṅgāt na hi viśva nirmāṇam antareṇa bhoga jñānayoḥ saṃbhavaḥ na hi tena vinā karma pravāha saṃrodhaḥ tatas yathā bhaviṣyan viśvasargaḥ uccheda pūrvakaḥ tathā ayam api iti samaya niyamaḥ tu prāṇinām karma vaiṣamye api varṣa ādi niyama vat udaya asta niyama vat vā draṣṭavyaḥ karmaṇām eva evam svabhāva tvāt etat artham eva hi purāṇeṣu sṛṣṭi pralayayoḥ divasa rātri vyavahāraḥ tathā api sarva prāṇi nāśa yaugapadye kim pramāṇam iti ced dvis sapta bhauma bhuvana prasāda bhaṅge api nirbhayāḥ eva grāma kuṭī haṭṭa vihāriṇaḥ śarīriṇaḥ iti mahatī prekṣā tasmāt sarga ādi mahājanam anu ādi parigraha pūrva koya madya yāvat anuvartate iti nāna vasara doṣa avakāśaḥ api iti yuktam utpaśyāmaḥ 
ĀTV_903.13–904.7	 tadā evam katham manu ādibhiḥ parigṛhyantām vedāḥ iti ced āyurveda vat āpta ukta tva niścayāt saḥ eva kutas iti ced adhyakṣataḥ teṣām api atīndriya artha darśi tvāt tādṛśām teṣām tad parigraheṇa kim prayojanam iti ced asmad vyavahāreṇa asmad apatya ādi vyutpadyatām tathā ca dharma saṃpradāyaḥ pravartatām iti bhūta dayā sva adhikāra sampādanam ca athavā sarga antara gṛhīta vyāpti prādurbhāve supta pratibuddha vat pitṛ tvena avipralambhaka tvam uccāvaca bhūta nirmāṇa darśanena sārvajñyam anumāyāḥ āpta tva niścayaḥ tasya teṣām yat vā bhagavān eva saṃpradāya pravartana vyasana vyagraḥ kāya sahastrāṇi vyutpādya vyutpādaka bhāva vyavasthitāni nirmāya tadātanam mahājanam parigrāhitavān naṭana upādhyāyaḥ iva svayam naṭitvā iti sarvam sustham pakṣa traye api atra purāṇa ādi saṃkathā api asti iti 
ĀTV_905.10–906.4	 syāt etat parameśvara pravartitaḥ ayam eva veda saṃpradāyaḥ sarga antara veda apekṣaḥ eva iti sa īśvaramī māṃsā pakṣaḥ kapila pakṣaḥ vā syāt iti ced kim artham punar iyam apekṣāḥ pūrvavede jaganna āsthasya na tāvat veda artha upalambhāya nitya sarvajña tvāt na api racanā artham sva bḥāvataḥ sarva kartṛka tayā ādarśa anapekṣaṇāt na api virodha parīhāra artham pratipādyānām tad anusandhāna vidhura tvāt avaidhurye vā kartuḥ sārvajñya vijñānāt eva samasta virodha vidhūnanāt tathā api pūrva sarga antara veda vyara hāraḥ api parameśvarasya gocaraḥ iti ced kaḥ sandehaḥ yadi ca etat eva vedasya pravāha nitya tvam na kevalam etasya kim tu ghaṭa ādeḥ api iti nyāyaḥ eva darśanam anyathā mīmāṃsā iti kva sa īśvaramīmāṃsa iti tasmāt ukta rūpaḥ parigrahaḥ na anyathā saṃbhavati iti pratibandha siddhiḥ tathā ca āpta ukta tvāt prāmāṇya siddhiḥ 
ĀTV_907.1–908.2^1	 katham punar sugata ādi āgameṣu na ādāraḥ chāndasānām veda vidveṣi darśana antar pāti puruṣa praṇīta tvāt iti mā śaṅkiṣṭhāḥ jinet rajagat indra prabhṛti praṇīteṣu api ādarāt tat kasya hetoḥ mahā jana parigṛhīta pūrva āgama aviruddha tayā tad anumāri tvāt kutas tarhi siddha prāmāṇya veda virodhāt katham tarhi katipayaiḥ api tad parigrahaḥ alasa bhīrubhiḥ duḥkha maya jāti akarma vidveṣāt uduṃbara gatīḥ yatantuvāya vat na tu evam vede karmaṇi eva nirbhara tvāt traivarṇika bahiṣkṛtaiḥ anadhikāribhiḥ ananya gatika tvāt kīrti prajñā kara vat na tu evam śrutau paraiḥ pūjyānām api atra apraveśāt itas patitānām api pariḥ upādānāt 
ĀTV_907.1–908.2^2	 bhakṣa peyāt ya t vaita rucibhiḥ ca rāgāt sarabha ādi vat na tu evam āmanāye tad vibhāga vyavasthā paratvāt kutarka abhyāsibhiḥ ca mohāt kāṇa ācārya ādi vat na tu evam brahmaṇi ābāla bhāvam pravṛtteḥ avivekibhiḥ ca pāṣaṇḍi saṃsargāt śauṇḍikā ādi vat na tu evam prakṛte pitṛ ādi krameṇa pravartanāt yoga abhyāsa abhimānibhiḥ ca avyagra tā abhisandhaḥ subhūti ādi tvat na tu evam prastute prathamasya karma kāṇḍaḥ eva niyogāt ayogyaiḥ ājīvanāt sāmānya śramaṇaka vat na tu evam prakrānte āgantukānām anadhikārāt kuhaka vañcitaiḥ samīcīna pratyayāt dīpaṅkara suṣira darśi bāliśa vat na tu evam prakṛte tad abhāvāt kin tu mahā jana parigrahāt vaktṛ prāmāṇyam anumāyaḥ āyurvede nairujya kāma vat iti 
ĀTV_909.17–910.20^1	 kim punar amīṣām mūlam na hi etāvantaḥ grantha rāśayaḥ para vipralambhana artham praṇīyante na ca viścam eva vipralabhyam iti ced bhavatu kiñcid mūlam kim anena cintitena ati nirbandhe tu kṣaṇika nairātmya ādi pratipādakānām tarka abhyāsaḥ pratipāditam ca tathā śūnyasa ākāra ādi pratipādakānām tu durabhyāsaḥ yoga śāstreṣu abhyasyataḥ svarūpa śūnyam iva bhāvyam ekam eva iti pratipādanāt caitya cīvara ādi pratipādakānām tu sva sthitim abhisandhāya darśana antara sthiti dveṣaḥ sva sthitau pramāṇam anapekṣya para sthitau vigānāt brahmacarya pratipādakānām tu vedāḥ eva nyāya aviruddham paratantra uktam api ānukūlya prasiddheḥ gṛhyate iti vimarṣāt 
ĀTV_909.17–910.20^2	 mantra koṣa pratipādakānām tu praṇava bīja jātayaḥ sarva sādhāraṇyaḥ śraddheya devatānām āṅkaḥ tu adhikaḥ śraddhā parigṛhītaḥ ca ākāraḥ devatā iti hasta samālocaḥ satya tapaḥ śālīnām vacanam mantraḥ viṣayavatyām cintāyām citta sthairyam prayojanam katham anyathā mahā ṛṣīṇām śāpa anugraha kṣamatā katham vā catur bhuja aṣṭa bhuja ādi avasthā iti durūhāt iti eka vipralambhana artham vā kenacid kiyat eva praṇītam tena anuṣṭitam aparaiḥ tad anuyāyibhiḥ gṛhītam anuṣṭitam vyākhyātam vivarddhitam ca iti kim anupapannam tasmāt viruddha āgama vyudāsena vedāḥ eva arvācīna puruṣa pūrvaka tva śaṅkā vyudāsena parameśvara praṇīta tvāt eva bhūta artha bhāgasya aprāmāṇya śaṅkā vyudāsena pramāṇam eva iti niyamaḥ 
ĀTV_913.13–913.19	 katham caramaḥ iti ced mahā jana parigrahasya tad sādhyasya vā sarvajña pūrvakatvasya puruṣa doṣa abhāvasya vā prāmāṇya hetoḥ bhūta bhāvya artha bhāgayoḥ sādhāraṇa tvāt kim tasya phalam iti ced sva artha pratipādanam kim tena prayojanam yathāyatham upādānam hānam mokṣaḥ ca tatra anartha hetūnām tattva jñānāt dhānam artha hetūnām upādānam ātmanaḥ mokṣaḥ iti 
ĀTV_915.1–916.18^1	 kaḥ punar ayam mokṣaḥ ātyantikī duḥkha nivṛttiḥ ātmanaḥ kim ātyantika tvam tad jātīya atyanta abhāva viśiṣṭa tvam teṣām abhāvaḥ katham kāraṇa mātra ucchedāt apuruṣa arthaḥ ayam iti ced na asatyasya akāmi asya aśakyasya durantasya tathā abhāvāt na tu ayam tathā satyaḥ ayam pramāṇa siddha tvāt sarvaiḥ abhyupagamāt kāmyaḥ ca duḥkhasya svabhāva heya tvāt sukha artham tat hānam iti ced na atad hetu tvāt vyāpteḥ iti ced na asiddheḥ na hi duḥkha abhāvaḥ sukhena vyāpyate iti 
ĀTV_915.1–916.18^2	 sukham tāvat tena vyāpyate iti ced tarhi sukhe sati a vaśyam duḥkha abhāvaḥ bhavet iti sukha prārthanā iti viparīta āpattiḥ na āvedya tvāt asau kāmyaḥ iti ced na duḥkha ārtānām katham anyathā deham api jahyuḥ avivekinaste iti ced kim atra vivekena iṣyamāṇa tā mātra anubandhi tvāt puruṣa artha tvasya gamya agamyayoḥ kāma vat bahutara anartha prasakti śaṅkayā śāstram anukūlayantaḥ te itarebhyaḥ bhidyante api ca evam kaṇṭaka ādi janya duḥkha nivṛttiḥ api puruṣa arthaḥ na syāt avedya tvāt prathamam vidyate tāvat asau iti ced tulyam mokṣe api 
ĀTV_915.1–916.18^3	 na adhyakṣeṇa iti ced tarhi durita kṣaya kāmasya karma anuṣṭhānānarthakya prasaṅgaḥ tad abhāva tad phala abhāvayoḥ api anadhyakṣa tvāt upalabdhi yogya tā āpanna aniṣṭa nivṛtti rūpa tvāt ayam adoṣaḥ iti ced tulyam duḥkha vat sukhasya api ucchedāt akāmyaḥ ayam iti ced na tṛṣṇāyāḥ doṣa tiraskāreṇa pravṛtti vat alampratyayena guṇa tiraskārān nivṛtteḥ api darśanāt madhu viṣa saṃpṛktam annam atra udāharaṇam santi ca kecana alampratyayavantaḥ na ca sama tvam duḥkhasya eva prācuryāt duḥkhe sukha hetu ananuṣaṅge api sukhe duḥkha hetu anuṣaṅga niyamāt tathā hi nyāya uparjiteṣu eva viṣayeṣu kiyatī sukha khadyotikā kiyanti ca arjana rakṣaṇa ādibhiḥ duḥkha durdināni anyāya upārjiteṣu yat bhaviṣyati tad manasā api cintayitum aśakyam vidāṅkurvantu ca santaḥ yadi kaṇṭaka ādi janyeṣu duḥkheṣu leśataḥ api sukha anuṣaṅgaḥ asti ca svarga ādi sukheṣu api bahulaḥ duḥkha śalya sambhedaḥ atas eva vivicya bhujyatām tuṣa taṇḍula vat iti aśakyam iti śakyaḥ ca ayam nirvartya tvāt svantaḥ ca aparāvṛtteḥ anartha vāsanā ananukūla abhisandhi tvāt ca iti 
ĀTV_921.3–922.8^1	 nityam tu sukham na satyam yogyā anupalambha bādhita tvāt śrutiḥ tatra mānam iti ced na yogyā anupalabdhi bādhite tad anavakāśāt avakāśe vā grāva plavana śruteḥ api tathā abhāva prasaṅgāt na api kāmyam sadātana tvāt na hi yat yasya asita sa tat kāmayate bhrānteḥ evam kaṇṭha stha cāmīkara vat iti ced na sva saṃvedyam nitya tvāt na api vikāryam apariṇāmi tvāt na api saṃskāryam anādheya atiśaya tvāt na prāpyam nitya saṃbandhavat tvāt na jñeyam jñānasya api nitya tvāt anitya tve vā śarīra ādi kāraṇa apāye tad anutpatteḥ utpattau vā teṣām akāraṇa tva prasaṅgāt tathā ca sarvaḥ sarva darśī syāt ātma manaḥ saṃyoga ādeḥ sarvatra aviśeṣāt 
ĀTV_921.3–922.8^2	 jñāna jñeyayoḥ nitya tve api tad saṃbandhaḥ janyate sa ca ṣaṣ padārtha vyatirekāt utpannaḥ api na nivartate dhvaṃsa vat iti ced na bhāva abhāvayoḥ prakāra antara abhāvāt tatra sa na abhāvaḥ pratiyogi anupapatteḥ bhāva tve tu avaśyam utpannaḥ nivartteta upādhi antara abhāvāt avidyā vidhvaṃsanam eva tad prāptiḥ iti ced atra na naḥ vivādaḥ na hi ekaviṃśati prabheda bhinna duḥkha vyatiriktā avidyā nāma tad vidhvaṃsanan ca puruṣa arthaḥ iti pratipādanāt iti durantam ca tat tad abhisandheḥ sukha saṃskāra sahakāri tayā tad udbhāve viśiṣṭa sukha abhilāṣiṇaḥ vaiṣayike api pravṛtti saṃbhavāt alābhe mattakāśinyā dṛṣṭā tiryakṣu kāmitā iti udāharaṇāt iti 
ĀTV_933.8–933.15	 syāt etat ātmā tu kim sva prakāśa sukha svabhāvaḥ anyathā vā iti pṛcchāmaḥ śrāddhaḥ asi ced upaniṣadaḥ pṛccha madhyasthaḥ asi ced anubhavam pṛccha naiyāyikaḥ asi ced na vaiṣayika sukha jñāna svabhāvaḥ iti niścinuyāḥ tad atirikte tu sukha jñāna vyavahāre bīja abhāvāt tad vyavahāra abhāvaḥ anugraha abhiṣvaṅga indriya prasāda ādi lakṣaṇam hi kāryam tat vyavahāra bījam artha pravaṇa tvam smṛti saṃskāra ādi kāryam jñāna vyavahāra ādi bījam loke tayoḥ ca abhāvaḥ ātmani iti 
ĀTV_935.5–936.15^1	 tasmāt śruteḥ śrutvā ātmānam tadanu samanukrānta vapuṣaḥ viniścitya nyāyāt atha vihata heya vyatikaram upāsīta śraddhā śama dama virāma eka vibhava ubhava ucchityai citta praṇidhi vihitaiḥ yoga vidhibhiḥ upāsyamāne ca tasmin prathamam bahis arthāḥ eva bhāsante yān a āśritya karma mīmāṃsa upasaṃhāraḥ cārvāka samutthānam ca tad pratipādana artham ca parāñci khāni ityādi tat hānāya param karmabhyaḥ ityādi atha artha ākāraḥ yam āśritya traidaṇḍikam atopa saṃhāraḥ yoga ācāra samutthānam ca tad pratipādana artham ātmā eva idam sarvam ityādi tad dhāna artham agandhamarasam ityādi atha artha abhāvaḥ yam āśritya vedānta dvāra mātra upasaṃhāraḥ śūnya nairātmya samutthānam ca tad pratipādana artham asat eva idam agre āsīt ityādi tad dhāna artham agandhaṃtamaḥ praviśanti ye ke ca ātma hanaḥ janāḥ ityādi 
ĀTV_935.5–936.15^2	 tatas vivekam yam āśritya sāṃkhyam atopa saṃhāraḥ śakti sattva samutthānam ca tat pratipādana artham prakṛteḥ parastāt ityādi tat hānāya na anyat sat ityādi tatas kevalaḥ ātmā prakāśate yama āśritya advaitam ata upa saṃhāraḥ tad pratipādana artham yatas vācaḥ nivartante aprāpya manasā saha iti sā ca avasthā na heyāḥ tad pratipādana artham na paśyati iti āhuḥ ekībhavati ityādi tad dhāna artham na advaitam na api dvaitam ityādi tatas samasta saṃskāra abhibhavāt kevalaḥ api na vikalpyate yam āśritya carama vedānta upasaṃhāraḥ mokṣa nagara gopurāyamāṇa tvāt nirvāṇam tu tasyāḥ svayam eva yam āśritya nyāya darśana upasaṃhāraḥ tad pratipādana artham atha yaḥ niṣkāmaḥ ātma kāmaḥ āpta kāmaḥ sa brahma eva san brahma apyeti na tasya prāṇāḥ utkrāmanti tatra eva samavalīyante ityādīni tasmāt abhyāsa kāmaḥ api apadvārāṇi vihāya dvāraiḥ eva praviśet yatas mārga vimārga saṃmoham āśaṅkamānaiḥ ucyate lakṣyeṇa dhanuṣām yogaḥ iti 
ĀTV_947.1–947.9	 bahutara paratantra prāntara dhvānta bhīta stimita pathika rakṣā sārthavāhena yatnāt tat idam udayanena nyāya loka āgamānāṃ vyatihati madhūya vyañjitam vartma mukteḥ na asya ślāghāma kalita guṇaḥ poṣayan prītaye naḥkaḥ andhaiḥ citraḥ tuti śata vidhau śilpinaḥ syāt prakarṣaḥ nindām eva prathayatu janaḥ kintu doṣān nirūpya prekṣān tathya skhalita kathanam prīṇayet eva bhūyas
